./  ADD  NAME=ENDIEIM1
/* REXX                                                              */
/*-------------------------------------------------------------------*/
/*                                                                   */
/*  COPYRIGHT (C) 1986-2010 CA. ALL RIGHTS RESERVED.                 */
/*                                                                   */
/* NAME: ENDIEIM1                                                    */
/*                                                                   */
/* PURPOSE: THIS IS A SAMPLE REXX EXEC THAT IS GIVEN CONTROL WHEN    */
/*  THE EDIT ELEMENT DIALOG USER SELECTS THE EDIT OR CREATE DIALOG   */
/*  OPTION.  THE EXEC CAN BE USED TO PERFORM ANY EDIT SESSION SET-UP */
/*  STEPS THAT THE USER MAY REQUIRE.  EXAMPLES INCLUDE SETTING THE   */
/*  CAPS ATTRIBUTE, DEFINING ADDITIONAL EDIT MACROS OR WRITING       */
/*  MESSAGES.                                                        */
/*                                                                   */
/*   NOTE: ENDIEIM1 CAN ALSO BE WRITTEN AS A CLIST.                  */
/*                                                                   */
/*-------------------------------------------------------------------*/
/*-------------------------------------------------------------------*/
trace o
opt_panel  = "COMPOPTS"                    /* options panel          */
show_all   = "N"                           /* don't show all options */
                                           /* when user requests     */
                                           /* advanced options this  */
                                           /* flag is set to Y       */
                                           /* ADVOPT is ISPF Var     */
mnote_after= "Y"                           /* put mnotes after       */
                                           /* when user requests     */
                                           /* mnotes after this      */
                                           /* flag is set to Y       */
                                           /* MNOTEAFT is ISPF Var   */
my_rc      = 0                             /* initialize rc          */
msg_cntr   = 0                             /* init msg counter       */
amsg_cntr  = 0                             /* init generic msg cntr  */
VOPT_cnt   = 0                             /* init options counter   */
caps_off   = " OPT TABLES SPPARM SPDEF RLF SQLPL FNPARM " /*caps off 4*/
num_off    = " OPT TABLES SPPARM SPDEF RLF SQLPL FNPARM "  ,
             " CTL MSG SKL PNL "                           /*num off 4*/
num_on_cob = " COB "
num_on_std = " PLI "
hilite_off = " TABLES PATTERNS "           /* types no hilitie 4     */
get_opts   = " OPT "                       /* option types           */
do_addquery= " COB "                       /* types 2 do addquery 4  */
severe_rc  = 12                            /* rc for sever error     */
option_dd  = "ENDVPRMS"                    /* DD 2 use for read opts */

glid = mvsVAR('symdef','GLBLID')
if glid = 'SY1' then,
   glid = 'SYT'
  /* This is a temporary Changes made 05/07/12 LAT to Correct LPAR */
if glid = 'SYD9' then,
   glid = 'SY9'

option_dsnt= "YourHQL.ENDV."glid".Test.TABLES(OPTIONS)" /* opts dsn     */
option_dsn = "YourHQL.ENDV."glid".Prod.TABLES(OPTIONS)" /* opts dsn     */

INITCMD.0=0
EXITCMD.0=0
MSGCMD.0=0

/*-------------------------------------------------------------------*/
/* FIRST, RETRIEVE THE DIALOG VARIABLES FROM THE PROFILE POOL.       */
/* NOTE: UNCOMMENT THIS CODE TO ACTIVATE THE VGET REQUEST.           */
/*-------------------------------------------------------------------*/
If USERID() = 'z#E094' then Trace ?r

address "ISPEXEC" ,
         'VGET (ENVBENV ENVBSYS ENVBSBS ENVBTYP ENVBSTGI ENVBSTGN
                ENVSENV ENVSSYS ENVSSBS ENVSTYP ENVSSTGI ENVSSTGN
                ENVELM  ENVPRGRP ENVCCID ENVCOM ENVGENE ENVOSIGN)
          PROFILE'

"ISREDIT (LINE) = CURSOR"   /* Determines whether any lines exist */
appl=strip(ENVBSYS)
stage=strip(ENVSSTGI)
elementn=strip(ENVELM)
system_opt =0
fac_opt    =0
appl_opt   =0
element_opt=0
infrastructure_opt=0
elementn_l=length(elementn)

if elementn="@DEFAULT"                            then system_opt =1
if elementn_l=8 & substr(elementn,1,7) ="DEFAULT" then fac_opt    =1
if appl=elementn & appl<>""                       then appl_opt   =1
if \system_opt & \fac_opt & \appl_opt             then element_opt=1
if appl="TEST SWET SWEF"                   then infrastructure_opt=1
if appl="ADMIN" & stage="Y"                then infrastructure_opt=1

ADDRESS ISREDIT 'NUM OFF'  /* Default to No sequence numbers */
if userid() = 'EGENG03' then Trace ?r

If substr(ENVBTYP,1,3) = 'TDF' then,  /* Telon Element */
   Do
   My_Rc = 24    /* 24 => nothing changed  (as default) */
   /*  'CUT' current source to import into TDF  ->  */
   ADDRESS ISREDIT "CUT" ;

   /*  Create a (temp) PDS and member for import into TDF  ->  */
   ADDRESS TSO,
    "ALLOC F(IMPORTSC) LRECL(80) BLKSIZE(0) SPACE(1,5)",
           "RECFM(F B) CYLINDERS  ",
           "DSORG(PO) DIR(50) DSNTYPE(PDS) ",
           "NEW UNCATALOG REUSE "     ;

   ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMINIT DATAID(IMPORT) DDNAME(IMPORTSC) " ;
   ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMOPEN DATAID("IMPORT") OPTION(INPUT) " ;
   LMOPEN_RC = RC ;
   ADDRESS ISPEXEC "ISPEXEC EDIT DATAID("IMPORT") MEMBER("ENVELM") ",
                   "MACRO(ENDIEIM4)"
   if RC > 0 then Return
   ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMCLOSE DATAID("IMPORT") ";
   ADDRESS TSO "EXECIO 0 DISKR IMPORTSC ( Finis"
   ADDRESS TSO "EXECIO 0 DISKW IMPORTSC ( Finis"

   /*  Imports to Telon then enter  TDF  ->  */
   Call EnterTelonDesignFacility ;
   /*    <-  Export  from Telon on the way out */
   /*        Export places member into TLGENLIB  */
   /*        TLEXIMIN helps us know the member name */
   x = LISTDSI("TLGENLIB" "FILE")
   If x > 4 then EXIT(My_RC)  /* 24 => nothing changed */
   x = LISTDSI("TLEXIMIN" "FILE")
   If x > 4 then EXIT(My_RC)  /* 24 => nothing changed */

   /*    Free the import PDS  */
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE  F(IMPORTSC)"

   /*    Get the contents of the member in TLGENLIB  */
   Call ExamineTDFExport ;
   /*    Put back all the LIBDEFs for Endevor        */
   Call RestoreEndevorLibraries;
   SA= 'Result from ENDIETDF is ' RESULT
   EXIT(My_RC)   /* 24 => nothing changed  / 20 => was changed */
   End    /* IF SUBSTR(ENVBTYP,1,3) = 'TDF' */

if substr(ENVBTYP,1,3) = 'OPT' then do
   if userid() = 'YourHQLG??' then trace ?r
   if LINE > 0 then do
      address "ISREDIT" " CURSOR = 1 1 "
      if RC > 0 then exit
      address "ISREDIT" " (LPOS1,CPOS1) = CURSOR "
      if RC > 0 then exit
      InterpretList = 'PGMTYPE IMS DB2 CICS IDMS DBUGOPT '  ,
                      'LINKTESTLoadlib '  ,
                      'Teradata MQSeries ISPF DeployType DB2Move'
      do w# = 1 to Words(InterpretList)
         wrd = Word(InterpretList,w#)
         tmp = wrd "= ''"
         interpret tmp
      end /* Do w# = 1 to Words(InterpretList) */
      FoundCommands = ' '
      FoundValues   = ' '
      FoundLines    = ' '
      do forever
         address "ISREDIT" " FIND P'=' 5 NEXT"
         if RC > 0 then leave
         address "ISREDIT" " (LPOS1,CPOS1) = CURSOR "
         address "ISREDIT" " (DLINE) = LINE "LPOS1
         IF substr(DLINE,1,1) = "*" then iterate
         tmp = Translate(DLINE," ","=")
         if words(tmp) < 2 then iterate
         if wordpos(word(tmp,1),InterpretList) = 0 then iterate
         valword= strip(strip(strip(strip(word(tmp,2)),B,'"'),B,"'"))
         FoundCommands = word(tmp,1)  " "  FoundCommands
         FoundValues   = valword  " "  FoundValues
         FoundLines    = LPOS1  " "  FoundLines
         interpret DLINE
      end  /* DO FOREVER */
   end   /*IF LINE > 0 */


   call Call_APIALELM                  /* Find PGMLANG .. via API */
   if userid() = 'YourHQLG??' then Trace ?r

   if pos('DeployType ',FoundCommands)>0 then DEPLOY   =DeployType
                                         else DEPLOY   =""
   if pos('Teradata ',FoundCommands)>0   then TERA     =Teradata
                                         else TERA     =""
   if pos('LINKTESTLoadlib ',FoundCommands)>0   then TL=LINKTESTLoadlib
                                         else TL       =""
   if pos('MQSeries ',FoundCommands)>0   then MQSERIES =MQSeries
                                         else MQSERIES =""
   if pos('DB2Move ',FoundCommands)>0    then DB2MOVE  =DB2Move
                                         else DB2MOVE  =""

   if strip(DEPLOY)<>"ENTERPRISE" then DEPLOY="NORMAL"
   if strip(PGMTYPE)=""           then PGMTYPE="BATCH"

   address "ISPEXEC" "DISPLAY PANEL ("opt_panel") "
   if RC > 0 then exit(24)

   DeployType     = DEPLOY
   Teradata       = TERA
   LINKTESTLoadlib= TL
   MQSeries       = MQSERIES
   DB2Move        = DB2MOVE


   if ADVOPT   = "A" then show_all    = "Y"
   if ADVOPT   = "I" then show_all    = "I"
   if ADVOPT   = "B" then show_all    = "N"
   if MNOTEAFT = "N" then mnote_after = "N"

   did_one=0
   DelLines=""

   if \element_opt then FIELDS="TL MQSERIES"
   do W# = 1 to words(FIELDS)                  /* gen list of all    */
      wrd = word(FIELDS,W#)                    /* lines with changed */
      if wrd="DEPLOY"   then wrd="DeployType"  /* values             */
      if wrd="TERA"     then wrd="Teradata"    /*                    */
      if wrd="TL"       then wrd="LINKTESTLoadlib"
      if wrd="DB2MOVE"  then wrd="DB2Move"
      if wrd="MQSERIES" then wrd="MQSeries"
      wrdValu=value(wrd)
      wp=wordpos(wrd,FoundCommands)
      if wp=0 then iterate
      oldvalue=word(FoundValues,wp)
      if oldvalue=wrdValu then iterate
      wl=word(FoundLines,wp)
      DelLines=DelLines  " "  wl
   end
   DelLines=DelLines  " "

   if strip(DelLines)<>"" then do
      do W# = 1 to words(FoundLines)            /* delete all the     */
         wl    =word(FoundLines,W#)             /* lines with changed */
         needle=" "  wl  " "                    /* values, will add   */
         if pos(needle,DelLines)=0 then iterate /* back later         */
         if \did_one then do
            "ISREDIT" "CAPS OFF"
            did_one=1
         end
         "ISREDIT" "DELETE "wl" "wl
      end
   end

   WHERE = 'LINE_BEFORE'
   TEMP  = '  OPT element for a' PGMLANG 'program.'
   if LINE > 0 then  'ISREDIT ' WHERE '.ZFIRST = MSGLINE "'TEMP'"'
   WHERE = 'LINE_AFTER'

   if USERID() = 'YourHQLG??' then trace ?r

   do W# = 1 to words(FIELDS)
      wrd = word(FIELDS,W#)
      if wrd="DEPLOY"   then wrd="DeployType"
      if wrd="TERA"     then wrd="Teradata"
      if wrd="TL"       then wrd="LINKTESTLoadlib"
      if wrd="DB2MOVE"  then wrd="DB2Move"
      if wrd="MQSERIES" then wrd="MQSeries"
      wrdValu=value(wrd)
      wp=wordpos(wrd,FoundCommands)
      if wp>0 then do
         oldvalue=word(FoundValues,wp)
         if oldvalue=wrdValu then iterate
      end
      if wp=0 & (wrdValu=''   wrdValu='N') then iterate
      TEMP=wrd  "= '"  wrdValu  "'"
      if wrd="LINKTESTLoadlib" & strip(wrdValu)="" then TEMP="*"  TEMP
      if \did_one then do
         "ISREDIT" "CAPS OFF"
         did_one=1
      end
      'ISREDIT ' WHERE '.ZLAST = DATALINE "'TEMP'"' ;
   end /* DO W# = 1 TO WORDS(FIELDS) */

end /* IF SUBSTR(ENVBTYP,1,3) = 'OPT' THEN */


IF SUBSTR(ENVBTYP,1,5) = 'EMAIL'   ,
   SUBSTR(ENVBTYP,1,4) = 'FORM'  THEN,
   DO
   IF LINE > 0 THEN,
      DO
      ADDRESS ISREDIT " CURSOR = 1 1 " ;
      IF RC > 0 THEN EXIT
      ADDRESS ISREDIT " (LPOS1,CPOS1) = CURSOR " ;
      IF RC > 0 THEN EXIT
      DO FOREVER
         ADDRESS ISREDIT " (DLINE) = LINE "LPOS1
         IF SUBSTR(DLINE,1,1) /= " " THEN,
            INTERPRET DLINE ;
         ADDRESS ISREDIT " FIND P'=' 1 NEXT" ;
         IF RC > 0 THEN LEAVE;
         ADDRESS ISREDIT " (LPOS1,CPOS1) = CURSOR " ;
      END;  /* DO FOREVER */
   END;  /*IF LINE = 0 */
   ADDRESS ISPEXEC,
       "DISPLAY PANEL ("ENVSTYP") "
   IF RC > 0 THEN MY_RC = 24 ;
   ELSE           MY_RC = 20 ;
   ADDRESS ISREDIT " DELETE ALL NX" ;
   WHERE = 'LINE_AFTER' ;
   TEMP = " "COPIES("_",80) ;
   'ISREDIT ' WHERE '.ZLAST = DATALINE "'TEMP'"' ;
   ADDRESS ISPEXEC,
       "VGET (ZSCREEN ZSCREENC ZSCREENI) SHARED"

   DO W# = 1 TO LENGTH(ZSCREENI) BY 80
      TEMP = " "SUBSTR(ZSCREENI,W#,80) ;
     'ISREDIT ' WHERE '.ZLAST = DATALINE "'TEMP'"' ;
   END

   TEMP = " "COPIES("_",80) ;
   'ISREDIT ' WHERE '.ZLAST = DATALINE "'TEMP'"' ;

   DO W# = 1 TO WORDS(FIELDS)
      TEMP = " "WORD(FIELDS,W#) "=",
         "'"VALUE(WORD(FIELDS,W#))"'" ;
     'ISREDIT ' WHERE '.ZLAST = DATALINE "'TEMP'"' ;
   END

   ADDRESS ISREDIT 'SAVE'
   EXIT(MY_RC) ;
END;
/*                                                                   */

/*--Changes for PDNF or PDA  -------------->>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>*/
   IF LINE > 0 THEN,
      ADDRESS ISREDIT 'PDA'    /*or use PDNFCSV */
/*--Changes for PDNF or PDA  -<<<<<<<<<<<<---------------------------*/



if my_rc <> 0 then return my_rc


which_IEWL=""
if PGMTYPE="STOREDPROC" then which_IEWL="SP"
if PGMTYPE="GLOBALSUB"  then which_IEWL="SP"
if PGMTYPE="SUBROUTINE" & (IMS="Y"   CICS = "Y") then which_IEWL="SP"
if PGMTYPE="ONLINE" then which_IEWL="ON"
show_when = "0"                 /*  0 - Generic option               */
If PGMLANG = 'ASM' then,
show_when = show_when  "A"      /*  A - Assembler                    */
If PGMLANG = 'TCOB' then,
show_when = show_when  "B"      /*  B - Cobol                        */
If PGMLANG = 'COB' then,
show_when = show_when  "B"      /*  B - Cobol                        */
If PGMLANG = 'C' then,
show_when = show_when  "E"      /*  E - D                            */
If CICS = 'Y' then,
show_when = show_when  "C"      /*  C - CICS                         */
If DB2 = 'Y' & PGMTYPE <> "STOREDPROC" & PGMTYPE <> "GLOBALSP" then,
show_when = show_when  "D"      /*  D - DB2 package                  */
If IDMS = 'Y' then,
show_when = show_when  "H"      /*  H - IDMS                         */
If IMS = 'Y' then,
show_when = show_when  "I"      /*  I - IMS                          */
If PGMLANG = 'JAVA' then,
show_when = show_when  "J"      /*  J - Java                         */
If DB2 = 'Y' & (PGMTYPE="ONLINE" PGMTYPE="BATCH") then,
show_when = show_when  "L"      /*  L - DB2 plan                     */
If MQSeries = 'Y' then,
show_when = show_when  "M"      /*  M - MQ                           */
If PGMTYPE  = 'STOREDPROC'   PGMTYPE = 'GLOBALSP' then ,
show_when = show_when  "P"      /*  P - DB2 Stored Proc              */
If PGMTYPE  = 'UDF'                               then ,
show_when = show_when  "F"      /*  P - DB2 Stored Proc              */
If PGMTYPE = "RLF" then,
show_when = "R"                 /*  R - RLF                          */
If ISPF     = 'Y' then,
show_when = show_when  "S"      /*  S - ISPF                         */
If Teradata = 'Y' then,
show_when = show_when  "T"      /*  T - Teradata                     */
If PGMLANG  = "SQL" & (PGMTYPE="STOREDPROC" PGMTYPE="GLOBALSP") then ,
show_when = show_when  "V"      /*  V - DB2 Native Stored Proc       */
If PGMLANG = 'REX' then,
show_when = show_when  "X"      /*  X - Rexx                         */
If PGMTYPE="DDLIVP" then,
show_when = show_when  "2"      /*  2 - DDL                          */



parm  = ENVBTYP  " "  ENVPRGRP
parm2 = ENVBTYP  " "  ENVPRGRP
if my_rc=0 then my_rc=init_cmds(ENVBTYP)      /* set initial cmds    */
if my_rc=0 then my_rc=exit_cmds(parm)         /* set exit    cmds    */
if my_rc=0 then my_rc=init_opts(ENVBTYP)      /* initialize opt array*/
if my_rc=0 then my_rc=build_lines(ENVBTYP)    /* build msg lines     */

do ii = 1 to INITCMD.0 while my_rc = 0  /* perform all  initial cmds */
   address "ISREDIT" INITCMD.ii
end

if my_rc=0 then my_rc=msg_cmds(LINE)          /* build msg cmds      */

do ii = 1 to MSGCMD.0 while my_rc = 0   /* perform all  msg     cmds */
   address "ISREDIT" MSGCMD.ii
end

do ii = 1 to EXITCMD.0 while my_rc = 0  /* perform all  exit    cmds */
   address "ISREDIT" EXITCMD.ii
end

return my_rc



/*-------*/
msg_cmds:  procedure expose MSGS. MSGCMD. AMSGS. mnote_after
/*-------*/
arg lineno

my_rc = 0

MSGCMD.0 = MSGS.0

if MSGS.0 = 0 then return 0

if lineno > 0 then do
   if mnote_after = "N" then do
      do ii = 1 to AMSGS.0
         MSGCMD.ii = 'LINE_BEFORE .ZF = NOTELINE "'  AMSGS.ii  '" '
      end
      jj = AMSGS.0
      do ii = 1 to MSGS.0
         jj = jj+1
         MSGCMD.jj = 'LINE_BEFORE .ZF = NOTELINE "'  MSGS.ii  '" '
      end
   end
   else do
      jj = 0
      do ii = MSGS.0 to 1 by -1
         jj = jj+1
         MSGCMD.jj = 'LINE_AFTER .ZLAST = NOTELINE "'  MSGS.ii  '" '
      end
      do ii = AMSGS.0 to 1 by -1
         jj = jj+1
         MSGCMD.jj = 'LINE_AFTER .ZLAST = NOTELINE "'  AMSGS.ii  '" '
      end
   end
end
else do
   jj = 0
   do ii = MSGS.0 to 1 by -1
      jj = jj+1
      MSGCMD.jj = 'LINE_AFTER .ZF = NOTELINE "'  MSGS.ii  '" '
   end
   do ii = AMSGS.0 to 1 by -1
      jj = jj+1
      MSGCMD.jj = 'LINE_AFTER .ZF = NOTELINE "'  AMSGS.ii  '" '
   end
end

MSGCMD.0 = jj

return my_rc


/*-------*/
init_cmds: procedure expose INITCMD. num_off caps_off hilite_off ,
                            num_on_cob num_on_std

/*-------*/
arg type

my_rc = 0
cntr = 0
needle = " "  strip(type)  " "

if pos(needle,hilite_off) = 0 then do
   cntr = cntr + 1
   INITCMD.cntr = "HILITE AUTO"
end

if pos(needle,caps_off) <> 0 then do
   cntr = cntr + 1
   INITCMD.cntr = "CAPS OFF"
end

if pos(needle,num_off) <> 0 then do
   cntr = cntr + 1
   INITCMD.cntr = "NUM OFF"
end

if pos(needle,num_on_cob) <> 0 then do
   cntr = cntr + 1
   INITCMD.cntr = "NUM ON COB"
end

if pos(needle,num_on_std) <> 0 then do
   cntr = cntr + 1
   INITCMD.cntr = "NUM ON STD"
end

cntr = cntr + 1
INITCMD.cntr = "(LINE) = CURSOR"

INITCMD.0 = cntr

return my_rc


/*-------*/
exit_cmds: procedure expose EXITCMD. do_addquery
/*-------*/
arg type group

my_rc = 0
cntr = 0
type   = strip(type)
needle = " "  substr(type,1,3)  " "
group   = strip(group)
group_l = length(group)


if pos(needle,do_addquery) <> 0 then do
   if group_l >= 5 then do
      if substr(group,5,1) = '2' then do
         cntr = cntr + 1
         EXITCMD.cntr = "ADDQRYNO"
      end
   end
end

EXITCMD.0 = cntr

return my_rc


/*-------*/
init_opts: procedure expose VOPT. VOPT_cnt option_dd severe_rc ,
                            option_dsn option_dsnt get_opts
/*-------*/
arg type

my_rc= 0
type = strip(type)
type_l = length(type)
if type_l < 3 then return 0
needle = " "  substr(type,1,3)  " "
if pos(needle,get_opts) = 0 then return 0

need_free = 0
dsn = ""
x = LISTDSI(option_dd "FILE")
if x <= 4 then do
   dsn = sysdsname  "(OPTIONS)"
end
if strip(dsn)<>"" then do
   if 'SYSDSN'("'"dsn"'") <> 'OK' then do
      dsn=""
      x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
      address "TSO" "FREE FI("option_dd")"
      x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
      need_free = 1
   end
end
if strip(dsn) = "" then do
   need_free = 1
   uuu=userid()
   dsn = option_dsn
   if substr(uuu,1,5)="YourHQLG"   ,
      substr(uuu,1,5)="EGENG" then do
      dsn = option_dsnt
      if 'SYSDSN'("'"dsn"'") <> 'OK' then dsn=option_dsn
   end
   cmd = "ALLOC FI("  option_dd  ") DA('"  dsn  "') SHR REUSE"
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" cmd
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      say "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "cmd
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
     end
     return severe_rc
   end
end

my_cmd = "EXECIO * DISKR "  option_dd  " (STEM PRMS."
my_cmd
io_rc = RC
if io_rc <> 0 then do
   say "IO Error RC="io_rc" for "my_cmd
   return severe_rc
end
do ii = 1 to PRMS.0
   if strip(PRMS.ii) = ""       then iterate
   if substr(PRMS.ii,1,1) = "*" then iterate
   VOPT_cnt = VOPT_cnt + 1
   VOPT.VOPT_cnt.PARM     = strip(substr(PRMS.ii,1,31))
   VOPT.VOPT_cnt.SHOWME   = strip(substr(PRMS.ii,32,1))
   VOPT.VOPT_cnt.XCLUDE   = strip(substr(PRMS.ii,33,1))
   VOPT.VOPT_cnt.DISPCODES= strip(substr(PRMS.ii,37,8))
   VOPT.VOPT_cnt.ROUTINE  = strip(substr(PRMS.ii,46,12))
   VOPT.VOPT_cnt.VALUES   = strip(substr(PRMS.ii,59,1940))
end
VOPT.0 = VOPT_cnt

if need_free=1 then do
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" "FREE FI("option_dd")"
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
end

return 0



/*-------*/
build_lines: procedure expose VOPT. MSGS. msg_cntr AMSGS. amsg_cntr ,
                              show_all show_when which_IEWL ,
                              infrastructure_opt appl ,
                              element_opt fac_opt appl_opt system_opt
/*-------*/
arg type

my_rc = 0

type = strip(type)
type_l = length(type)
if type_l < 3 then return 0
type_s = substr(type,1,3)

if my_rc=0 then my_rc=all_lines()
if my_rc=0 & type_s="OPT" then my_rc=opt_lines(type_s)
if my_rc=0 & ,
   (type="SHIPMENT") then my_rc=ship_lines()
if my_rc=0 & ,
   (type="MEMPRINT") then my_rc=fprint_lines()
if my_rc=0 & ,
   (type="PATTERNS") then my_rc=patt_lines()
if my_rc=0 & ,
   (type="DESTVALD") then my_rc=destvald_lines()
if my_rc=0 & ,
   (type="DESTTABL") then my_rc=desttabl_lines()
if my_rc=0 & ,
   (type="SPDEF"   type="SPPARM") then my_rc=sp_lines()
if my_rc=0 & ,
   (type="FNPARM") then my_rc=fn_lines()
if my_rc=0 & ,
   (type="SQLPL")                 then my_rc=sqlpl_lines()
if my_rc=0 & ,
   (type="RLF") then my_rc=rlf_lines()


MSGS.0 = msg_cntr

return my_rc




/*-------*/
opt_lines: procedure expose VOPT. MSGS. msg_cntr show_all show_when ,
                              infrastructure_opt which_IEWL ,
                              element_opt fac_opt appl_opt system_opt
/*-------*/
arg type
my_rc = 0
line_length = 72
n = line_length-31-1

do ii = 1 to VOPT.0 while my_rc = 0
   if VOPT.ii.ROUTINE = "ver_notallo" then iterate
   opt = strip(VOPT.ii.PARM)
   val = strip(VOPT.ii.VALUES)
   rtn = strip(VOPT.ii.ROUTINE)
   show= strip(VOPT.ii.SHOWME)
   xcld= strip(VOPT.ii.XCLUDE)
   cod= strip(VOPT.ii.DISPCODES)
   if show="N" then iterate                  /* if never show then */
                                             /* skip               */
   if xcld="E" & element_opt then iterate    /* not applic to      */
                                             /* element, skip      */
   if xcld="I" & \infrastructure_opt then iterate  /* if not       */
                                             /* infrastructure,skip*/
   if xcld="F" & (element_opt appl_opt) ,    /* not applic to      */
      then iterate                           /* element/ appl skip */

   if xcld="A" & (appl_opt fac_opt)     ,    /* if appl or fac     */
      then iterate                           /* skip               */

   if xcld="L" & (appl_opt)             ,    /* if appl            */
      then iterate                           /* skip               */

   if xcld="G" & (element_opt appl_opt fac_opt)  /* not applic     */
      then iterate                           /* element/appl/fac   */
                                             /* skip               */
   if show_all="I" & show="A" then iterate   /* if advanced, don't */
                                             /* show for intermed  */
   if show_all="N" & show<>"Y" then iterate  /* if not always show */
                                             /* then skip          */

   codes = strip(show_when)
   showit=0
   do jj = 1 to length(codes) while showit=0
      x = substr(codes,jj,1)
      if pos(x,cod) <> 0 then showit=1
   end
   if showit = 0 then iterate

   if rtn = "ver_num"   then val = word(val,1)
   if rtn = "ver_clist" then val = word(val,1)
   if rtn = "ver_1List" then do
      parse var val w1 rest
      rest = strip(rest)
      rest = translate(rest,'/',' ')
      val = w1  "  /"  rest
   end
   if rtn = "ver_noneL" & element_opt then do
      parse var val "'" f1 "'" j1 "SP('" f2 "')" j2 "ON('" f3 "')" j3
      if which_IEWL =""   then val="'"f1"'"
      if which_IEWL ="SP" then val="'"f2"'"
      if which_IEWL ="ON" then val="'"f3"'"
   end
   opt_l = length(opt)
   val_l = length(val)
   if val_l <=n then do
      msg_cntr = msg_cntr + 1
      MSGS.msg_cntr = left(opt,31)  "="  val
   end
   else do
      if opt_l+1+val_l <=line_length then do
         msg_cntr = msg_cntr + 1
         MSGS.msg_cntr = opt  "="  val
      end
      else do
         msg_cntr = msg_cntr + 1
         MSGS.msg_cntr = opt  "=,"
         val = strip(strip(strip(strip(val),B,'"'),B,"'"))
         val_l = length(val)
         if val_l <= 70 then do
            msg_cntr = msg_cntr + 1
            MSGS.msg_cntr = "'"  val  "'"
            val_l = 0
         end
         do while val_l > 0
            if val_l > 60 then do
               msg_cntr = msg_cntr + 1
               MSGS.msg_cntr = "'"  substr(val,1,59)  "',"
               val = delstr(val,1,59)
               val_l = length(val)
            end
            else do
               msg_cntr = msg_cntr + 1
               MSGS.msg_cntr = "'"  val  "'"
               val_l = 0
            end
         end
      end
   end
end

return 0

/*-------*/
all_lines: procedure expose AMSGS. amsg_cntr
/*-------*/

my_rc = 0

amsg_cntr=amsg_cntr + 1
AMSGS.amsg_cntr = "***"
amsg_cntr=amsg_cntr + 1
AMSGS.amsg_cntr = "*** Use MD line command to retain example line(s)"
amsg_cntr=amsg_cntr + 1
AMSGS.amsg_cntr = "***   MD is the ISPF EDIT MakeData command"
amsg_cntr=amsg_cntr + 1
AMSGS.amsg_cntr = "***"

AMSGS.0 =amsg_cntr

return my_rc

Call_APIALELM :       /* Find PGMLANG by using API to search Endevor */

   if USERID() = 'DIRTBAG' then trace  r

   ADDRESS TSO
/*                                                                   */
    "ALLOC F(SYSPRINT) DUMMY REUSE " ;
    "ALLOC F(SYSOUT) DUMMY REUSE " ;
/*                                                                   */
    "ALLOC F(SYSIN) LRECL(80) BLKSIZE(0) SPACE(5,5)",
           "RECFM(F B) TRACKS ",
           "NEW UNCATALOG REUSE "     ;
    "ALLOC F(MSGFILE) LRECL(133) BLKSIZE(13300) SPACE(5,5)",
           "RECFM(F B) TRACKS ",
           "NEW UNCATALOG REUSE "     ;
    "ALLOC F(ELEMLIST) LRECL(2048) BLKSIZE(22800) SPACE(5,5)",
           "RECFM(V B) TRACKS DSORG(PS) ",
           "NEW UNCATALOG REUSE "     ;
       ENVIRONMENT = '        ' ;
       ENVIRONMENT = SUBSTR(ENVSENV'        ',1,8) ;
             STAGE = ENVSSTGI ;
            SYSTEM = ENVSSYS  ;
         SUBSYSTEM = ENVBSBS  ;
              TYPE = '*       ' ;
         ELEMENT   = ENVELM ;
       QUEUE 'AACTL MSGFILE ELEMLIST'
  /*                                                                */
  /*     V - COLUMN 7 = RETURN SETTING                              */
  /*       = ' ' FOR FIRST FOUND                                    */
  /*       = 'F' FOR FIRST FOUND                                    */
  /*       = 'A' FOR ALL FOUND                                      */
  /*      V - COLUMN 8 = SEARCH SETTING                             */
  /*       = ' ' FOR FIRST                                          */
  /*       = 'A' FOR ALL                                            */
  /*       = 'B' FOR BETWEEN                                        */
  /*       = 'E' FOR NEXT                                           */
  /*       = 'N' FOR NO                                             */
  /*       = 'R' FOR RANGE                                          */
  /*       VVVVVVVV - COLUMN 10-17 ENVIRONMENT NAME                 */
  /*               V - COLUMN 18 = STAGE ID                         */
  /*                VVVVVVVV - COLUMN 19-26 SYSTEM NAME             */
  /*                        VVVVVVVV - COLUMN 27-34 SUBSYSTEM NAME  */
  /*   COLUMN 35-44 = ELEMENT NAME  VVVVVVVVVV                      */
  /*   COLUMN 45-52 = TYPE NAME               VVVVVVVV              */
  /*                                                                */
       TEMP= COPIES(" ",80);
       TEMP= Overlay('ALELM    ',TEMP,1) ;
       TEMP= Overlay(ENVIRONMENT,TEMP,10) ;  /* Enter Env info here*/
       TEMP= Overlay(STAGE,TEMP,18) ;
       TEMP= Overlay(SYSTEM,TEMP,19) ;
       TEMP= Overlay(SUBSYSTEM,TEMP,27) ;
       TEMP= Overlay(ELEMENT,TEMP,35) ;
       TEMP= Overlay(TYPE,TEMP,45) ;
       SA= TEMP;
       QUEUE TEMP ;
       QUEUE 'RUN' ;

       QUEUE 'AACTLY ' ;
       QUEUE 'RUN' ;
       QUEUE 'QUIT' ;
       ADDRESS TSO,
       "EXECIO" QUEUED() "DISKW SYSIN (FINIS "
       RETURN_RC = 0  ;
       ADDRESS TSO "PROFILE NOWTPMSG " ;

       ADDRESS ISPEXEC "SELECT PGM(ENTBJAPI)" ;
       IF RC > 0 THEN,
          DO
          SA= 'CANNOT GET INFORMATION FROM ENDEVOR' ;
          EXIT
          END ;
       RETURN_RC = RC ;

   ADDRESS TSO,
   "EXECIO * DISKR ELEMLIST (STEM ENDEVOR. FINIS" ;
    DISKR_rc = RC
    ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(ELEMLIST) "

    LangList=""
    DO I = 1 to ENDEVOR.0
       tmp = TRANSLATE(ENDEVOR.I,"'",'"') ;
       Ltemp    = Substr(tmp,49,8)
       if Ltemp="FNPARM" then Ltemp="SQL"
       if Ltemp="SPPARM" then Ltemp="SQL"
       if Ltemp="SQLPL"  then Ltemp="SQL"
       if wordpos(Ltemp,LangList)=0 then LangList=Langlist  " "  Ltemp
    END ; /* DO I = 1 TO ENDEVOR.0*/

    PGMLANG=""
    tryLangs="COB ASM PLI C REX JAVA SQL DDLIVP TCOB"
    do la=1 to words(tryLangs) while PGMLANG=""
       lal=word(tryLangs,la)
       if wordpos(lal,LangList)=0 then iterate
       PGMLANG=lal
    end
    if PGMLANG<>"" then return

    skipLangs="OPT"
    do la=1 to words(LangList) while PGMLANG=""
       lal=word(LangList,la)
       if wordpos(lal,skipLangs)<>0 then iterate
       PGMLANG=lal
    end
    PGMLANG="?"

   Return ;

EnterTelonDesignFacility :

   NumberQueued  = QUEUED()
   /* Clear any data on the stack */
   Do q# = 1 to NumberQueued
      Pull values
   End;

   /* Save Endevor choices        */
   ADDRESS ISPEXEC "VGET (GLID ENDVTEST) PROFILE"

   ADDRESS TSO,
    "ALLOC F(QUIKEDIT) LRECL(80) BLKSIZE(0) SPACE(5,5)",
           "RECFM(F B) TRACKS ",
           "NEW UNCATALOG REUSE "     ;
   PUSH 'ENVELM=' ENVELM
   PUSH 'ENVSENV='ENVSENV
   PUSH 'ENVBENV='ENVBENV
   PUSH 'ENVBSBS='ENVBSBS
   PUSH 'ENVSSBS='ENVSSBS
   PUSH 'ENVBSYS='ENVBSYS
   PUSH 'ENVSSYS='ENVSSYS
   "EXECIO" QUEUED() "DISKW QUIKEDIT ( FINIS"

   ADDRESS ISPEXEC "SELECT CMD(ENDIETDF) NEWAPPL(TDF) PASSLIB "
   TDF_RC  = RC ;

   ADDRESS TSO,
    "FREE  F(QUIKEDIT)"

   Return;

ExamineTDFExport :
  /* Telon uses its own member name structure....
     ... a different arrangement of the parts    */
  "EXECIO * DISKR TLEXIMIN ( Stem tln. FINIS"

  MEMBERtail = Word(tln.1,2)            /*  BD / SD */
  sa = 'in ENDIEIM1'
  MEMBER = Substr(ENVELM,1,2)    Substr(ENVELM,5)    MEMBERtail
  MEMBER = STRIP(MEMBER)

  ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMINIT DATAID(TELON) DDNAME(TLGENLIB) " ;
  ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMOPEN DATAID("TELON") OPTION(INPUT) " ;
  LMOPEN_RC = RC ;
  ADDRESS ISPEXEC "ISPEXEC VIEW DATAID("TELON") MEMBER("MEMBER") ",
                  "MACRO(ENDIEIM2)"
  if RC > 0 then Return
  ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMCLOSE DATAID("TELON") ";

  ADDRESS ISREDIT "DELETE ALL NX" ;
  ADDRESS ISREDIT "PASTE AFTER .ZFIRST"
  if RC > 0 then Return
  ADDRESS ISREDIT "SAVE"

  My_Rc = 20    /* 20 => Element changed  */
  SA= "TELON PROGRAM "ENVELM "UPDATED FROM TDF" ;

  "FREE DD(TLGENLIB)"   /* Free Exported Telon dataset(member) */
  "FREE DD(TLEXIMIN)"   /* Free Exported Telon dataset(member) */

  Return

RestoreEndevorLibraries:
 /* Telon routines establised a different set of library allocations */
 /* This routint makes Endevor happy again  */

 LibNodes = "'YourHQL.ENDV."GLID".Prod.REX'" ;
 If ENDVTEST = 'Y' then,
    LibNodes = "'YourHQL.ENDV."GLID".Test.REX'" LibNodes
 ADDRESS TSO

 "ALTLIB DEACTIVATE APPLICATION(CLIST)"

 "ALTLIB ACTIVATE APPLICATION(CLIST)",
      "DATASET(",
              LibNodes ,
              "'SYS3.CAENDV.Q.R15.CSIQCLS0'",
              "'YourHQL.ENDV.SYQ.ENDEVOR.EXEC'",
              ")"

 LibNodes = "'YourHQL.ENDV."GLID".Prod.PNL'" ;
 If ENDVTEST = 'Y' then,
    LibNodes = "'YourHQL.ENDV."GLID".Test.PNL'" LibNodes
  ADDRESS ISPEXEC
  "LIBDEF ISPPLIB DATASET ID(",
              LibNodes ,
          "'SYS3.CAENDV.Q.R15.CSIQPENU'",
          ") COND STACK"

 LibNodes = "'YourHQL.ENDV."GLID".Prod.MSG'" ;
 If ENDVTEST = 'Y' then,
    LibNodes = "'YourHQL.ENDV."GLID".Test.MSG'" LibNodes
  ADDRESS ISPEXEC
  "LIBDEF ISPMLIB DATASET ID(",
              LibNodes ,
          "'SYS3.CAENDV.Q.R15.CSIQMENU'",
          ") COND STACK"

 LibNodes = "'YourHQL.ENDV."GLID".Prod.SKL'" ;
 If ENDVTEST = 'Y' then,
    LibNodes = "'YourHQL.ENDV."GLID".Test.SKL'" LibNodes
  ADDRESS ISPEXEC
  "LIBDEF ISPSLIB DATASET ID(",
              LibNodes ,
          "'SYS3.CAENDV.Q.R15.CSIQSENU'",
          ") COND STACK"

  Return

./  ADD  NAME=ENDIEIM2
/*   REXX   */
  "ISREDIT MACRO " ;
  TRACE O
  ADDRESS ISREDIT "CUT" ;
  ADDRESS ISREDIT "CANCEL" ;
  EXIT

./  ADD  NAME=ENDIEIM3
/*   REXX   */
  "ISREDIT MACRO " ;

  ADDRESS ISPEXEC
            'VGET (ENVSENV ENVSSYS ENVSSBS ENVSTYP ENVSSTGI ENVSSTGN
                   ENVELM  ENVPRGRP ENVCCID ENVCOM ENVGENE ENVOSIGN)

  "ISREDIT COPY '"OPT_LIBRARY"("ENVSTYP")'",
                   "AFTER  .ZLAST  " ;

  ADDRESS ISREDIT "CHANGE '<NAME>' '"ENVELM"' ALL "

  ADDRESS ISREDIT "RESET"


   line = COPIES("<",04) COPIES(" ",64) COPIES(">",04)
   TEXT = "Program" ENVELM "does not have"
   line = overlay(text,line,5) ;
      'ISREDIT  LINE_BEFORE .ZF   = INFOLINE "'line'"' ;

   line = COPIES("<",04) COPIES(" ",64) COPIES(">",04)
   TEXT = "either a default OPT or a program OPT."
   line = overlay(text,line,9) ;
      'ISREDIT  LINE_BEFORE .ZF   = INFOLINE "'line'"' ;

   line = COPIES("<",04) COPIES(" ",64) COPIES(">",04)
   TEXT = "An example OPT is presented below",
          "for your review. "
   line = overlay(text,line,5) ;
      'ISREDIT  LINE_BEFORE .ZF   = INFOLINE "'line'"' ;

   line = COPIES("<",04) COPIES(" ",64) COPIES(">",04)
   TEXT = "Modify and 'End' to cause it",
          "to be created automatically for you."
   line = overlay(text,line,5) ;
      'ISREDIT  LINE_BEFORE .ZF   = INFOLINE "'line'"' ;

   line = COPIES("<",04) COPIES(" ",64) COPIES(">",04)
      'ISREDIT  LINE_BEFORE .ZF   = INFOLINE "'line'"' ;

   line = "***<DB2* = '*STAGE *SUBSYS *PLAN****",
                    "*MEMBER*  *QUAL** *OWNER**'"
      'ISREDIT  LINE_AFTER .ZL   = NOTELINE "'line'"' ;

   line = "  BIND.# = 'PRD    DP1G    CAZZZZZZ ",
             "CASZZZZZ  PFSYUC  PFSYUC'";
      'ISREDIT  LINE_AFTER .ZL   = NOTELINE "'line'"' ;

   line = "  BIND.# = 'QA     D2DA    CAZZZZZZ ",
             "CASZZZZZ  PHQAUG  PHQAUG '";
      'ISREDIT  LINE_AFTER .ZL   = NOTELINE "'line'"' ;

   line = "  BIND.# = 'UT     D2DB    CAZZZZZZ ",
             "CASZZZZZ  PHDVUG  USERID'";
      'ISREDIT  LINE_AFTER .ZL   = NOTELINE "'line'"' ;

   line = "***>DB2* = '*STAGE *SUBSYS *PLAN****",
                    "*MEMBER*  *QUAL** *OWNER**'"
      'ISREDIT  LINE_AFTER .ZL   = NOTELINE "'line'"' ;


   TEXT = "  LINK1.# = 'INCLUDE SYSLIB(CAZZZZZZ)' "

./  ADD  NAME=ENDIETDF
/* REXX                                                              */
/*-------------------------------------------------------------------*/
/*  Direct a Quick-Edit session request to the Telon TDF panels.     */
/*-------------------------------------------------------------------*/
   Trace O

  IF USERID()  = 'Z#E094' THEN trace ?r ;
   /* Element information is passed within QUIKEDIT data */
   "EXECIO * DISKR QUIKEDIT ( Stem qedit. FINIS"
   NumberQueued  = QUEUED()
   Do q# = 1 to qedit.0
      Interpret qedit.q#
   End;

/* Establish hlq prefixes for work libraries    */
   ImportDatasetNamePrefix = USERID()    '.TDF.IMPORT.'   ENVELM

/* Determine which TDF libraries to use    */
   Enode = '1'
   If Substr(ENVBENV,1,4) = 'TEST' then,
      Enode = Substr(ENVBENV,5,1) ;
   VSQUAL='TE.AA.E1.TELON'
   VSQUAL='TE.AA.E'    Enode    '.TELON'

   /* Element information is passed within QUIKEDIT data */
   TDF_RC  = 0
   Call TelonLibraryAllocations ;
   Call ImportToTDF

   Call EnterTelonDesignFacility;

   Call TelonLibraryAllocations ;
   Call ExportToPDS ;
   Call TelonLibraryFrees ;

   IF TDF_RC > 0 THEN EXIT(24)  /* No changes, just Exit */
   EXIT(0)     /* All is OK */

ImportToTDF :

   /* Delete previous work libraries if they exist       */
   X = OUTTRAP(LINE.);
  "DELETE  '"ImportDatasetNamePrefix".*'"
   X = OUTTRAP(OFF);

   /* Source for Import is within the IMPORDSC dd (file) */
   /*  ... placed there by ENDIEIM1                      */
   x = LISTDSI("IMPORTSC" "FILE")
   if x > 4 then,
      Do
      Say 'Trouble . getting out'
      Exit(8)
      End
   IMPORTSC_Dsn = SYSDSNAME ;

   /* These Rexx procedures are like the stesp of the IMPORT JCL */
   MODLIB_Dsn = ImportDatasetNamePrefix".MODLIB"
   Call ImportStep1_IEBUPDTE ;

   RUNPRMS_Dsn = ImportDatasetNamePrefix".RUNPRMS"
   Call Import_SETPARM_ADPACTLC

   SCRNDEF_Dsn = ImportDatasetNamePrefix".SCRNDEF"
   Call Import_CONTROL_ADPCCARD

   CTLCRDS_Dsn = ImportDatasetNamePrefix".CTLCRDS"
   Call Import_GEN_ASMA90

   CARDIN_Dsn = ImportDatasetNamePrefix".CARDIN"
   Call Import_GETCODE_IEBPTPCH

   Call Import_IMPORT_TELONTDF

   Return

ImportStep1_IEBUPDTE :
  /*  Allocate Datasets for import IEBUPDTE                   */
   /*  Create a (temp) PDS (like MODLIB)                   ->  */
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(SYSUT1) DUMMY SHR REUSE "
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(SYSPRINT)",
          "LRECL(133) BLKSIZE(13300) SPACE(5,5)",
          "RECFM(V B) TRACKS ",
          "NEW UNCATALOG REUSE "     ;
   ADDRESS TSO,
    "ALLOC F(SYSUT2) DA('"MODLIB_Dsn"')",
           "LRECL(80) BLKSIZE(0) SPACE(1,5)",
           "RECFM(F B) CYLINDERS  ",
           "DSORG(PO) DIR(50) DSNTYPE(PDS) ",
           "NEW CATALOG REUSE "     ;
   ADDRESS TSO,
    "ALLOC F(SYSIN) DA('"IMPORTSC_Dsn"("ENVELM")') SHR REUSE"
   ADDRESS LINKMVS 'IEBUPDTE' 'NEW'

   IF RC > 4 THEN,
       Do
       Say "Could not Import the program" ENVELM
       ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMINIT DATAID(DDID) DDNAME(SYSPRINT)"
       ADDRESS ISPEXEC "VIEW DATAID(&DDID)"
       ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMFREE DATAID(&DDID)"
       EXIT(8)
       End

   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSIN)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSUT1)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSUT2)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSPRINT)"

   Return

Import_SETPARM_ADPACTLC :
  /*  Allocate Datasets for import ADPACTLC                   */
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(D) DA('"RUNPRMS_Dsn"')",
          "LRECL(80) BLKSIZE(800) SPACE(1,1)",
          "RECFM(F B) TRACKS ",
          "NEW CATALOG REUSE "     ;
   PARMS = 'IEFBR14,,D,I 00'
   ADDRESS ISPEXEC "SELECT PGM(ADPACTLC) PARM("PARMS")"

   IF RC > 4 THEN,
       Do
       Say "Could not Import the program" ENVELM
       EXIT(8)
       End

   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(D)"

   Return

Import_CONTROL_ADPCCARD :
  /*  Allocate Datasets                                       */

   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(SYSIN) DUMMY SHR REUSE "
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(SYSOUT) DA(*) SHR REUSE "

   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(SYSUT1)",
               "DA('"MODLIB_Dsn"("SCRNDEF")') SHR REUSE"

   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(SYSUT2) DA('"SCRNDEF_Dsn"')",
          "LRECL(080) BLKSIZE(03600) SPACE(5,5)",
          "RECFM(F B) TRACKS ",
          "NEW CATALOG REUSE "     ;

   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(SYSPRINT)",
          "LRECL(133) BLKSIZE(13300) SPACE(5,5)",
          "RECFM(V B) TRACKS ",
          "NEW UNCATALOG REUSE "     ;

   PARMS='RGEN1.2'
   ADDRESS ISPEXEC "SELECT PGM(ADPCCARD) PARM("PARMS")"

   IF RC > 4 THEN,
       Do
       Say "Could not Import the program" ENVELM
       ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMINIT DATAID(DDID) DDNAME(SYSPRINT)"
       ADDRESS ISPEXEC "VIEW DATAID(&DDID)"
       ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMFREE DATAID(&DDID)"
       EXIT(8)
       End

   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSIN)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSOUT)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSUT1)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSUT2)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSPRINT)"

   Return

Import_GEN_ASMA90 :

   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(SYSIN) DA('"SCRNDEF_Dsn"')"
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(SYSLIN) DUMMY REUSE "
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(SYSLIB)",
          "DA('SDPROD.TELON.R51.CAWLMAC') SHR REUSE"
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(SYSPUNCH) DA('"CTLCRDS_Dsn"')",
          "LRECL(080) BLKSIZE(06160) SPACE(5,5)",
          "RECFM(F B) TRACKS ",
          "NEW CATALOG REUSE "     ;
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(SYSPRINT)",
          "LRECL(133) BLKSIZE(13300) SPACE(5,5)",
          "RECFM(V B) TRACKS ",
          "NEW UNCATALOG REUSE "     ;
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(SYSUT1) SPACE(5,5) CYLINDERS "
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(SYSUT2) SPACE(5,5) CYLINDERS "
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(SYSUT3) SPACE(5,5) CYLINDERS "

   PARMS='SYSPARM(RGEN1.2),NOOBJECT,DECK'
   ADDRESS ISPEXEC "SELECT PGM(ASMA90) PARM("PARMS")"

   IF RC > 4 THEN,
       Do
       Trace ?r
       Say "Could not Import the program" ENVELM
       ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMINIT DATAID(DDID) DDNAME(SYSPRINT)"
       ADDRESS ISPEXEC "VIEW DATAID(&DDID)"
       ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMFREE DATAID(&DDID)"
       EXIT(8)
       End

   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSIN)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSLIN)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSLIB)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSPRINT)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSPUNCH)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSUT1)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSUT2)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSUT3)"
   Return

Import_GETCODE_IEBPTPCH :

   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(SYSUT1) DA('"MODLIB_Dsn"') SHR REUSE"
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(SYSIN)",
          "DA('SDPROD.TELON.R51.CAWLINST(CINPTPCH)') SHR REUSE"
   ADDRESS TSO,
    "ALLOC F(SYSUT2) DA('"CARDIN_Dsn"')",
           "LRECL(81) BLKSIZE(6156) SPACE(1,5)",
           "RECFM(F B A) CYLINDERS  ",
           "NEW CATALOG REUSE "     ;
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(SYSPRINT) DUMMY REUSE"

   ADDRESS LINK 'IEBPTPCH'
/*
   ADDRESS ISPEXEC "SELECT PGM(IEBPTPCH)"
*/

   IF RC > 4 THEN,
       Do
       Trace ?r
       Say "Could not Import the program" ENVELM
/*
       ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMINIT DATAID(DDID) DDNAME(SYSPRINT)"
       ADDRESS ISPEXEC "VIEW DATAID(&DDID)"
       ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMFREE DATAID(&DDID)"
*/
       EXIT(8)
       End

   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSUT1)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSUT2)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSIN)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSPRINT)"

   Return

Import_IMPORT_TELONTDF:

   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(CARDIN)   DA('"CARDIN_Dsn"') SHR REUSE"
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(INFILE)   DA('"CTLCRDS_Dsn"') SHR REUSE"
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(INPARMS)  DA('"RUNPRMS_Dsn"') SHR REUSE"
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(SYSOUT)   DA(*) REUSE "
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(SYSUDUMP) DA(*) REUSE "
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(SYSDBOUT) DA(*) REUSE "
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(MESSAGES) DA(*) REUSE "
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(TNCCIMSG)",
          "LRECL(210) SPACE(1,5)",
          "BLKSIZE(21000)",
          "RECFM(F B) CYLINDERS",
          "NEW UNCATALOG REUSE "     ;
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(SYSPRINT) DA(*) REUSE"
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(TLEXIMIN) DUMMY REUSE"
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(TNSYSLIB)",
          "DA('SDPROD.TELON.R51.CAWLLOAD') SHR REUSE"
   ADDRESS TSO "ALLOC F(TLTRACE)  DA(*) REUSE"
   ADDRESS TSO
      "ALLOC F(TNTCCL) DA('"VSQUAL".TNTCCL') SHR REUSE"
      "ALLOC F(TNTDD)  DA('"VSQUAL".TNTDD') SHR REUSE"
      "ALLOC F(TNTDDW) DA('"VSQUAL".TNTDDW') SHR REUSE"
      "ALLOC F(TNTDX)  DA('"VSQUAL".TNTDX') SHR REUSE"
      "ALLOC F(TNTDXW) DA('"VSQUAL".TNTDXW') SHR REUSE"

   PARMS='ADPADLS/DLS,TNPCEXIM,TNFDMDL3,,,N'
   ADDRESS ISPEXEC "SELECT PGM(TELONTDF) PARM("PARMS")"

   IF RC > 0 THEN,
       Do
       Say "Could not Import the program" ENVELM
       ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMINIT DATAID(DDID) DDNAME(TNCCIMSG)"
       ADDRESS ISPEXEC "VIEW DATAID(&DDID)"
       ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMFREE DATAID(&DDID)"
       EXIT(8)
       End

   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(CARDIN) "
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(INFILE) "
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(INPARMS)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSOUT) "
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSUDUMP)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSDBOUT)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(MESSAGES)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(TNCCIMSG)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SYSPRINT)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(TLEXIMIN)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(TNSYSLIB)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(TNTCCL)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(TNTDD)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(TNTDDW)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(TNTDX)"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(TNTDXW)"

   Return

TelonLibraryAllocations:

 ADDRESS TSO
 "ALTLIB ACTIVATE APPLICATION(CLIST)",
      "DATASET(",
          "'W#E0.COMPILE.CLIST'",
          "'W#E0.TSOCLIB'",
          "'W#E0.COMPILE.COMPREXX'",
          "'YourHQL.ENDV.SYQ.ENDEVOR.EXEC'",
              ")"

  ADDRESS ISPEXEC
  "LIBDEF ISPPLIB DATASET ID(",
                   "'W#E0.COMPILE.PANELS'",
                   "'W#E0.COMPILE.HELP'",
          ") COND STACK"

  ADDRESS ISPEXEC
  "LIBDEF ISPMLIB DATASET ID(",
                   "'W#E0.COMPILE.MSGS'",
                   "'SYS3.CAENDV.Q.R15.CSIQMENU'",
          ") COND STACK"

  ADDRESS ISPEXEC
  "LIBDEF ISPSLIB DATASET ID(",
                   "'W#E0.COMPILE.SKELS'",
          ") COND STACK"

  ADDRESS ISPEXEC
  "LIBDEF ISPTLIB DATASET ID(",
                   "'W#E0.TSOTLIB'",
          ") COND STACK"

  ADDRESS TSO
  "ALLOCATE DD(TNSYSLIB) DA(",
                   "'SDPROD.TELON.R51.CAWLLOAD'",
                   "'SDPROD.TELON.R51.CAWLLOAD'",
                   " ) SHR REUSE"
  ADDRESS ISPEXEC
  "LIBDEF ISPLLIB DATASET ID(",
                   "'SDPROD.TELON.R51.CAWLLOAD'",
                   "'SDPROD.TELON.R51.CAWLLOAD'",
                   "'W#E0.COMPILE.PGMLIB'",
          ") COND STACK"

  ADDRESS TSO
  "ALLOCATE DD(TLGENLIB) LRECL(80) BLKSIZE(6160) SPACE(5,10)",
         "RECFM(F B) CYLINDERS ",
         "DSORG(PO) DIR(15)",
         "NEW UNCATALOG REUSE "     ;
  "ALLOCATE DD(CARDIN)  DUMMY SHR REUSE"
  "ALLOCATE DD(INFILE)  DUMMY SHR REUSE"
  "ALLOCATE DD(MESSAGES) DA(*) SHR REUSE"
  "ALLOCATE DD(SYSOUT)   DA(*) SHR REUSE"
  "ALLOCATE DD(SYSPRINT) DA(*) SHR REUSE"
  "ALLOCATE DD(SYSUDUMP) DUMMY SHR REUSE"
  "ALLOCATE DD(TLTRACE)  DA(*) SHR REUS"
  "ALLOCATE DD(TNDRVRLD) DA('SDPROD.TELON.R51.CAWLLOAD')  SHR REUSE"
  "ALLOCATE DD(TNHELP)  DA('SDPROD.CAITELON.R41M503.TNHELP') SHR REUSE"
  "ALLOCATE DD(TNHOLD)  DA('"VSQUAL".TNHOLD') SHR REUSE "
  "ALLOCATE DD(TNTCCL)   DA('"VSQUAL".TNTCCL')         SHR REUSE"
  "ALLOCATE DD(TNTDD)    DA('"VSQUAL".TNTDD')        SHR REUSE"
  "ALLOCATE DD(TNTDDW)   DA('"VSQUAL".TNTDDW') SHR REUSE"
  "ALLOCATE DD(TNTDF)    DA('"VSQUAL".TNTDF')        SHR REUSE"
  "ALLOCATE DD(TNTDFW)   DA('"VSQUAL".TNTDFW') SHR REUSE"
  "ALLOCATE DD(TNTDX)    DA('"VSQUAL".TNTDX')        SHR REUSE"
  "ALLOCATE DD(TNTDXW)   DA('"VSQUAL".TNTDXW') SHR REUSE"
  "ALLOCATE DD(TLSYSLIB) DA(",
           "'SDPROD.TELON.R51.CAWLLOAD'",
           "'SDPROD.TELON.R51.CAWLLOAD'",
                       " )  SHR REUSE"

  Return

EnterTelonDesignFacility:

 /* Execute the command to enter into the TDF       */
  ADDRESS ISPEXEC "SELECT CMD(TDFR51)  NEWAPPL(TLN) PASSLIB"
  TDF_RC  = RC ;

 Return;

TelonLibraryFrees:

/* Do not Free the TLGENLIB or TLEXIMIN  files         */
/* They must remain to be used for updating Endevor    */
/* "FREE DD(TLGENLIB)"                                 */
/* "FREE DD(TLEXIMIN)"                                 */
/* ENDIEIM1 will free them .                           */
   "FREE DD(TLSYSLIB)"
   "FREE DD(TLTRACE)"
   "FREE DD(TNDRVRLD)"
   "FREE DD(TNHELP)"
   "FREE DD(TNHOLD)"
   "FREE DD(TNSYSLIB)"
   "FREE DD(TNTCCL)"
   "FREE DD(TNTDD)"
   "FREE DD(TNTDDW)"
   "FREE DD(TNTDF)"
   "FREE DD(TNTDFW)"
   "FREE DD(TNTDX)"
   "FREE DD(TNTDXW)"
   "FREE DD(CARDIN)"
   "FREE DD(INFILE)"
   "FREE DD(MESSAGES)"
   "FREE DD(SYSOUT)  "
   "FREE DD(SYSPRINT)"
   "FREE DD(SYSUDUMP)"

  "ALTLIB DEACTIVATE APPLICATION(CLIST)"

   Return

ExportToPDS:

  /* Exporting - from TDF to a temporary PDS member  */

  WhereIam =  MVSVAR(SYSNAME)     ;
  IF WhereIam == 'BAMD'   ,
     WhereIam == 'CAMD' THEN
      FacilityNode = 'SYQ'
  ELSE
  IF WhereIam == 'NEA1'   ,
     WhereIam == 'NEB1' THEN
      FacilityNode = 'SYU'
  ELSE
  IF WhereIam == 'SYD9' THEN
      FacilityNode = 'SY9'
  Sa= "You are running on"  FacilityNode

  /* Fetch and examine Endevor OPTs to determine    */
  /*  whether the element is BATCH/ONL/Sub etc...  */
  OPT_DSN = ImportDatasetNamePrefix".OPT"
  OPT. = 0
  CALL Get_OPT_for_ENVELM;
/*
 Not done at Ford:
  IF TDF_RC > 0 THEN,
     DO
     CALL EDIT_OPT_ENVELM ;
     IF TDF_RC = 0 THEN,
        CALL ADD_OPT_ENVELM           ;
     END;

  IF TDF_RC > 0 & LINE > 0 then RETURN;
  IF TDF_RC > 0 then,
        DO
        CALL Get_OPT_for_ENVELM;
        IF TDF_RC > 0 THEN RETURN;
        END;
*/

 /* Default PGMTYPE to Batch. Options may override  */
  PGMTYPE = 'BATCH'
  If OPT.0 > 0 then,
     DO optn# = 1 TO OPT.0
        IF WORD(OPT.optn#,1) = "PGMTYPE"  ,
           WORD(OPT.optn#,1) = "PGMTYPE=" then,
           INTERPRET OPT.optn#;
     END; /* DO optn# = 1 TO OPT.0 */

  IF USERID()  = 'W#E094' THEN trace ?r ;
 /* Export from TDF into the Endevor element   */
  tdfheadr = Substr(ENVELM,1,2) ;       /* First 2 chars */
  tdfmem = tdfheadr  substr(ENVELM,5)   /* Last 4 chars */
  MEMBERtail = Substr(ENVELM,3,2)       /*  BP / IM / SR */
  If MEMBERtail = 'BP' then MEMBERtail = 'BD'
  If MEMBERtail = 'IM' then MEMBERtail = 'SD'
  If PGMTYPE = 'BATCH' then MEMBERtail = 'BD'

  env      = 'B'                        /* B / I */
  tlnfrmat = 'N'                        /* N / M */
  tlnims = 'I'

  If MEMBERtail = 'SD' then,
     Do
     env      = 'I'                        /* B / I */
     tlnfrmat = 'M'                        /* N / M */
     End;

  card1 = "X",
      MEMBERtail   ,
      COPIES(' ',7)   ,
      env,
      tlnfrmat,
      tlnims,
      "C",
      tdfmem

  /* TLEXIMIN  must contain the Export control card data for TDF */
  ADDRESS TSO
  "ALLOCATE DD(TLEXIMIN) LRECL(80) BLKSIZE(6160) SPACE(5,5)",
         "RECFM(F B) TRACKS ",
         "NEW UNCATALOG REUSE "     ;

  PUSH CARD1
  "EXECIO 1 DISKW TLEXIMIN ( FINIS"
/*                                                                    */
  ADDRESS TSO

  PARMS  ="ADPADLS/DLS,TNPCEXIM,TNFDMEXP,Y,10,N"
  ADDRESS ISPEXEC "SELECT PGM(TELONTDF) PARM("PARMS")"
  TELONTDF_RC = RC            ;

  IF TELONTDF_RC > 4 THEN,
      Do
      Trace ?r
      Say "Could not Export the program" ENVELM
      ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(TLGENLIB)"
/*
      ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMINIT DATAID(DDID) DDNAME(SYSPRINT)"
      ADDRESS ISPEXEC "VIEW DATAID(&DDID)"
      ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMFREE DATAID(&DDID)"
*/
      EXIT(8)
      End

  IF USERID()  = 'Z#E094'  THEN ADDRESS TSO "ISRDDN" ;
  IF TELONTDF_RC > 0 THEN EXIT

  Return

Get_OPT_for_ENVELM:

  IF USERID()  = 'W#E094' THEN trace ?r ;
  ADDRESS TSO,
  "ALLOCATE F(SYSIN) LRECL(80) BLKSIZE(1600) SPACE(1,1)",
        "RECFM(F B) TRACKS DSORG(PS) ",
            "NEW UNCATALOG REUSE "     ;

  /* Get SYSTEM OPT element */
  QUEUE "./  REPRO NEW=PS,NAME="ENVBSYS

  ADDRESS TSO,
  "EXECIO 1 DISKW SYSIN (FINIS" ;

  ADDRESS TSO,
  "ALLOCATE DD(SYSPRINT) DUMMY REUSE"

  ADDRESS TSO,
  "ALLOCATE DD(SYSUT1) REUSE SHR DA(",
       "'YourHQL.ENDV."FacilityNode".Test.OPT' ",
       "'YourHQL.ENDV."FacilityNode".Prod.OPT' ",
       "'YourHQL.ENDV."FacilityNode"."ENVBENV"."ENVBSYS"."ENVBSBS".OPT' ",
       "'YourHQL.ENDV."FacilityNode".PROD."ENVBSYS".OPT' ",
                                       " )" ;
  ADDRESS ISPEXEC
     "VGET (ZSCREEN) SHARED"

  ADDRESS TSO,
  "ALLOCATE LRECL(80) BLKSIZE(16000) SPACE(5,5)",
        "DA('"OPT_DSN"') ",
        "RECFM(F B) TRACKS DSORG(PS) ",
            "NEW CATALOG REUSE "     ;
  ADDRESS TSO,
  "ALLOCATE F(SYSUT2) DA('"OPT_DSN"') SHR REUSE"

  ADDRESS LINK "IEBUPDTE";
  TDF_RC = RC;

  ADDRESS TSO,
  "ALLOCATE F(SYSUT2) LRECL(80) BLKSIZE(16000) SPACE(5,5)",
        "DA('"OPT_DSN"') ",
        "RECFM(F B) TRACKS DSORG(PS) ",
            "MOD CATALOG REUSE "     ;

  ADDRESS TSO "FREE DD(SYSIN) " ;
  ADDRESS TSO,
  "ALLOCATE F(SYSIN) LRECL(80) BLKSIZE(1600) SPACE(1,1)",
        "RECFM(F B) TRACKS DSORG(PS) ",
            "NEW UNCATALOG REUSE "     ;
  /* Get OPT element for the TDF element */
  QUEUE "./  REPRO NEW=PS,NAME="ENVELM
  ADDRESS TSO,
  "EXECIO 1 DISKW SYSIN (FINIS" ;

  ADDRESS LINK "IEBUPDTE";
  TEMP_RC = RC;
  TDF_RC = MIN(TDF_RC,TEMP_RC) ;

  IF TDF_RC = 0 THEN,
     ADDRESS TSO "EXECIO * DISKR SYSUT2 (STEM OPT. FINIS" ;

  ADDRESS TSO "FREE DD(SYSPRINT) " ;
  ADDRESS TSO "FREE DD(SYSIN) " ;
  ADDRESS TSO "FREE DD(SYSUT1) " ;
  ADDRESS TSO "FREE DD(SYSUT2) "

  return;

EDIT_OPT_ENVELM:
  Return

  ADDRESS TSO,
  "ALLOCATE F(OPT) LRECL(80) BLKSIZE(1600) SPACE(1,1)",
        "DA('"OPT_DSN"') ",
        "RECFM(F B) TRACKS DSORG(PS) ",
            "NEW UNCATALOG REUSE "     ;

  ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMINIT DATAID(TOPT) DDNAME(OPT) " ;
  ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMOPEN DATAID("TOPT") OPTION(INPUT) " ;
  LMOPEN_RC = RC ;
  ADDRESS ISPEXEC "ISPEXEC EDIT DATAID("TOPT") ",
                  "MACRO(ENDIEIM3)"
  TDF_RC = RC ;
  ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMCLOSE DATAID("TOPT") ";

  RETURN

ADD_OPT_ENVELM:
  Return

  EEVGENS1 = " SET FROM FILE 'OPT' .";
  EEVGENS2 = " SET TO ENVIRONMENT "ENVBENV" SYSTEM " ENVBSYS
  EEVGENS3 = "    SUBSYSTEM " ENVBSBS " TYPE OPT . "
  EEVGENS4 = " SET OPTIONS CCID " ENVCCID
  EEVGENS5 = "    COMMENT '"ENVCOM"'  ."
  EEVGENS6 = " ADD ENVELM "ENVELM   " ."

  VNBDD20  = "//OPT DD DISP=(OLD,DELETE),DSN="OPT_DSN
  EEVINJCL = Y
  VNBDD01  = ""
  VNBDD02  = ""
  VNBDD03  = ""
  VNBDD04  = ""
  VNBDD05  = ""
  VNBDD06  = ""
  VNBDD07  = ""
  VNBDD08  = ""
  VNBDD09  = ""
  VNBDD10  = ""
  VNBDD11  = ""
  VNBDD12  = ""
  VNBDD13  = ""
  VNBDD14  = ""
  VNBDD15  = ""
  VNBDD16  = ""
  VNBDD17  = ""
  VNBDD18  = ""
  VNBDD19  = ""
/*                                                                   */
/*  BUILD ENDEVOR JOBSTREAM FOR DOING ADD FOR OPT                    */
/*                                                                   */
/*    SYSI.NDVR70.ISPSLIB(ENDES000)                                  */
/*                                                                   */
  ADDRESS ISPEXEC "FTOPEN TEMP"
  ADDRESS ISPEXEC "FTINCL ENDES000"

  ADDRESS ISPEXEC "FTCLOSE " ;
  ADDRESS ISPEXEC "VGET (ZUSER ZTEMPF ZTEMPN) ASIS" ;

  DEBUG = 'YES'     ;
  DEBUG = 'NO'      ;
  IF DEBUG = 'YES' THEN,
     DO
     ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMINIT DATAID(DDID) DDNAME(&ZTEMPN)"
     ADDRESS ISPEXEC "EDIT DATAID(&DDID)"
     ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMFREE DATAID(&DDID)"
     END;
  ELSE,
     ADDRESS TSO "SUBMIT '"ZTEMPF"'" ;


  ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(OPT)"

  line = COPIES("*",04) COPIES(" ",64) COPIES("*",04)
  TEXT = "A OPT is created. Now edit the program source."
  TEXT = "A job to Add the OPT is submitted.",
         "Now edit the program source."
  line = overlay(text,line,6) ;
     'ISREDIT  LINE_AFTER .ZF   = INFOLINE "'line'"' ;

  return;

ADD_OPT_ENVELM_FOREGROUND:

/*                                                                  */
/*   ENDEVOR ADD FOR OPT IN FOREGROUND (NOT USED)                   */
/*                                                                  */

  ADDRESS TSO,
  "ALLOC F(SCLIN) BLKSIZE(8000) ",
     "TRACKS LRECL(80) SPACE(5 5)",
     "RECFM(F B) NEW REUSE UNCATALOG" ;

  ADDRESS TSO,
    "ALLOC F(MSGOUT1) DUMMY SHR REUSE"
  ADDRESS TSO,
    "ALLOC F(MSGOUT2) DUMMY SHR REUSE"
  ADDRESS TSO,
    "ALLOC F(SYSOUT)  DUMMY SHR REUSE"

  QUEUE " SET FROM FILE 'OPT' .";
  QUEUE ' SET TO ENVIRONMENT 'ENVBENV' SYSTEM ' ENVBSYS
  QUEUE '    SUBSYSTEM ' ENVBSBS ' TYPE OPT . '
  QUEUE ' SET OPTIONS CCID ' ENVCCID
  QUEUE "    COMMENT '"ENVCOM"'  ."
  QUEUE " ADD ENVELM "ENVELM   " ."
/*                                                                  */

  ZEDSMSG = "SAVING OPT ENVELM"
  ZEDLMSG = "OPT ENVELM BEING ADDED TO ENDEVOR"
  ADDRESS ISPEXEC "SETMSG MSG(ISRZ001)"

  ADDRESS TSO "EXECIO 6 DISKW SCLIN (FINIS" ;
  IF USERID()  = 'XXXXXXZ' THEN,
     ADDRESS TSO "ISRDDN"



  ADDRESS ISPEXEC,
  "SELECT PGM(C1BM3000) ",
     "PARM(SCLIN,MSGOUT1,,MSGOUT2) "


  ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(MSGOUT1)"
  ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(MSGOUT2)"
  ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(SCLIN)"
/*                                                                  */
/*   END ENDEVOR ADD FOR OPT                                        */
/*                                                                  */

  ADDRESS TSO "FREE F(OPT)"

  line = COPIES("*",04) COPIES(" ",64) COPIES("*",04)
  TEXT = "A OPT is created. Now edit the program source."
  line = overlay(text,line,9) ;
     'ISREDIT  LINE_AFTER .ZF   = INFOLINE "'line'"' ;

  return;

EXIT 0
