./  ADD  NAME=ENDLCONV
/* REXX */
/*======================================================*/
/*===  name   : ENDLCONV                             ===*/
/*===  purpose: I am an edit macro to be used when   ===*/
/*===           converting an application(s) from    ===*/
/*===     LMS / Librarian to endevor                 ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*===           I create a A2CNV file and allow      ===*/
/*===           user to enter the apps to convert    ===*/
/*===           I validate the apps that are entered ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*===           I replace uncommented ENODE=oldvalue ===*/
/*===           with endevor node (ie A,B,C,1,9...)  ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*===           I replace uncommented DSFX=oldvalue  ===*/
/*===           with current date suffix             ===*/
/*===           All "output" datasets should be      ===*/
/*===           suffixed sith the datetime suffix    ===*/
/*===           to ensure that we have a history     ===*/
/*===           of what was done                     ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*===  parms  : admin sfx  P/T/D  P=default          ===*/
/*===           debug flag Y/N    N=default          ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*======================================================*/

/* 2014.04.29 Stefan - Added ALLOC of TCOBD         ===*/

address "ISREDIT" "MACRO (ADMIN DEBUG REDO INPFX) PROCESS"
address "ISPEXEC" "CONTROL ERRORS RETURN"

q# = QUEUED()
if q# > 0 then,
   Do
   Say 'QUEUED()=' QUEUED()
   Call DANPULL
   End

upper ADMIN
admin = strip(ADMIN)
if admin<>"T" & admin<>"D" then admin="P"

redo_me=0

upper DEBUG
debug = strip(DEBUG)
if debug = "" then debug = "N"
if debug = "Y" then trace r

upper REDO
REDO=strip(REDO)
if REDO="Y" then redo_me=1

upper INPFX
INPFX=strip(INPFX)

zmsg000l =""
my_rc    =0
error_rc =8

if length(INPFX)>10 then do
   zmsg000l="dataset prefix longer than 10 bytes: "INPFX
   address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
   return error_rc
end

found_cnt=0
done     =0
the_dd   ="ENDVCVDD"
the_tdd  ="ENDVCV"
pfx      ="YourHQL.ENDV.SY"
epfx     =pfx
if INPFX<>"" then pfx=INPFX               /* allow for dset pfx      */
                                          /* override but discourage */
middle   ="CV"
tailApps ="APPS"
tailArea ="AREA"
editmacroApps="ENDLCONM"
editmacroArea="ENDLCONR"
AppsHdr  ="*Appl2Conv"

d=date("O")                               /* set dte= new DSFX= value*/
t=time()
parse var d yy"/"mm"/"dd .
parse var t hh":"mi":"ss .
dte="D"  substr(yy,2,1)  mm  dd  ".T"  hh  mi
ADDRESS ISREDIT "CHANGE 'D?????.T????' '"dte"' all "

enode=getenode(debug)                       /* set endevor node*/
ADDRESS ISREDIT "CHANGE 'SY?' 'SY"enode"' all "
ADDRESS ISREDIT "CHANGE 'E?' '"enode"' all "
if strip(enode)="" then do
   zmsg000l="getenode("  debug  ") returned null string"
   address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
   return error_rc
end

fac=getfac(debug)                           /* set facility*/
if strip(fac)="" then do
   zmsg000l="getfac("  debug  ") returned null string"
   address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
   return error_rc
end

ppfx=pfx  enode  "."  middle
epfx     =epfx  enode
vpfx     =epfx  "."  middle  ".ENDEVOR"
ppfxa=pfx  "A."  middle
AppsDsn=ppfx  "."  dte  "."  tailApps
AreaDsn=ppfx  "."  dte  "."  tailArea
JCLdsn =ppfx  "."  dte  ".JCL"
CONVdsn =ppfx  "."  dte  ".CONVSFX"
cmncmpnt="YourHQL.CHGMAN.DP.CMN"  enode  ".CMNCMPNT.V5"
cmnpmast="YourHQL.CHGMAN.DP.CMN"  enode  ".CMNPMAST.V5"
if enode="1" then do
   cmncmpnt="YourHQL.CHGMAN.P.CMNF.CMNCMPNT.V5"
   cmnpmast="YourHQL.CHGMAN.P.CMNF.CMNPMAST.V5"
end

try_netrc=" "userid()  ".HOLD.TCPIP.NETRC "  ,
          " "userid()  ".TCPIP.NETRC "  ,
          " "userid()  ".NETRC "
found_netrc=0
searched_in=""
do kk=1 to words(try_netrc) while \found_netrc
   netrc=word(try_netrc,kk)
   tempds="'"  netrc  "'"
   searched_in=searched_in  " "  tempds
   if sysdsn(tempds) = "OK" then found_netrc=1
end
if \found_netrc then do
   zmsg000l="Unable to find NETRC dataset, please allocate. "  ,
             "Searched:"searched_in
   address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
   return error_rc
end

try_admin=" D T P "
searched_in=""
if admin="T" then try_admin=" T P "
if admin="P" then try_admin=" P "
APPTBLpfx="YourHQL.ENDV.SY"
APPTBLsfx=".TABLES(APPMASTR)"
found_admin=0
do kk=1 to words(try_admin) while \found_admin
   APPTBLmid=".ADMIN"  word(try_admin,kk)
   tempds="'"  APPTBLpfx  enode  APPTBLmid  APPTBLsfx  "'"
   searched_in=searched_in  " "  tempds
   if sysdsn(tempds) = "OK" then found_admin=1
end
if \found_admin then do
   zmsg000l="Unable to find APPMASTR in ADMIN TABLES, searched "  ,
             searched_in
   address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
   return error_rc
end

APPTBL =APPTBLpfx  enode  APPTBLmid  APPTBLsfx


APPTBLsfx=".TABLES(ENVMASTR)"
found_admin=0
searched_in=""
do kk=1 to words(try_admin) while \found_admin
   APPTBLmid=".ADMIN"  word(try_admin,kk)
   tempds="'"  APPTBLpfx  enode  APPTBLmid  APPTBLsfx  "'"
   searched_in=searched_in  " "  tempds
   if sysdsn(tempds) = "OK" then found_admin=1
end
if \found_admin then do
   zmsg000l="Unable to find ENVMASTR in ADMIN TABLES, searched "  ,
             searched_in
   address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
   return error_rc
end
ENVTBL =APPTBLpfx  enode  APPTBLmid  APPTBLsfx

APPTBLsfx=".TABLES(TYPMASTR)"
found_admin=0
searched_in=""
do kk=1 to words(try_admin) while \found_admin
   APPTBLmid=".ADMIN"  word(try_admin,kk)
   tempds="'"  APPTBLpfx  enode  APPTBLmid  APPTBLsfx  "'"
   searched_in=searched_in  " "  tempds
   if sysdsn(tempds) = "OK" then found_admin=1
end
if \found_admin then do
   zmsg000l="Unable to find TYPMASTR in ADMIN TABLES, searched "  ,
             searched_in
   address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
   return error_rc
end
TYPTBL =APPTBLpfx  enode  APPTBLmid  APPTBLsfx

APPTBLsfx=".TABLES(ALCOTHER)"
found_admin=0
searched_in=""
do kk=1 to words(try_admin) while \found_admin
   APPTBLmid=".ADMIN"  word(try_admin,kk)
   tempds="'"  APPTBLpfx  enode  APPTBLmid  APPTBLsfx  "'"
   searched_in=searched_in  " "  tempds
   if sysdsn(tempds) = "OK" then found_admin=1
end
if \found_admin then do
   zmsg000l="Unable to find ALCOTHER in ADMIN TABLES, searched "  ,
             searched_in
   address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
   return error_rc
end
ALCOTHER =APPTBLpfx  enode  APPTBLmid  APPTBLsfx

APPTBLsfx=".TABLES(ALCMASTR)"
found_admin=0
searched_in=""
do kk=1 to words(try_admin) while \found_admin
   APPTBLmid=".ADMIN"  word(try_admin,kk)
   tempds="'"  APPTBLpfx  enode  APPTBLmid  APPTBLsfx  "'"
   searched_in=searched_in  " "  tempds
   if sysdsn(tempds) = "OK" then found_admin=1
end
if \found_admin then do
   zmsg000l="Unable to find ALCMASTR in ADMIN TABLES, searched "  ,
             searched_in
   address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
   return error_rc
end
ALCTBL =APPTBLpfx  enode  APPTBLmid  APPTBLsfx

APPTBLsfx=".TABLES(LMSTOEND)"
found_admin=0
searched_in=""
do kk=1 to words(try_admin) while \found_admin
   APPTBLmid=".ADMIN"  word(try_admin,kk)
   tempds="'"  APPTBLpfx  enode  APPTBLmid  APPTBLsfx  "'"
   searched_in=searched_in  " "  tempds
   if sysdsn(tempds) = "OK" then found_admin=1
end
if \found_admin then do
   zmsg000l="Unable to find ALCMASTR in ADMIN TABLES, searched "  ,
             searched_in
   address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
   return error_rc
end
LMSTOEND=APPTBLpfx  enode  APPTBLmid  APPTBLsfx

APPTBLsfx=".TABLES(OVERRIDE)"
found_admin=0
searched_in=""
do kk=1 to words(try_admin) while \found_admin
   APPTBLmid=".ADMIN"  word(try_admin,kk)
   tempds="'"  APPTBLpfx  enode  APPTBLmid  APPTBLsfx  "'"
   searched_in=searched_in  " "  tempds
   if sysdsn(tempds) = "OK" then found_admin=1
end
if \found_admin then do
   zmsg000l="Unable to find ALCMASTR in ADMIN TABLES, searched "  ,
             searched_in
   address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
   return error_rc
end
OVERRIDE=APPTBLpfx  enode  APPTBLmid  APPTBLsfx

APPTBLsfx=".TABLES(TYPWACK)"
found_admin=0
searched_in=""
do kk=1 to words(try_admin) while \found_admin
   APPTBLmid=".ADMIN"  word(try_admin,kk)
   tempds="'"  APPTBLpfx  enode  APPTBLmid  APPTBLsfx  "'"
   searched_in=searched_in  " "  tempds
   if sysdsn(tempds) = "OK" then found_admin=1
end
if \found_admin then do
   zmsg000l="Unable to find TYPWACK in ADMIN TABLES, searched "  ,
             searched_in
   address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
   return error_rc
end
TYPWACK=APPTBLpfx  enode  APPTBLmid  APPTBLsfx

REXX1  =APPTBLpfx  enode  ".Prod.REX"
REXX2  =APPTBLpfx  enode  ".Prod.REX"
REXX3  =APPTBLpfx  enode  ".Prod.REX"
REXX1A =APPTBLpfx  "A.Prod.REX"
REXX2A =APPTBLpfx  "A.Prod.REX"
REXX3A =APPTBLpfx  "A.Prod.REX"
if admin="D" then do
   REXX1  =APPTBLpfx  enode  ".ADMIND.REX"
   REXX2  =APPTBLpfx  enode  ".Test.REX"
   REXX1A =APPTBLpfx  "A.ADMIND.REX"
   REXX2A =APPTBLpfx  "A.Test.REX"
end
if admin="T" then do
   REXX1  =APPTBLpfx  enode  ".Test.REX"
   REXX2  =APPTBLpfx  enode  ".Test.REX"
   REXX1A =APPTBLpfx  "A.Test.REX"
   REXX2A =APPTBLpfx  "A.Test.REX"
end

CONVSFX.1="OPT"                           /* dataset suffixes that   */
CONVSFX.2="SPPARM"                        /* need further processing */
CONVSFX.3="FNPARM"                        /* we write these out to a */
CONVSFX.4="SQLPL"                         /* dataset, other steps    */
CONVSFX.0=4                               /* in conversion will read */

MyArea=do_Area_Alloc()                    /* ask user for Area       */
if MyArea='x' then Exit(8)                /* If user canceled edit  */
zmsg=AreaDsn  " created.  "
ADDRESS ISREDIT "CHANGE 'A?' '"MyArea"' all "

my_rc=do_appl_ds(the_dd)                  /* ask user for appls 2    */
if my_rc<>0 then return my_rc             /* convert                 */
zmsg=AppsDsn  " created.  "

if my_rc<=4 then my_rc=do_allocs(the_tdd) /* create other datasets   */
if my_rc<>0 then return my_rc             /* for conversion process  */
zmsg=zmsg  "  "  ppfx  "."  dte  ".** datasets created.  "


REPL.1="ENODE="
REPL.1.VALUE=enode
REPL.2="DSFX="
REPL.2.VALUE=dte
REPL.3="DPFX="
REPL.3.VALUE=ppfx
REPL.4="REXX1="
REPL.4.VALUE=REXX1
REPL.5="REXX2="
REPL.5.VALUE=REXX2
REPL.6="REXX3="
REPL.6.VALUE=REXX3
REPL.7="ITMS="
REPL.7.VALUE=APPTBL
REPL.8="ADMIN="
REPL.8.VALUE=admin
REPL.9="EPFX="
REPL.9.VALUE=epfx
REPL.10="NETRC="
REPL.10.VALUE=netrc
REPL.11="CMNCMPNT="
REPL.11.VALUE=cmncmpnt
REPL.12="CMNPMAST="
REPL.12.VALUE=cmnpmast
REPL.13="FAC="
REPL.13.VALUE=fac
REPL.14="VPFX="
REPL.14.VALUE=vpfx
REPL.15="$USER$$"
REPL.15.VALUE=userid()
REPL.16="$LP$"
REPL.16.VALUE=getlpar()
REPL.17="ENVTBL="
REPL.17.VALUE=ENVTBL
REPL.18="ALCTBL="
REPL.18.VALUE=ALCTBL
REPL.19="TYPTBL="
REPL.19.VALUE=TYPTBL
REPL.20="LMSTOEND="
REPL.20.VALUE=LMSTOEND
REPL.21="OVERRIDE="
REPL.21.VALUE=OVERRIDE
REPL.22="TYPWACK="
REPL.22.VALUE=TYPWACK
REPL.23="ALCOTHER="
REPL.23.VALUE=ALCOTHER
REPL.24="$USER###"
REPL.24.VALUE=userid()  fac
REPL.25="REXX1A="
REPL.25.VALUE=REXX1A
REPL.26="REXX2A="
REPL.26.VALUE=REXX2A
REPL.27="REXX3A="
REPL.27.VALUE=REXX3A
REPL.28="DPFXA="
REPL.28.VALUE=ppfxa
REPL.29="AREA="
REPL.29.VALUE=area
REPL.0=29
                                          /* input decks do not like */
                                          /* numbers                 */
address "ISREDIT" "NUM ON"
address "ISREDIT" "UNNUM"
                                          /* loop finding and        */
                                          /* replacing old value     */
                                          /* with new value          */

                                          /* loop finding and        */
                                          /* replacing old value     */
                                          /* with new value          */
do rr=1 to REPL.0 while my_rc=0
   done     =0
   found_cnt=0
   fstring  ="FIND FIRST '"  REPL.rr  "'"
   nstring  ="FIND NEXT '"  REPL.rr  "'"
   fmsg.rr  =""
   fmsg.0=rr
   do while my_rc=0 & \done
      address "ISREDIT" fstring
      select
         when rc=4 & found_cnt=0 then do
            fmsg.rr=REPL.rr  " not found in JCL RC="  ,
                     rc
            my_rc=4
         end
         when rc=4 & found_cnt<>0 then do
            fmsg.rr=REPL.rr  " "  ,
                     found_cnt  " times"
            done=1
         end
         when rc>4 then do
            fmsg.rr="ISPF error RC="  rc
            my_rc=rc
         end
         otherwise nop
      end
      fstring=nstring

      found=0
      do while my_rc=0 & \found & \done
         address "ISREDIT" "(L1) = CURSOR"
         address "ISREDIT" "(D1) = LINE &L1"
         if substr(d1,1,3)="//*" & REPL.rr<>"$LP$" then found=1
         do kk=1 to words(d1) while \found
            w=word(d1,kk)
            if pos(REPL.rr,w)<>1 & (REPL.rr<>"$USER$$" & ,
                                    REPL.rr<>"$USER###" & ,
                                    REPL.rr<>"$LP$") then iterate
            found=1
            cstr="C '"  w  "' '"  REPL.rr  REPL.rr.VALUE  "'"
            if pos(REPL.rr,w)<>1 & (REPL.rr="$USER$$"   ,
                                    REPL.rr="$USER###"   ,
                                    REPL.rr="$LP$" )  then ,
               cstr="C '"REPL.rr"' '"  REPL.rr.VALUE  "'"
            address "ISREDIT" cstr
            if rc=0 then found_cnt=found_cnt+1
            else do
               my_rc=rc
               fcnt=found_cnt+1
               fmsg.rr="Error on replace of "  REPL.rr  ,
                       " occurrence #"  fcnt
            end
         end
      end
   end
   if fmsg.rr<>"" & my_rc > 4 then  do
      zmsg000l=fmsg.rr  ".  "
      address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
      zmsg000l=""
      return my_rc
   end
end

zmsg000l=zmsg000l  " Replaced "
do kk=1 to fmsg.0
   zmsg000l=zmsg000l  fmsg.kk  ". "
end
cparmc="REP '"  JCLdsn  "' .ZF .ZL"
address "ISREDIT" cparmc
hold_rc=rc
if hold_rc>4 then do
   cmsg=cparmc  " failed with RC= "  hold_rc  "."
end
else cmsg="  This JCL saved at "  JCLdsn  "."

zmsg000l=zmsg000l  zmsg  cmsg
address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
zmsg000l=""

return rc

/*-------*/
do_free:    procedure
/*-------*/
arg DD

x=OUTTRAP("msg.")
address "TSO" "FREE FI("DD")"
x=OUTTRAP(OFF)

return 0

/*-------*/
valid_app:  procedure expose APPTBL alist anums enode badnums itmsapp ,
                             error_txt error_cnt redo_me ,
                             curr_pquor curr_equor quor_app error_rc
/*-------*/
arg DD
                                  /* verify that the apps are in the*/
                                  /* master application list        */
                                  /* and are valid for this enode   */

VALA.0=0
vparm.1="ALLOC FILE("  DD  ") DSN('"APPTBL"') SHR REUSE"
vparm.2="EXECIO * DISKR "  DD  " (STEM VALA. FINIS "
vparm.0=2
badnums=" "

do kk=1 to vparm.0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" vparm.kk
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      zmsg000l="ERROR RC="  io_rc  " for "  vparm.kk
      say zmsg000l
      error_txt=zmsg000l
      error_cnt=error_cnt+1
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say omsg.i
      end
      xrc=do_free(DD)
      address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
      return error_rc
   end
end

x=OUTTRAP("msg.")
address "TSO" "FREE FI("DD")"
x=OUTTRAP(OFF)

descfpos=pos(' SysDescription',VALA.1)
if descfpos=0 then do
   zmsg000l="SysDescription AppsHdr column missing in "APPTBL
   say zmsg000l
   error_txt=zmsg000l
   error_cnt=error_cnt+1
   address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
   return error_rc
end
else do
  descfpos=descfpos+1
  descfend=descfpos
end
ll=length(VALA.1)
done=0
do kk=descfpos to ll while \done
   if substr(VALA.1,kk,1)<>" " then descfend=descfend+1
                               else done=1
end
descflen=descfend-descfpos+1

whichfpos=pos(' WhichFacilities',VALA.1)
if whichfpos=0 then do
   zmsg000l="WhichFacilities AppsHdr column missing in "APPTBL
   say zmsg000l
   error_txt=zmsg000l
   error_cnt=error_cnt+1
   address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
   return error_rc
end
else do
  whichfpos=whichfpos+1
  whichfend=whichfpos
end
ll=length(VALA.1)
done=0
do kk=whichfpos to ll while \done
   if substr(VALA.1,kk,1)<>" " then whichfend=whichfend+1
                               else done=1
end
whichflen=whichfend-whichfpos+1

pconvertedfpos=pos(' ConvertDate',VALA.1)
if pconvertedfpos=0 then do
   zmsg000l="ConvertDate AppsHdr column missing in "APPTBL
   say zmsg000l
   error_txt=zmsg000l
   error_cnt=error_cnt+1
   address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
   return error_rc
end
else do
  pconvertedfpos=pconvertedfpos+1
  pconvertedfend=pconvertedfpos
end
ll=length(VALA.1)
done=0
do kk=pconvertedfpos to ll while \done
   if substr(VALA.1,kk,1)<>" " then pconvertedfend=pconvertedfend+1
                               else done=1
end
pconvertedflen=pconvertedfend-pconvertedfpos+1

pquorfpos=pos(' ProdQuorum',VALA.1)
if pquorfpos=0 then do
   zmsg000l="ProdQuorum AppsHdr column missing in "APPTBL
   say zmsg000l
   error_txt=zmsg000l
   error_cnt=error_cnt+1
   address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
   return error_rc
end
else do
  pquorfpos=pquorfpos+1
  pquorfend=pquorfpos
end
ll=length(VALA.1)
done=0
do kk=pquorfpos to ll while \done
   if substr(VALA.1,kk,1)<>" " then pquorfend=pquorfend+1
                               else done=1
end
pquorflen=pquorfend-pquorfpos+1


equorfpos=pos(' EmerQuorum',VALA.1)
if equorfpos=0 then do
   zmsg000l="EmerQuorum AppsHdr column missing in "APPTBL
   say zmsg000l
   error_txt=zmsg000l
   error_cnt=error_cnt+1
   address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
   return error_rc
end
else do
  equorfpos=equorfpos+1
  equorfend=equorfpos
end
ll=length(VALA.1)
done=0
do kk=equorfpos to ll while \done
   if substr(VALA.1,kk,1)<>" " then equorfend=equorfend+1
                               else done=1
end
equorflen=equorfend-equorfpos+1

done=0
needle=" "  enode  " "

do kk=2 to VALA.0 while \done
   if strip(VALA.kk)      ="" then iterate
   if substr(VALA.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   curr_app=word(VALA.kk,1)
   curr_fac=" "  substr(VALA.kk,whichfpos,whichflen)  " "
   curr_desc=substr(VALA.kk,descfpos,descflen)
   curr_itms=word(curr_desc,1)
   curr_cdate=substr(VALA.kk,pconvertedfpos,pconvertedflen)
   curr_pquor=substr(VALA.kk,pquorfpos,pquorflen)
   curr_equor=substr(VALA.kk,equorfpos,equorflen)
   quor_app=quor_app  " "  curr_app  "-"  strip(curr_pquor)  "-"  ,
                                     strip(curr_equor)
   if \datatype(curr_itms,'W') then do
      zmsg000l="ITMS# missing in APPMASTR for "  curr_app
      say zmsg000l
      error_txt=zmsg000l
      error_cnt=error_cnt+1
      address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
      return error_rc
   end
   np=pos(needle,curr_fac)
   skiprest=0
   do jj=words(alist) to 1 by -1 while \skiprest
      wapp=word(alist,jj)
      wnum=word(anums,jj)
      if wapp=curr_app then do
         if strip(curr_cdate)<>'-' & \redo_me  then do
            zmsg000l="Application "  ,
                     curr_app  " converted on "  curr_cdate
            say zmsg000l
            error_txt=zmsg000l
            error_cnt=error_cnt+1
            address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
            return error_rc
         end
         alist=delword(alist,jj,1)
         anums=delword(anums,jj,1)
         if np=0 then badnums=badnums  wnum  " "
         skiprest=1
         itmsapp=itmsapp  " "  curr_app  "-"  curr_itms
      end
   end
   if words(alist)=0 then done=1
end

if words(alist)<>0   words(badnums)<>0 then return 4
                                       else return 0


/*-------*/
do_appl_ds: procedure expose debug AppsDsn error_rc AppsHdr ,
                             editmacroApps ,
                             APPTBL the_tdd enode APPLS. itmsapp ,
                             quor_app redo_me
/*-------*/
arg DD

itmsapp=""
quor_app=""

qdsn="'"  APPTBL  "'"
qres =sysdsn(qdsn)
if qres <> "OK" then do
   zmsg000l="sysdsn("qdsn") returned "qres
   address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
   return error_rc
end


wparm="EXECIO 1 DISKW "  DD  " (FINIS "
rparm="EXECIO * DISKR "  DD  " (STEM APPLS. FINIS "
dparm="EXECIO * DISKW "  DD  " (STEM APPLS. FINIS "
aparm="ALLOC FILE("  DD  ") MOD CATALOG LRECL(80) SPACE(1,5) "  ,
      "UNIT(SYSDA) TRACKS RECFM( F B ) DSORG(PS) "  ,
      "DA('"AppsDsn"')"

done=0
quit=0

xrc=do_free(DD)

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
io_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
if io_rc > 4 then do
   zmsg000l="ERROR RC="  io_rc  " for "  aparm
   say zmsg000l
   do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
      say omsg.i
   end
   xrc=do_free(DD)
   address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
   return error_rc
end

AppsHdr_l=length(AppsHdr)
queue AppsHdr

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" wparm
io_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
if io_rc > 4 then do
   zmsg000l="ERROR RC="  io_rc  " for "  wparm
   say zmsg000l
   do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
      say omsg.i
   end
   xrc=do_free(DD)
   address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
   return error_rc
end

do while \done & \quit
   eparm="EDIT DATASET('"  AppsDsn  "') MACRO("  editmacroApps  ")"
   address "ISPEXEC" eparm
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      zmsg000l="ERROR RC="  io_rc  " for "  eparm
      say zmsg000l
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say omsg.i
      end
      xrc=do_free(DD)
      address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
      return error_rc
   end

   drop APPLS.
   APPLS.0=0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" rparm
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      zmsg000l="ERROR RC="  io_rc  " for "  rparm
      say zmsg000l
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say omsg.i
      end
      xrc=do_free(DD)
      address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
      return error_rc
   end

   alist=" "
   anums=" "
   acnt=0
   error_cnt=0
   error_hdr=0
   error_txt=""
   do kk=1 to APPLS.0 while \quit
      w=word(APPLS.kk,1)
      wl=length(w)
      a=strip(APPLS.kk,'T')
      if strip(a)="QUIT"   strip(a)="quit" then do
         quit=1
         iterate
      end
      l=length(a)
      if kk=1 then do
         if a<>AppsHdr then do
            error_txt=error_txt  "Header line reset. "
            error_hdr=error_hdr+1
            APPLS.kk=AppsHdr
         end
         iterate
      end
      if strip(a)="" then iterate
      if substr(a,1,1)="*" then iterate
      needle=" "  strip(a)  " "
      needlep=pos(needle,alist)
      pp="#"
      if words(a)>1   wl>8 then pp=">"
      if words(a)>1   wl>8   needlep<>0 then do
         if substr(a,1,1)=" " then APPLS.kk=pp  substr(a,2,l-1)
                              else APPLS.kk=pp  substr(a,1,l)
         if error_cnt=0 then ,
            error_txt=error_txt  "See >,# for Errors, lines:"
         error_cnt=error_cnt+1
         error_txt=error_txt  " "  kk
         iterate
      end
      alist=alist  strip(a)  " "
      anums=anums  kk  " "
      acnt=acnt+1
      APPLS.kk=" "  strip(a)
   end

   if \quit & words(alist)>0 then do
      xrc=valid_app(the_tdd)
      if xrc>4 then quit=1
      if xrc=4 then do
         do vv=1 to words(anums)
            ww=word(anums,vv)
            if vv=1 then ,
               error_txt=error_txt  ,
               "   Apps not in App Master are tagged with $, lines:"
            error_cnt=error_cnt+1
            error_txt=error_txt  " "  word(anums,vv)
            l=length(APPLS.ww)
            if substr(APPLS.ww,1,1)=" " ,
               then APPLS.ww="$"  substr(APPLS.ww,2,l-1)
               else APPLS.ww="$"  substr(strip(APPLS.ww,'T'),1,l-1)
         end
         do vv=1 to words(badnums)
            ww=word(badnums,vv)
            if vv=1 then ,
               error_txt=error_txt  ,
               "   Apps not on this facility per App Master are "  ,
               "tagged with @, lines:"
            error_cnt=error_cnt+1
            error_txt=error_txt  " "  word(badnums,vv)
            l=length(APPLS.ww)
            if substr(APPLS.ww,1,1)=" " ,
               then APPLS.ww="@"  substr(APPLS.ww,2,l-1)
               else APPLS.ww="@"  substr(strip(APPLS.ww,'T'),1,l-1)
         end
      end
   end

   if \quit & (error_cnt>0   error_hdr>0) then do
      x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
      address "TSO" dparm
      io_rc = RC
      x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
      if io_rc > 4 then do
         zmsg000l="ERROR RC="  io_rc  " for "  dparm
         say zmsg000l
         do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
            say omsg.i
         end
         xrc=do_free(DD)
         address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
         return error_rc
      end
      zmsg000l=error_txt
      address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
   end
   else done=1
end

xrc=do_free(DD)
                                          /* loop finding and        */
if quit then do
   if error_cnt=0 then do
      zmsg000l="Terminated per your request"
      address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
   end
   return error_rc
end

if acnt=0 then do
   zmsg000l="No applications were entered"
   address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
   return error_rc
end

return 0



/*-------*/
do_allocs:  procedure expose debug error_rc APPLS. ppfx dte itmsapp ,
                                   REXX1 REXX2 REXX3 quor_app ,
                                   JCLdsn CONVSFX. CONVdsn
/*-------*/
arg DD

my_rc=0
pfx=ppfx  "."  dte

   TDD=DD  kk

   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      zmsg000l="ERROR RC="  io_rc  " for "  bparm.kk
      say zmsg000l
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say omsg.i
      end
      address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
      return error_rc
   end
end

rexx_mbrs="ENDVCVSI ENDVCVSJ ENDVCVSK ENDVCVSL ENDVCVSN "  ,
          "ENDVMDDV ENDVMDDW ENDVMDDI ENDVMDAP ENDVMDDP "  ,
          "ENDVCVST ENDVMDDR ENDVMDAR ENDVMDSR ENDVCVSA "  ,
          "ENDVMDAU ENDVMDAW ENDVMDAX ENDVMDAZ ENDVMDAY "  ,
          "ENDVMDGR ENDVMDSB ENDVMDSY ENDVMDTY ENDVMDAL ENDVMDAV "

/*  These additional Rexx modules were changed to reference LMSTOEND
    instead of CMNTOEND
          ENDVTSGY ENDVTSHY ENDVTSIF ENDVTSL5 ENDVTSL6 ENDVTSMA ENDVTSXM
          ENDVTSXX
*/

rexx_allo=""
do kk=1 to words(rexx_mbrs)
   mb=word(rexx_mbrs,kk)
   use_rexx="'"  REXX1  "("  mb  ")'"
   qres =sysdsn(use_rexx)
   if qres <> "OK" then do
      use_rexx="'"  REXX2  "("  mb  ")'"
      qres =sysdsn(use_rexx)
      if qres <> "OK" then do
         use_rexx="'"  REXX3  "("  mb  ")'"
         qres =sysdsn(use_rexx)
      end
   end
   if qres <> "OK" then do
      zmsg000l="Unable to locate "  mb  " in REXX library"
      address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
      return error_rc
   end
   rexx_allo=rexx_allo  " "  use_rexx
end

a=0
d=0
do kk=1 to words(rexx_mbrs)
   mb=word(rexx_mbrs,kk)
   lb=word(rexx_allo,kk)
   a=a+1
   d=d+1
   s="IO"  d
   aparm.a="ALLOC FILE("  DD  d  ") SHR REUSE "  ,
              "DA("  lb  ")"
   a=a+1
   aparm.a="EXECIO * DISKR "  DD  d  " (FINIS STEM "  s  ". "
   a=a+1
   d=d+1
   aparm.a="ALLOC FILE("  DD  d  ") SHR REUSE "  ,
              "DA('"  pfx  ".CVINPUT("  mb  ")')"
   a=a+1
   aparm.a="EXECIO * DISKW "  DD  d  " (FINIS STEM "  s  ". "
end
aparm.0=a

do kk=1 to d
   TDD=DD  kk
   xrc=do_free(TDD)
end

           "DA('"  pfx  ".#"  ap  ".ADD2EN(DELETE)')"
   do kk=1 to aparm.0
      x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
      address "TSO" aparm.kk
      io_rc = RC
      x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
      if io_rc > 4 then do
         zmsg000l="ERROR RC="  io_rc  " for "  aparm.kk
         say zmsg000l
         do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
            say omsg.i
         end
         address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
         return error_rc
      end
   end
end

do kk=1 to 1
   TDD=DD  kk
   xrc=do_free(TDD)
end

AO.1=" DELETE APPROVER RELATION "
AO.3="   FROM ENVIRONMENT 'PROD'"
AO.5="        SUBSYSTEM '*'"
AO.6="        TYPE      '*'"
AO.7="        STAGE ID  '*'"
AO.8="   TYPE IS STANDARD"
AO.9 ="   ."
AO.10=" DELETE APPROVER RELATION "
AO.12="   FROM ENVIRONMENT 'PROD'"
AO.14="        SUBSYSTEM '*'"
AO.15="        TYPE      '*'"
AO.16="        STAGE ID  '*'"
AO.17="   TYPE IS EMERGENCY"
AO.18 ="   ."
AO.0=18
aparm.2="EXECIO "  AO.0  " DISKW "  DD  "1 (STEM AO. FINIS"
aparm.0=2
do jj=1 to APPLS.0 while my_rc=0
   if substr(APPLS.jj,1,1)="*" then iterate
   ap=word(APPLS.jj,1)
   do kk=1 to 1
      TDD=DD  kk
      xrc=do_free(TDD)
   end
   AO.2="   FOR APPROVER GROUP '"  ap  "LEAD'"
   AO.4="        SYSTEM '"  ap  "'"
   AO.11="   FOR APPROVER GROUP '"  ap  "EMER'"
   AO.13="        SYSTEM '"  ap  "'"
   aparm.1="ALLOC FILE("  DD  "1) SHR REUSE "  ,
           "DA('"  pfx  ".#"  ap  ".ADD2EN(DELAPPRV)')"
   do kk=1 to aparm.0
      x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
      address "TSO" aparm.kk
      io_rc = RC
      x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
      if io_rc > 4 then do
         zmsg000l="ERROR RC="  io_rc  " for "  aparm.kk
         say zmsg000l
         do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
            say omsg.i
         end
         address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
         return error_rc
      end
   end
end

do kk=1 to 1
   TDD=DD  kk
   xrc=do_free(TDD)
end
AO.0=28
aparm.2="EXECIO "  AO.0  " DISKW "  DD  "1 (STEM AO. FINIS"
aparm.0=2
hold_quor=translate(quor_app,' ','-')
do jj=1 to APPLS.0 while my_rc=0
   if substr(APPLS.jj,1,1)="*" then iterate
   ap=word(APPLS.jj,1)
   do kk=1 to 1
      TDD=DD  kk
      xrc=do_free(TDD)
   end
   wwp=wordpos(ap,hold_quor)
   pquor=word(hold_quor,wwp+1)
   equor=word(hold_quor,wwp+2)
   AO.1  ="DEFINE APPROVER GROUP "  ap  "EMER                "
   AO.2  ="    TO ENVIRONMENT PROD                           "
   AO.3  ="    TITLE 'Approver group for "  ap  " EMERGENCY' "
   AO.4  ="    QUORUM SIZE "  equor  "                      "
   AO.5  ="    .                                             "
   AO.6  ="DEFINE APPROVER GROUP "  ap  "LEAD                "
   AO.7  ="    TO ENVIRONMENT PROD                           "
   AO.8  ="    TITLE 'Approver group for "  ap  "LEAD'       "
   AO.9  ="    QUORUM SIZE "  pquor  "                      "
   AO.10 ="    .                                             "
   AO.11 ="DEFINE APPROVER RELATION                          "
   AO.12 ="    FOR APPROVER GROUP '"  ap  "EMER'             "
   AO.13 ="    TO ENVIRONMENT 'PROD'                         "
   AO.14 ="    SYSTEM '"  ap  "'                             "
   AO.15 ="    SUBSYSTEM '*'                                 "
   AO.16 ="    TYPE '*'                                      "
   AO.17 ="    STAGE ID *                                    "
   AO.18 ="    TYPE IS EMERGENCY                             "
   AO.19 ="    .                                             "
   AO.20 ="DEFINE APPROVER RELATION                          "
   AO.21 ="    FOR APPROVER GROUP '"  ap  "LEAD'             "
   AO.22 ="    TO ENVIRONMENT 'PROD'                         "
   AO.23 ="    SYSTEM '"  ap  "'                             "
   AO.24 ="    SUBSYSTEM '*'                                 "
   AO.25 ="    TYPE '*'                                      "
   AO.26 ="    STAGE ID *                                    "
   AO.27 ="    TYPE IS STANDARD                              "
   AO.28 ="    .                                             "
   aparm.1="ALLOC FILE("  DD  "1) SHR REUSE "  ,
           "DA('"  pfx  ".#"  ap  ".ADD2EN(DEFAPPRV)')"
   do kk=1 to aparm.0
      x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
      address "TSO" aparm.kk
      io_rc = RC
      x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
      if io_rc > 4 then do
         zmsg000l="ERROR RC="  io_rc  " for "  aparm.kk
         say zmsg000l
         do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
            say omsg.i
         end
         address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
         return error_rc
      end
   end
end

do kk=1 to 1
   TDD=DD  kk
   xrc=do_free(TDD)
end

return 0

do_Area_Alloc: procedure expose AreaDsn editmacroArea

/* Librarian master files exist for each of the ValidAreas  */
/* An example file is WA.LI.xSRCMST where x is one of the ValidArea */
ValidAreas = 'B C D E G H I J K L M N P Q S T U W X Y'
MyArea = ' '

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
"FREE FILE(AREAFILE)"
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)

"ALLOC FILE(AREAFILE) MOD CATALOG LRECL(80) SPACE(1,5) "  ,
      "UNIT(SYSDA) TRACKS RECFM( F B ) DSORG(PS) "  ,
      "DA('"AreaDsn"')"

do forever
   eparm="EDIT DATASET('"  AreaDsn  "') MACRO("  editmacroArea  ")"
   address "ISPEXEC" eparm
   io_rc = RC
   if io_rc > 0 then,
      Do
      zmsg000l="Terminated per your request"
      address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISPZ000)"
      Return('x')
   end
   message = ' '
   "EXECIO * DISKR AREAFILE (Stem area. finis"
   if area.0 > 2 then,
      message = 'Only one Area may be entered'
   MyArea = Word(area.2,1) ;
   If WordPos(MyArea,ValidAreas) = 0 then,
      message = 'Must enter one of the valid Areas:' ValidAreas
   If message /= ' ' then Push message
   If message = ' ' then Leave;
End

"FREE  FILE(AREAFILE)"

qed = QUEUED()
Do q# = 1 to qed
   Pull what
End

return MyArea

./  ADD  NAME=ENDVTSAB
/* REXX */
/*======================================================*/
/*===  name   : ENDVTSAB                             ===*/
/*===  purpose: used endevor conversion process      ===*/
/*===           to allocate BASE datasets            ===*/
/*===           ... originally written by giri ...   ===*/
/*===           ... modified to remove hardwired     ===*/
/*===               datasets  etc                    ===*/
/*===  parms  : DEBUG()   - debug flag Y/N N=deflt   ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*======================================================*/
parse upper arg my_parms
numeric digits 10
my_parms = " "  my_parms  " "    /* add spaces 4 parsing*/
my_rc = 0

                                       /* pull off debug parm */
                                       /* default is no debug */
                                       /* trace if debug=Y    */
parse var my_parms " DEBUG(" debug ")" .
my_item = "DEBUG("debug")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
debug = strip(debug)
if debug = "" then debug = "N"
if debug = "Y" then trace r
call do_init

if my_rc=0 then my_rc=do_work(the_WHAT)

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    "RC="my_rc

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_work: procedure expose my_name INP.
/*-------*/
arg action

my_rc=0
alloc_count = 0
already_present = 0
err_count = 0
/* For each DSN provided and the Others, Delete or Allocate          */
Do jj=1 to INP.0
   parse var INP.jj stuff "DSN('" dataset_name "')" rest
   if strip(dataset_name)="" then iterate

   xx=sysdsn("'"dataset_name"'")
   if xx='OK' & action='ALLOCATE' then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          'Dataset ' dataset_name ' was already allocated '
      already_present = already_present + 1
      iterate
   end

   if xx<>'OK' & action='DELETE' then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          'Dataset ' dataset_name ' not present '
      already_present = already_present + 1
      iterate
   end

   if action="DELETE" then do
      vparm.1="DELETE '"  dataset_name  "'"
      vparm.0=1
   end
   else do
      vparm.1="ALLOCATE "  INP.jj
      vparm.2="FREE DATASET('"  dataset_name  "')"
      vparm.0=2
   end

   do zz=1 to vparm.0
      x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
      address "TSO" vparm.zz
      io_rc = RC
      x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
      if io_rc > 4 then do
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "vparm.zz
         do ee= 1 to omsg.trapped
            say left(my_name,9),
                left(time("L"),16),
                omsg.ee
         end
         if zz=1 then do
            err_count = err_count + 1
            errds.err_count = dataset_name
            err_count.0 = err_count
         end
      end
      else do
         if zz=1 then alloc_count=alloc_count+1
      end
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          'Command Executed:' vparm.1
   end zz
end

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16)
if action="ALLOCATE" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       '* Allocated ' alloc_count ' datasets '
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       '* ' already_present ' Datasets were already allocated '
   If err_count > 0 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          '* Could not allocate the following' err_count.0 ' datasets'
       do j = 1 to err_count.0
          say left(my_name,9),
              left(time("L"),16),
              '          ' errds.j
       end
       my_rc=8
   end
end
else do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       '* Deleted ' alloc_count ' datasets '
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       '* ' already_present ' Datasets were not present '
   If err_count > 0 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          '* Could not delete the following' err_count.0 ' datasets'
       do j = 1 to err_count.0
          say left(my_name,9),
              left(time("L"),16),
              '          ' errds.j
       end
       my_rc=8
   end
end

return my_rc



/*------*/
do_init:
/*------*/

parse source w1 w2 w3 w4 w5 w6 w7 w8
my_name = w3

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'do_init: Begin'

error_rc=8
unknown_parms_rc=4

LIBS.0=0
the_APP_dflt        = ""
the_INDD_dflt       = "ESYMS"
the_ALCOTHER_dflt   = "ALCOTHER"
the_APPMASTR_dflt   = "APPMASTR"
the_DPFX_dflt       = ""
the_WHAT_dflt       = "ALLOCATE"
the_WHAT_values     = " ALLOCATE DELETE "


                                       /* pull off APP        */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " APP(" the_APP ")" .
my_item = "APP("the_APP")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_APP = strip(the_APP)
if the_APP = "" then the_APP = the_APP_dflt
if strip(the_APP) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Parm APP() required"
   my_rc=error_rc
end


                                       /* pull off DPFX       */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " DPFX(" the_DPFX ")" .
my_item = "DPFX("the_DPFX")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_DPFX = strip(the_DPFX)
if the_DPFX = "" then the_DPFX = the_DPFX_dflt
if strip(the_DPFX) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Parm DPFX() required"
   my_rc=error_rc
end


                                       /* pull off WHAT       */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " WHAT(" the_WHAT ")" .
my_item = "WHAT("the_WHAT")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_WHAT = strip(the_WHAT)
if the_WHAT = "" then the_WHAT = the_WHAT_dflt
if strip(the_WHAT) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Parm WHAT() required"
   my_rc=error_rc
end
else do
   x = " "  the_WHAT  " "
   if INDEX(the_WHAT_values,the_WHAT) = 0 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "Parm WHAT must be one of "the_WHAT_values
      my_rc = 8
   end
end

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Parm WHAT() =' "'"the_WHAT"'"

                                       /* pull off INDD       */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " INDD(" the_INDD ")" .
my_item = "INDD("the_INDD")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_INDD = strip(the_INDD)
if the_INDD = "" then the_INDD = the_INDD_dflt
if strip(the_INDD) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Parm INDD() required"
   my_rc=error_rc
end


                                       /* pull off ALCOTHER   */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " ALCOTHER(" the_ALCOTHER ")" .
my_item = "ALCOTHER("the_ALCOTHER")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_ALCOTHER = strip(the_ALCOTHER)
if the_ALCOTHER = "" then the_ALCOTHER = the_ALCOTHER_dflt
if strip(the_ALCOTHER) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Parm ALCOTHER() required"
   my_rc=error_rc
end


                                       /* pull off APPMASTR   */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " APPMASTR(" the_APPMASTR ")" .
my_item = "APPMASTR("the_APPMASTR")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_APPMASTR = strip(the_APPMASTR)
if the_APPMASTR = "" then the_APPMASTR = the_APPMASTR_dflt
if strip(the_APPMASTR) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Parm APPMASTR() required"
   my_rc=error_rc
end


                                       /* any garbage parms?  */
if strip(my_parms) <> "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Unrecognized parms ignored: "my_parms
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Valid parms are DEBUG() INDD() WHAT() APPMASTR() ALCOTHER()",
       " APP() DPFX()"
   my_rc=unknown_parms_rc
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc

aparm.1="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_INDD      " (STEM INX. FINIS "
aparm.2="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_APPMASTR  " (STEM APM. FINIS "
aparm.3="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_ALCOTHER  " (STEM ALC. FINIS "
aparm.0=3
do kk=1 to aparm.0 while my_rc=0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
      my_rc=error_rc
   end
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Read' INX.0 'records from' the_INDD
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Read' APM.0 'records from' the_APPMASTR
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Read' ALC.0 'records from' the_ALCOTHER

   Do i = 1 to ALC.0
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          '   ALC.'i '=' "'"Strip( ALC.i)"'"
   End i

cc=0
hold=""
do kk=1 to INX.0
   if strip(INX.kk)="." then do
      if hold<>"" then do
         cc=cc+1
         INP.cc=hold
         hold=""
      end
      iterate
   end
   hold=hold  " "  INX.kk
end

INP.0=cc
drop INX.

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'INDD Processed'
   Do i = 1 to INP.0
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          '   INP.'i '=' "'"INP.i"'"
   End i

descfpos=pos(' SysEnvironments',APM.1)
if descfpos=0 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "SysEnvironments header column missing in "the_APPMASTR
   my_rc=error_rc
   return error_rc
end
else do
  descfpos=descfpos+1
  descfend=descfpos
end
ll=length(APM.1)
done=0
do kk=descfpos to ll while \done
   if substr(APM.1,kk,1)<>" " then descfend=descfend+1
                              else done=1
end
descflen=descfend-descfpos+1

e_list=""
do kk=1 to APM.0
   if strip(APM.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(APM.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   if the_APP<>word(APM.kk,1) then iterate
   e_list=e_list  " "  substr(APM.kk,descfpos,descflen)  " "
end

env_list=""
do kk = 1 to words(e_list)
   w=word(e_list,kk)
   if wordpos(w,env_list)=0 then env_list=env_list  " "  w
end

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'env_list =' "'"env_list"'"

c=INP.0
do kk=1 to words(env_list)
   do jj=1 to ALC.0
      if strip(ALC.jj)="" then iterate
      if substr(ALC.jj,1,1)="*" then iterate
      rcf=word(ALC.jj,6)
      if rcf="VB" then rcf="V B"
      if rcf="FB" then rcf="F B"
      unt=word(ALC.jj,2)
      if unt="CYL" then szu="CYLINDERS"
                   else szu="TRACKS"
      blk=word(ALC.jj,8)
      if blk=0 then blksz=""
               else blksz=" BLKSIZE("  blk  ") "

      e=word(env_list,kk)
      x="DSN('"  the_DPFX  "."  e  "."  the_APP  "."
      do_these=""
      if substr(e,1,4)="TEST" then do_these="BASE REL1 REL2 REL3 REL4"
      if do_these="" then do
         x=x  word(ALC.jj,1)  "') NEW CATALOG DSORG(PO) UNIT(SYSDA) "  ,
           " RECFM("  rcf  ") "  ,
           szu  " DSNTYPE(LIBRARY) SPACE("  word(ALC.jj,3)  " "  ,
           word(ALC.jj,4)  ") LRECL("  word(ALC.jj,7)  ") "  blksz
         c=c+1
         INP.c=x
         iterate
      end
      do uu=1 to words(do_these)
        xmore=word(do_these,uu)  "."  ,
           word(ALC.jj,1)  "') NEW CATALOG DSORG(PO) UNIT(SYSDA) "  ,
           " RECFM("  rcf  ") "  ,
           szu  " DSNTYPE(LIBRARY) SPACE("  word(ALC.jj,3)  " "  ,
           word(ALC.jj,4)  ") LRECL("  word(ALC.jj,7)  ") "  blksz
        c=c+1
        INP.c=x  xmore
      end
   end
end
INP.0=c

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'ENV  Processed'
   Do i = 1 to INP.0
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          '   INP.'i '=' "'"Word( INP.i, 1)"'"
   End i

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'do_init: End  '

return my_rc
./  ADD  NAME=ENDVTSEB
/* REXX                                                               */
/**********************************************************************/
/* Name    : ENDVTSEB                                                 */
/* Desc    : Build the Environment File                              */
/* Version : 14/05/13                                                 */
/**********************************************************************/

/**********************************************************************/
/* Process :                                                          */
/*                                                                    */
/* Read the file of Extracted Stages from Endevor                     */
/* Extract the Stage 1 and Stage 2 records for each Environment       */
/* Write 1 record for each Environment                                */
/*                                                                    */
/**********************************************************************/

   Call SIV_SetInitialVars
   Call RIF_ReadIpFile

   ro = 1
   RecsOp.ro =,
      '*Envname  Stg1ID Stg1nme   Stg2ID Stg2nme  Entrystg# AdminEnv'

   Do r = 1 to RecsIn.0
      EnvName = Substr( RecsIn.r, 14, 8)
      StgName = Substr( RecsIn.r, 22, 8)
      StgID   = Substr( RecsIn.r, 30, 1)
      StgNum  = Substr( RecsIn.r, 31, 1)
      StgEntry= Substr( RecsIn.r, 97, 1)

      If StgNum = '1' Then
      Do
         Outrec = ' '  Left( EnvName, 8) Left( StgID, 6),
            Left( StgName, 9)
         If StgEntry = 'Y' Then
            EntryStg  = '1'
      End
      Else
      Do
         If StgEntry = 'Y' Then
            EntryStg  = '2'
         Outrec = Outrec Left( StgID, 6) Left( StgName, 8),
            Left( EntryStg, 9)
         If Left( EnvName, 3) = 'ADM' Then
            Outrec = Outrec 'Y'

         ro = ro + 1
         RecsOp.ro = Outrec
      End

   End r
   RecsOp.0 = ro

   Call WOF_WriteOpFile

EOJ:
   Say ' '
   Say '*' ExecName 'Return Code =' ExecRC
   Say '*' ExecName '  Ends' Date( 'N') Time( 'N')
   Say Copies( '*', 72)

   Exit ExecRC

/**********************************************************************/
/*                     S U B P R O C E D U R E S                      */
/**********************************************************************/
SIV_SetInitialVars:

   Parse Source . . ExecName . .

   Say ' '
   Say Copies( '*', 72)
   Say '*' ExecName 'Begins' Date( 'N') Time( 'N')

/* Set Initial VARs.                                                  */
   ExecRC   = 0

   RecsIn.  = ''

   RecsOp.  = ''
   RecsOp.0 = 0

   Return

/**********************************************************************/
RIF_ReadIpFile: Procedure Expose RecsIn.

   DdNameIn = 'ENDVLIST'

/* Read All Records into Stem RecsIn.                                 */
   'Execio * DiskR ' DdNameIn ' (Stem RecsIn. Finis'

   Say ' '
   Say '   Read' RecsIn.0 'lines from Input file' DdNameIn

   Return RC

/**********************************************************************/
WOF_WriteOpFile: Procedure Expose RecsOp.

   DdNameOp = 'ENVIRONS'

   'Execio * DiskW ' DdNameOp ' (Stem RecsOp. Finis'

   Say '   Wrote' RecsOp.0 'lines to Output file' DdNameOp

   Return RC

/**********************************************************************/
./  ADD  NAME=ENDVTSES
/* REXX */
/*======================================================*/
/*===  name   : ENDVTSES                             ===*/
/*===  purpose: used endevor conversion process      ===*/
/*===           to create ESYMBOL members            ===*/
/*===  parms  : DEBUG()   - debug flag Y/N N=deflt   ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*======================================================*/

parse upper arg my_parms
numeric digits 10
my_parms = " "  my_parms  " "    /* add spaces 4 parsing*/
my_rc = 0

                                       /* pull off debug parm */
                                       /* default is no debug */
                                       /* trace if debug=Y    */
parse var my_parms " DEBUG(" debug ")" .
my_item = "DEBUG("debug")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
debug = strip(debug)
if debug = "" then debug = "N"
if debug = "Y" then trace r
call do_init

do ii = 1 to LIBS.0 while my_rc<=4
   my_rc=do_work(LIBS.ii)
end

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    "RC="my_rc

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_work: procedure expose my_name OUTDD_dsn OPTB. OUTDD2_dsn
/*-------*/
arg the_dsn

cnt=0
my_rc=0
tbltool_parm="A"

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'do_work:'
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Processing the_dsn =' the_dsn

                                           /* obtain a list of member*/
                                           /* names from input dset  */
drop mud.
v = outtrap('mud.')
"LISTDS ('"the_dsn"') MEMBERS"
v = outtrap(OFF)
do vv = 1 to mud.0 until strip(mud.vv) = "--MEMBERS--"
end
do vvv = vv+1 to mud.0
   cnt=cnt+1
   MBRS.cnt=strip(mud.vvv)
end
MBRS.0=cnt


do jj=1 to MBRS.0 while my_rc=0

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Processing MBR     =' MBRS.jj

   my_rc=do_free("TBLOUT")
   my_rc=do_free("TABLE")
   my_rc=do_free("OPTIONS")
   L.1="ffffaaaa='"  MBRS.jj  "'"
   L.2="aaaabbbb=''"
   L.0=2
   vparm.1="ALLOC FILE(TABLE)  DSN('"  the_dsn    "("  MBRS.jj  ,
           ")') SHR REUSE"
   vparm.2="ALLOC FILE(TBLOUT) DSN('"  OUTDD_dsn  "("  MBRS.jj  ,
           ")') SHR REUSE"
   vparm.3="ALLOC FILE(OPTIONS) NEW DELETE UNIT(SYSDA) "  ,
           "SPACE(1 5) TRACK LRECL(80) RECFM(F B) REUSE"
   vparm.4="EXECIO "  L.0  " DISKW OPTIONS (STEM L."
   vparm.5="EXECIO "  OPTB.0  " DISKW OPTIONS (STEM OPTB. FINIS"
   vparm.0=5

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Allocating TABLE  to' the_dsn     '('MBRS.jj')'
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Allocating TBLOUT to' OUTDD_dsn   '('MBRS.jj')'

   do kk=1 to vparm.0 while my_rc=0
      x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
      address "TSO" vparm.kk
      io_rc = RC
      x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
      if io_rc > 4 then do
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "vparm.kk
         do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
            say left(my_name,9),
                left(time("L"),16),
                omsg.i
         end
         my_rc=error_rc
      end
   end

   if my_rc = 0 then do
      call "TBL#TOOL" tbltool_parm
      io_rc=result
      say "TBL#TOOL "tbltool_parm" RC="result" member="MBRS.jj
      if io_rc > 4 then do
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             "ERROR RC="io_rc" for TBL#TOOL "tbltool_parm" member=",
              MBRS.jj
         my_rc=error_rc
       end
       xx_rc=do_close("TBLOUT")  /*TBL#TOOL bug leaves it open */
   end
end

do jj=1 to MBRS.0 while my_rc=0
   my_rc=do_free("TBLOUT")
   my_rc=do_free("TABLE")
   my_rc=do_free("OPTIONS")
   L.1="ffffaaaa='"  MBRS.jj  "'"
   L.2="aaaabbbb='YourHQL.#.'"
   L.0=2
   vparm.1="ALLOC FILE(TABLE) DSN('"  the_dsn  "("  MBRS.jj  ,
           ")') SHR REUSE"
   vparm.2="ALLOC FILE(TBLOUT) DSN('"  OUTDD2_dsn  "("  MBRS.jj  ,
           ")') SHR REUSE"
   vparm.3="ALLOC FILE(OPTIONS) NEW DELETE UNIT(SYSDA) "  ,
           "SPACE(1 5) TRACK LRECL(80) RECFM(F B) REUSE"
   vparm.4="EXECIO "  L.0  " DISKW OPTIONS (STEM L."
   vparm.5="EXECIO "  OPTB.0  " DISKW OPTIONS (STEM OPTB. FINIS"
   vparm.0=5

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Allocating TABLE  to' the_dsn      '('MBRS.jj')'
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Allocating TBLOUT to' OUTDD2_dsn   '('MBRS.jj')'

   do kk=1 to vparm.0 while my_rc=0
      x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
      address "TSO" vparm.kk
      io_rc = RC
      x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
      if io_rc > 4 then do
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "vparm.kk
         do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
            say left(my_name,9),
                left(time("L"),16),
                omsg.i
         end
         my_rc=error_rc
      end
   end

   if my_rc = 0 then do
      call "TBL#TOOL" tbltool_parm
      io_rc=result
      say "TBL#TOOL "tbltool_parm" RC="result" member="MBRS.jj
      if io_rc > 4 then do
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             "ERROR RC="io_rc" for TBL#TOOL "tbltool_parm" member=",
              MBRS.jj
         my_rc=error_rc
       end
       xx_rc=do_close("TBLOUT")  /*TBL#TOOL bug leaves it open */
   end

end
my_rc=do_free("TBLOUT")
my_rc=do_free("TABLE")
my_rc=do_free("OPTIONS")

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_close:   procedure expose my_name error_rc
/*-------*/
arg DD

my_rc=0
cparm="EXECIO 0 DISKW "  DD  " (FINIS"

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" cparm
io_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
if io_rc > 4 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "cparm
   do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          omsg.i
   end
   my_rc=error_rc
end

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_free:    procedure
/*-------*/
arg DD

x=OUTTRAP("msg.")
address "TSO" "FREE FI("DD")"
x=OUTTRAP(OFF)

return 0


/*------*/
do_init:
/*------*/

parse source w1 w2 w3 w4 w5 w6 w7 w8
my_name = w3

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'do_init:'

error_rc=8
unknown_parms_rc=4

LIBS.0=0
the_INDD_dflt       = "PTBLS"
the_OUTDD_dflt      = "PESYMS"
the_OUTDD2_dflt     = "QESYMS"
the_OPTIN_dflt      = "OPTIN"


                                       /* pull off INDD       */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " INDD(" the_INDD ")" .
my_item = "INDD("the_INDD")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_INDD = strip(the_INDD)
if the_INDD = "" then the_INDD = the_INDD_dflt
if strip(the_INDD) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Parm INDD() required"
   my_rc=error_rc
end

                                       /* pull off OPTIN      */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " OPTIN(" the_OPTIN ")" .
my_item = "OPTIN("the_OPTIN")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_OPTIN = strip(the_OPTIN)
if the_OPTIN = "" then the_OPTIN = the_OPTIN_dflt
if strip(the_OPTIN) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Parm OPTIN() required"
   my_rc=error_rc
end


                                       /* pull off OUTDD      */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " OUTDD(" the_OUTDD ")" .
my_item = "OUTDD("the_OUTDD")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_OUTDD = strip(the_OUTDD)
if the_OUTDD = "" then the_OUTDD = the_OUTDD_dflt
if strip(the_OUTDD) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Parm OUTDD() required"
   my_rc=error_rc
end
if my_rc > 0 then return my_rc     /* quit if no place to write   */

                                       /* pull off OUTDD2     */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " OUTDD2(" the_OUTDD2 ")" .
my_item = "OUTDD2("the_OUTDD2")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_OUTDD2 = strip(the_OUTDD2)
if the_OUTDD2 = "" then the_OUTDD2 = the_OUTDD2_dflt
if strip(the_OUTDD2) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Parm OUTDD2() required"
   my_rc=error_rc
end
if my_rc > 0 then return my_rc     /* quit if no place to write   */
                                   /* output                      */


                                       /* any garbage parms?  */
if strip(my_parms) <> "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Unrecognized parms ignored: "my_parms
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Valid parms are DEBUG() INDD() OUTDD() OPTIN() OUTDD2()"
   my_rc=unknown_parms_rc
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc

INDD_dsn=""
x = LISTDSI(the_INDD "FILE")
if x <= 4 then do
   INDD_dsn=sysdsname
end
INDD_dsn=strip(INDD_dsn)

OUTDD_dsn=""
x = LISTDSI(the_OUTDD "FILE")
if x <= 4 then do
   OUTDD_dsn=sysdsname
end
OUTDD_dsn=strip(OUTDD_dsn)

if OUTDD_dsn="" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Unable to retrieve dataset name for DD "the_OUTDD
   my_rc=error_rc
end

OUTDD2_dsn=""
x = LISTDSI(the_OUTDD2 "FILE")
if x <= 4 then do
   OUTDD2_dsn=sysdsname
end
OUTDD2_dsn=strip(OUTDD2_dsn)

if OUTDD2_dsn="" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Unable to retrieve dataset name for DD "the_OUTDD2
   my_rc=error_rc
end

if INDD_dsn="" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Unable to retrieve dataset name for DD "the_INDD
   my_rc=error_rc
end
else do
   LIBS.1=INDD_dsn
   LIBS.0=1
end

aparm.1="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_OPTIN  " (STEM OPTB. FINIS "
aparm.0=1
do kk=1 to aparm.0 while my_rc=0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
      my_rc=error_rc
   end
end

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       ' '

return my_rc
./  ADD  NAME=ENDVTSEW
/* REXX */
/*======================================================*/
/*===  name   : ENDVTSEW                             ===*/
/*===  purpose: used endevor conversion process      ===*/
/*===           to create ESYMBOL members            ===*/
/*===  parms  : DEBUG()   - debug flag Y/N N=deflt   ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*======================================================*/
parse upper arg my_parms
numeric digits 10
my_parms = " "  my_parms  " "    /* add spaces 4 parsing*/
my_rc = 0

                                       /* pull off debug parm */
                                       /* default is no debug */
                                       /* trace if debug=Y    */
parse var my_parms " DEBUG(" debug ")" .
my_item = "DEBUG("debug")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
debug = strip(debug)
if debug = "" then debug = "N"
if debug = "Y" then trace r
call do_init

do kk=1 to DOIT.0 while my_rc=0
   my_rc=do_work(DOIT.kk)
end

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    "RC="my_rc

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_work: procedure expose my_name APPList
/*-------*/
arg flag libout libbase libprod libprom

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'do_work:'

cnt=0
my_rc=0
commline="********"
geneline="******** Generated on "  date()  " at "  time()
baseline="******** BaseLine   BASE   @P       "
prodline="******** Production PROD   $P       "
promline="******** Promotion Datasets         "
educline="******** Promotion Datasets for EDUC    @E "
inteline="******** Promotion Datasets for INTE    @F-INTE2 @G-INTE1 "
testline="******** Promotion Datasets for TEST Subsystem "
testln.1="********           @A -TEST1 @B =TEST2 @C -TEST3 @D -TEST4"
testln.2="********           @A1-TEST1 @B1=TEST2 @C1-TEST3 @D1-TEST4"
testln.3="********           @A2-TEST1 @B2=TEST2 @C2-TEST3 @D2-TEST4"
testln.4="********           @A3-TEST1 @B3=TEST2 @C3-TEST3 @D3-TEST4"
testln.5="********           @A4-TEST1 @B4=TEST2 @C4-TEST3 @D4-TEST4"
testln.0=5
emerline="******** Promotion Datasets for EMER    @H"

/* For each App */
do jj=1 to words(APPList) while my_rc=0
   drop L.
   L.0=0
   ap=word(APPList,jj)
   x=ap
   if length(x)<5 then x=x  "#"
   mbr_sfx=""

/* Set Live */
   if flag="N" then do
      L.1="          $ESYMBOL SYMNAME=#"  x  "PILOT,SYMDATA=' '"
      L.2="          $ESYMBOL SYMNAME=#"  x  "PREP,SYMDATA=' '"
      L.0=2
   end

/* Set Pilot */
   if flag="Y" then do
      L.1="          $ESYMBOL SYMNAME=#"  x  "PILOT,SYMDATA='YourHQL.#.'"
      L.2="          $ESYMBOL SYMNAME=#"  x  "PREP,SYMDATA=' '"
      L.0=2
      mbr_sfx="#"
   end

/* Set Prep */
   if flag="R" then do
      L.1="          $ESYMBOL SYMNAME=#"  x  "PILOT,SYMDATA='YourHQL.#.'"
      L.2="          $ESYMBOL SYMNAME=#"  x  "PREP,SYMDATA='YourHQL.#.'"
      L.0=2
      mbr_sfx="@"
   end

   lcnt=L.0

   my_rc=do_free("DDOUT")
   my_rc=do_free("DDBASE")
   my_rc=do_free("DDPROD")
   my_rc=do_free("DDPROM")

   blib="'"  libbase  "("  ap  ")'"
   plib="'"  libprod  "("  ap  ")'"
   mlib="'"  libprom  "("  ap  ")'"
   vcnt=1
   INBASE.0=0
   INPROD.0=0
   INPROM.0=0
   vparm.1="ALLOC FILE(DDOUT) DSN('"  libout  "("  ap  mbr_sfx  ,
           ")') SHR REUSE"
   if sysdsn(blib)="OK" then do
      vcnt=vcnt+1
      vparm.vcnt="ALLOC FILE(DDBASE) DSN("  blib  ") SHR REUSE"
      vcnt=vcnt+1
      vparm.vcnt="EXECIO * DISKR DDBASE (STEM INBASE. FINIS"
   end
   if sysdsn(plib)="OK" then do
      vcnt=vcnt+1
      vparm.vcnt="ALLOC FILE(DDPROD) DSN("  plib  ") SHR REUSE"
      vcnt=vcnt+1
      vparm.vcnt="EXECIO * DISKR DDPROD (STEM INPROD. FINIS"
   end
   if sysdsn(mlib)="OK" then do
      vcnt=vcnt+1
      vparm.vcnt="ALLOC FILE(DDPROM) DSN("  mlib  ") SHR REUSE"
      vcnt=vcnt+1
      vparm.vcnt="EXECIO * DISKR DDPROM (STEM INPROM. FINIS"
   end
   vparm.0=vcnt

   do kk=1 to vparm.0 while my_rc=0
      x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
      address "TSO" vparm.kk
      io_rc = RC
      x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
      if io_rc > 4 then do
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "vparm.kk
         do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
            say left(my_name,9),
                left(time("L"),16),
                omsg.i
         end
         my_rc=error_rc
      end
   end

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Allocated File DDOUT  to' "'"libout"'"

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Allocated File DDBASE to' blib
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Records Read           =' INBASE.0

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Allocated File DDPROD to' plib
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Records Read           =' INPROD.0

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Allocated File DDPROM to' mlib
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Records Read           =' INPROM.0

   top_test=0
   top_emer=0
   top_inte=0
   top_educ=0
   bot_test=0
   bot_emer=0
   bot_inte=0
   bot_educ=0
   do kk=1 to INPROM.0
      if top_test=0 & ,
         (pos('@A',INPROM.kk)<>0   ,
          pos('@B',INPROM.kk)<>0   ,
          pos('@C',INPROM.kk)<>0   ,
          pos('@D',INPROM.kk)<>0  )            then top_test=kk
      if top_inte=0 & ,
         (pos('@G',INPROM.kk)<>0   ,
          pos('@F',INPROM.kk)<>0  )            then top_inte=kk
      if top_emer=0 & (pos('@H',INPROM.kk)<>0) then top_emer=kk
      if top_educ=0 & (pos('@E',INPROM.kk)<>0) then top_educ=kk
   end
   if top_educ<>0 then do
      bot_educ=INPROM.0
      if top_emer<>0 then bot_educ=top_emer-1
      if top_test<>0 then bot_educ=top_test-1
      if top_inte<>0 then bot_educ=top_inte-1
   end
   if top_inte<>0 then do
      bot_inte=INPROM.0
      if top_emer<>0 then bot_inte=top_emer-1
      if top_test<>0 then bot_inte=top_test-1
   end
   if top_test<>0 then do
      bot_test=INPROM.0
      if top_emer<>0 then bot_test=top_emer-1
   end
   if top_emer<>0 then do
      bot_emer=INPROM.0
   end
 /*say "EDUC "top_educ bot_educ
   say "INTE "top_inte bot_inte
   say "TEST "top_test bot_test
   say "EMER "top_emer bot_emer */

   lcnt=lcnt+1
   L.lcnt=commline
   lcnt=lcnt+1
   L.lcnt=commline
   lcnt=lcnt+1
   L.lcnt=geneline
   lcnt=lcnt+1
   L.lcnt=commline
   lcnt=lcnt+1
   L.lcnt=commline
   lcnt=lcnt+1
   L.lcnt=baseline
   lcnt=lcnt+1
   L.lcnt=commline
   do kk=1 to INBASE.0
      lcnt=lcnt+1
      L.lcnt=INBASE.kk
   end

   lcnt=lcnt+1
   L.lcnt=commline
   lcnt=lcnt+1
   L.lcnt=prodline
   lcnt=lcnt+1
   L.lcnt=commline
   do kk=1 to INPROD.0
      lcnt=lcnt+1
      L.lcnt=INPROD.kk
   end

   lcnt=lcnt+1
   L.lcnt=commline
   lcnt=lcnt+1
   L.lcnt=promline
   lcnt=lcnt+1
   L.lcnt=commline
   found_c=0
   found_d=0
   found_e=0
   found_h=0

   do kk=top_educ to bot_educ while top_educ<>0
      if \found_e & pos('@E',INPROM.kk)<>0 then do
         found_e=1
         lcnt=lcnt+1
         L.lcnt=commline
         lcnt=lcnt+1
         L.lcnt=educline
         lcnt=lcnt+1
         L.lcnt=commline
      end
      lcnt=lcnt+1
      L.lcnt=INPROM.kk
   end

   do kk=top_inte to bot_inte while top_inte<>0
      if kk=top_inte then do
         lcnt=lcnt+1
         L.lcnt=commline
         lcnt=lcnt+1
         L.lcnt=inteline
         lcnt=lcnt+1
         L.lcnt=commline
         last_one=""
      end
      if pos('$ESYMBOL',INPROM.kk)=0 then do
         lcnt=lcnt+1
         L.lcnt=INPROM.kk
      end
      else do
         parse var INPROM.kk xxx 'SYMNAME=' this_one '@' xxxx
         if this_one<>last_one then do
            if kk<>top_inte then do
               lcnt=lcnt+1
               L.lcnt='*'
            end
            last_one=this_one
         end
         lcnt=lcnt+1
         L.lcnt=INPROM.kk
      end
   end

   test_gens="BASE REL1 REL2 REL3 REL4"
   do ii=1 to words(test_gens) while top_test<>0
      do kk=top_test to bot_test while top_test<>0
         if kk=top_test then do
            lcnt=lcnt+1
            L.lcnt=commline
            lcnt=lcnt+1
            L.lcnt=testline  word(test_gens,ii)
            lcnt=lcnt+1
            L.lcnt=testln.ii
            lcnt=lcnt+1
            L.lcnt=commline
            last_one=""
         end
         if pos('$ESYMBOL',INPROM.kk)=0 then do
            lcnt=lcnt+1
            L.lcnt=INPROM.kk
         end
         else do
            parse var INPROM.kk xxx 'SYMNAME=' this_one '@' xxxx
            if this_one<>last_one then do
               if kk<>top_test then do
                  lcnt=lcnt+1
                  L.lcnt='*'
               end
               last_one=this_one
            end
            ppp=pos(', ',INPROM.kk)
            tpb=delstr(INPROM.kk,ppp)
            tpe=delstr(INPROM.kk,1,ppp+1)
            lcnt=lcnt+1
            if ii>1 then L.lcnt=tpb  left(ii-1,1)  ","  tpe
                    else L.lcnt=tpb  ", "  tpe
         end
      end
   end

   do kk=top_emer to bot_emer while top_emer<>0
      if \found_h then do
         found_h=1
         lcnt=lcnt+1
         L.lcnt=commline
         lcnt=lcnt+1
         L.lcnt=emerline
         lcnt=lcnt+1
         L.lcnt=commline
      end
      lcnt=lcnt+1
      L.lcnt=INPROM.kk
   end

   L.0=lcnt

   vparm.1="EXECIO "  L.0  " DISKW DDOUT (STEM L. FINIS"
   vparm.0=1

   do kk=1 to vparm.0 while my_rc=0
      x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
      address "TSO" vparm.kk
      io_rc = RC
      x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
      if io_rc > 4 then do
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "vparm.kk
         do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
            say left(my_name,9),
                left(time("L"),16),
                omsg.i
         end
         my_rc=error_rc
      end
   end

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Records Written to DDOUT =' L.0
   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       ' '

end jj

my_rc=do_free("DDOUT")
my_rc=do_free("DDBASE")
my_rc=do_free("DDPROD")
my_rc=do_free("DDPROM")

return my_rc



/*-------*/
do_free:    procedure
/*-------*/
arg DD

x=OUTTRAP("msg.")
address "TSO" "FREE FI("DD")"
x=OUTTRAP(OFF)

return 0
