./  ADD  NAME=ENDVTSGY
/* REXX */
/*======================================================*/
/*===  name   : ENDVTSGY                             ===*/
/*===  purpose: used endevor conversion process      ===*/
/*===           to create endevor SCL                ===*/
/*===  parms  : DEBUG()   - debug flag Y/N N=deflt   ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*======================================================*/

/**********************************************************************/
/* Changed all occurrences of CMNTOEND to LMSTOEND                    */
/*                                                                    */
/* Allow for reading these datasets:                                  */
/*    YourHQL.ENDV.SYQ.CV.D40423.T2140.ECPYMST.V01                         */
/*    YourHQL.ENDV.SYQ.CV.D40423.T2140.ECTLMST.V01                         */
/*    YourHQL.ENDV.SYQ.CV.D40423.T2140.EDOCMST.V01                         */
/*    YourHQL.ENDV.SYQ.CV.D40423.T2140.EMACMST.V01                         */
/*    YourHQL.ENDV.SYQ.CV.D40423.T2140.EMFSMST.V01                         */
/*    YourHQL.ENDV.SYQ.CV.D40423.T2140.ENEPMST.V01                         */
/*    YourHQL.ENDV.SYQ.CV.D40423.T2140.EPRCMST.V01                         */
/*    YourHQL.ENDV.SYQ.CV.D40423.T2140.EPSBMST.V01                         */
/*    YourHQL.ENDV.SYQ.CV.D40423.T2140.ESRCMST.V01                         */
/*    YourHQL.ENDV.SYQ.CV.D40423.T2140.ETSOMST.V01                         */
/*                                                                    */
/**********************************************************************/

parse upper arg my_parms
numeric digits 10
my_parms = " "  my_parms  " "    /* add spaces 4 parsing*/
my_rc = 0

                                       /* pull off debug parm */
                                       /* default is no debug */
                                       /* trace if debug=Y    */
parse var my_parms " DEBUG(" debug ")" .
my_item = "DEBUG("debug")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
debug = strip(debug)
if debug = "" then debug = "N"
if debug = "Y" then trace r

call do_init

openned=0
last_app=""
did_it=""
do ii = 1 to SC.0 while my_rc<=4
   my_rc=do_work(ii)
end
xx_rc=do_free(the_TEMPDD)
xx_rc=do_free(the_TEMPDD2)
xx_rc=do_free(the_TEMPDD3)
xx_rc=do_free(the_TEMPDD4)
xx_rc=do_free(the_TEMPDD5)
xx_rc=do_free(the_TEMPDD6)
xx_rc=do_free(the_TEMPDD7)
xx_rc=do_free(the_TEMPDD8)

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    "RC="my_rc

ZISPFRC=my_rc
vparm="VPUT (ZISPFRC)"
address "ISPEXEC" vparm
hold_rc = RC
if hold_rc > 4 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "ERROR RC="my_rc  " for: "  vparm
end

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_work: procedure expose my_name error_rc SC. MB. the_TEMPDD openned,
                          last_ap the_DPFX the_TEMPDD2 the_TEMPDD3 ,
                          the_TEMPDD4 the_TEMPDD5 the_TEMPDD6 ,
                          the_TEMPDD7 ,
                          the_TEMPDD8 ,
                          generate_GENFROM generate_GENCODE ,
                          generate_GENMFS generate_GENPSB ,
                          generate_GENPSO DSETPFX FORDLIB ,
                          did_it SKP. SKA. SPL. chk_dcl split_list
/*-------*/
arg ndx

   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'do_work: Begin'

my_rc=0
skip_it=0
chk_me=0
if SC.ndx.CTYP="DCL" & chk_dcl then chk_me=1
if chk_me & wordpos(SC.ndx,split_list)=0  then chk_me=0

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    "Processing App:"SC.ndx" Lib:"SC.ndx.CTYP

ctt=SC.ndx.CTYP
ct1=substr(SC.ndx.CTYP,1,1)
ct2=substr(SC.ndx.CTYP,1,2)
if ct1='$'   then skip_it=1
if ct2='IM'  then skip_it=1
if ct2='IS'  then skip_it=1
if ct2='NM'  then skip_it=1
if ct2='NS'  then skip_it=1
if ct2='WM'  then skip_it=1
if ct2='WS'  then skip_it=1
if ctt='PKG' then skip_it=1
if ctt='DBB' then skip_it=1
if ctt='DBR' then skip_it=1
if ctt='LDP' then skip_it=1
if ctt='LDI' then skip_it=1
if ctt='GRP' then skip_it=1
if ctt='LOD' then skip_it=1
if ctt='MFR' then skip_it=1
if ctt='FMT' then skip_it=1
if ctt='PSL' then skip_it=1
if skip_it then do
    say "Skipping "SC.ndx.CTYP
    return my_rc
end
ectt=SC.ndx.CETYP

do kk=0 to SC.ndx.CMAX while my_rc=0
   if my_rc <=4 then my_rc=0

   if SC.ndx<>last_ap then do
      oparm=the_TEMPDD2  " "  the_TEMPDD3  " "  ,
            the_TEMPDD4  " "  the_TEMPDD5  " "  ,
            the_TEMPDD6  " "  the_TEMPDD7  " "  the_TEMPDD8  " "  ndx
      if openned then my_rc=do_close(oparm)
      if my_rc=0 then my_rc=do_open(oparm)
      last_ap=SC.ndx
      if my_rc<>0 then iterate
   end

   cnt=0
   drop MBRS.
   MBRS.0=0

   the_dsn=SC.ndx.CLPFX  right(kk,2,'0')

   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'LISTDS in ' "'"the_dsn"'"

   drop mud.
   v = outtrap('mud.')
   "LISTDS ('"the_dsn"') MEMBERS"
   my_rc=RC
   v = outtrap(OFF)
   if my_rc>4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="my_rc" for "the_dsn
   end
   if my_rc>4 then return error_rc

   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'LISTDS out' "'"the_dsn"'"

   dclpos=1
   do vv = 1 to mud.0 until strip(mud.vv) = "--MEMBERS--"
   end
   do vvv = vv+1 to mud.0
      dclkeep=1
      if chk_me then do
         dclkeep=0
         do ccc=dclpos to SPL.0 while \dclkeep
            if words(SPL.ccc)<>3 then iterate
            cccA=word(SPL.ccc,1)
            cccT=word(SPL.ccc,2)
            cccM=word(SPL.ccc,3)
            if cccA>SC.ndx then leave
            if cccA<SC.ndx then iterate
            if cccT>SC.ndx.CTYP then leave
            if cccT<SC.ndx.CTYP then iterate
            if cccM>strip(mud.vvv) then leave
            if cccM<strip(mud.vvv) then iterate
            dclkeep=1
            leave
         end
         dclpos=ccc
      end
      if dclkeep then do
         cnt=cnt+1
         MBRS.cnt=strip(mud.vvv)
      end
   end
   MBRS.0=cnt

   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Members =' "'"MBRS.0"'"

   lastndx=1
   if kk=0 then do
      MASTER.0=MBRS.0
      do jj=1 to MBRS.0
         MASTER.jj=MBRS.jj
         MASTER.jj.FND="00"
         MASTER.jj.MODTIME=""
         MASTER.jj.MODDATE=""
         MBRS.jj.MASTER=jj
         MASTER.jj.SKIP=0
         MASTER.jj.SKIPADD=0
         do mm=1 to SKA.0
            if word(SKA.mm,1)>SC.ndx      then leave
            if SC.ndx<>word(SKA.mm,1)     then iterate
            if word(SKA.mm,2)>MASTER.jj   then leave
            if MASTER.jj<>word(SKA.mm,2)  then iterate
            MASTER.jj.SKIPADD=1
            say "Will skip add for "MASTER.jj,
                " App="SC.ndx
            leave
         end
         do mm=lastndx to SKP.0
            if word(SKP.mm,1)>SC.ndx      then leave
            if SC.ndx<>word(SKP.mm,1)     then iterate
            if word(SKP.mm,2)>ectt        then leave
            if ectt<>word(SKP.mm,2)       then iterate
            if word(SKP.mm,3)>MASTER.jj   then leave
            if MASTER.jj<>word(SKP.mm,3)  then iterate
            MASTER.jj.SKIP=1
            say "Will skip generation for "MASTER.jj" Type="ectt,
                "App="SC.ndx
            leave
         end
         lastndx=mm
      end
   end
   else do
      mpos=1
      do jj=1 to MBRS.0
         do ii=mpos to MASTER.0
            if MBRS.jj=MASTER.ii then do
               MASTER.ii.FND=MASTER.ii.FND  " "  right(kk,2,'0')
               MBRS.jj.MASTER=ii
               mpos=ii
               leave
            end
         end
      end
   end
   if MBRS.0=0 then iterate

   lastgg=1
   do ff=1 to MASTER.0
      MASTER.ff.DEACT=0
      MASTER.ff.MTYP=""
      MASTER.ff.MPRC=""
      do gg=lastgg to MB.0
         if MB.gg>MASTER.ff  then leave
         if MASTER.ff<>MB.gg then iterate
         if MB.gg.EPRC="DEACT" then MASTER.ff.DEACT=1
         MASTER.ff.MTYP=MB.gg.ETYP
         MASTER.ff.MPRC=MB.gg.EPRC
         leave
      end
      lastgg=gg
      if MASTER.ff="OECCHDIV"   ,
         MASTER.ff="OECCOEEA"   ,
         MASTER.ff="OECCONEA"   ,
         MASTER.ff="OECMVPRP"   ,
         MASTER.ff="CNCPSVBD"   ,
         MASTER.ff="C70GETJB"   ,
         MASTER.ff="C7000106"   ,
         MASTER.ff="C70002A8"   ,
         MASTER.ff="C70002A9"   ,
         MASTER.ff="CRP9205B"   ,
         MASTER.ff="DESC02"   ,
         MASTER.ff="GTU01"   ,
         MASTER.ff="GTU02"   ,
         MASTER.ff="HRSNON04"   ,
         MASTER.ff="HR009013"   ,
         MASTER.ff="HR009014"   ,
         MASTER.ff="HR009050"   ,
         MASTER.ff="HR009110"   ,
         MASTER.ff="LGTHCALC"   ,
         MASTER.ff="PGMABORT"   ,
         MASTER.ff="SETDD"   ,
         MASTER.ff="SNOFXIT"   ,
         MASTER.ff="STRNGFND"   ,
         MASTER.ff="OEFGVWAS" then do
         MASTER.ff.MTYP="ASM"
         MASTER.ff.MPRC="COMPILE"
      end
      if wordpos(MASTER.ff,FORDLIB)<>0 then do
         MASTER.ff.MTYP="ASM"
         MASTER.ff.MPRC="COMPILE"
      end
   end

   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       '         ' "'"MBRS.0"'"

   xx_rc=do_free(the_TEMPDD)
   aparm="ALLOC FI("  the_TEMPDD  ") DA('"  the_dsn  "') SHR REUSE"
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm
   my_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if my_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="my_rc" for "aparm
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
      my_rc=error_rc
   end
   if my_rc>4 then return error_rc

   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Allocating DSN' "'"DSN"'"

   address "ISPEXEC" "CONTROL ERRORS RETURN"
   aparm="LMINIT DATAID(DID) DDNAME("  the_TEMPDD  ") ENQ(SHR)"
   address "ISPEXEC" aparm
   my_rc=RC
   if my_rc>4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="my_rc" for "aparm
   end
   if my_rc>4 then return error_rc

   aparm="LMOPEN DATAID("  DID  ") OPTION(INPUT)"
   address "ISPEXEC" aparm
   my_rc=RC
   if my_rc>4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="my_rc" for "aparm
   end
   if my_rc>4 then return error_rc

   do jj=1 to MBRS.0 while my_rc<=4
      aparm="LMMFIND DATAID("  DID  ") MEMBER("  MBRS.jj  ") STATS(YES)"
      address "ISPEXEC" aparm
      my_rc=RC
      if my_rc>4 then do
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             "ERROR RC="my_rc" for "aparm
      end
      if my_rc>4 then return error_rc

      xx=MBRS.jj.MASTER
      MASTER.xx.MODTIME=MASTER.xx.MODTIME  " "  ZLMTIME
      MASTER.xx.MODDATE=MASTER.xx.MODDATE  " "  ZLM4DATE
   end


   aparm.1="LMCLOSE DATAID("  DID  ")"
   aparm.2="LMFREE DATAID("  DID  ")"
   aparm.0=2
   do ii=1 to aparm.0 while my_rc<=4
      address "ISPEXEC" aparm.ii
      my_rc=RC
      if my_rc>4 then do
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             "ERROR RC="my_rc" for "aparm.ii
      end
      if my_rc>4 then return error_rc
   end

   xx_rc=do_free(the_TEMPDD)

end

wparm=the_TEMPDD2  " "  the_TEMPDD3  " "  ,
      the_TEMPDD4  " "  the_TEMPDD5  " "  ,
      the_TEMPDD6  " "  the_TEMPDD7  " "  the_TEMPDD8  " "  ndx
if my_rc <=4 then my_rc=do_write(wparm)

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_open:   procedure expose my_name error_rc SC. the_DPFX openned
/*-------*/
arg DD DD2 DD3 DD4 DD5 DD6 DD7 ndx

   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'do_open: Begin'

my_rc=0

xx_rc=do_free(DD)
xx_rc=do_free(DD2)
xx_rc=do_free(DD3)
xx_rc=do_free(DD4)
xx_rc=do_free(DD5)
xx_rc=do_free(DD6)
xx_rc=do_free(DD7)

aparm.1="ALLOC FI("  DD   ") DA('"  SC.ndx.CADSN   "') SHR REUSE"
aparm.2="ALLOC FI("  DD2  ") DA('"  SC.ndx.CGDSN   "') SHR REUSE"
aparm.3="ALLOC FI("  DD3  ") DA('"  SC.ndx.CGCODE  "') SHR REUSE"
aparm.4="ALLOC FI("  DD7  ") DA('"  SC.ndx.CGCOPY  "') SHR REUSE"
aparm.5="ALLOC FI("  DD4  ") DA('"  SC.ndx.CGPSO   "') SHR REUSE"
aparm.6="ALLOC FI("  DD5  ") DA('"  SC.ndx.CGPSB   "') SHR REUSE"
aparm.7="ALLOC FI("  DD6  ") DA('"  SC.ndx.CGMFS   "') SHR REUSE"
aparm.8 ="EXECIO 0 DISKW "  DD
aparm.9 ="EXECIO 0 DISKW "  DD2
aparm.10="EXECIO 0 DISKW "  DD3
aparm.11="EXECIO 0 DISKW "  DD4
aparm.12="EXECIO 0 DISKW "  DD5
aparm.13="EXECIO 0 DISKW "  DD6
aparm.14="EXECIO 0 DISKW "  DD7
aparm.0=14

do kk=1 to aparm.0 while my_rc=0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   my_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if my_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="my_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
     return error_rc
   end
   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Executing' aparm.kk
end kk
openned=1

   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'do_open: End'

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_close:   procedure expose my_name error_rc openned
/*-------*/
arg DD DD2 DD3 DD4 DD5 DD6 DD7 ndx

my_rc=0
openned=0

aparm.1="EXECIO 0 DISKW "  DD   " (FINIS"
aparm.2="EXECIO 0 DISKW "  DD2  " (FINIS"
aparm.3="EXECIO 0 DISKW "  DD3  " (FINIS"
aparm.4="EXECIO 0 DISKW "  DD4  " (FINIS"
aparm.5="EXECIO 0 DISKW "  DD5  " (FINIS"
aparm.6="EXECIO 0 DISKW "  DD6  " (FINIS"
aparm.7="EXECIO 0 DISKW "  DD7  " (FINIS"
aparm.0=7

do kk=1 to aparm.0 while my_rc=0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   my_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if my_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="my_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
     return error_rc
   end
end


return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_write:   procedure expose my_name error_rc openned SC. MASTER. ,
                             generate_GENFROM generate_GENCODE ,
                             generate_GENMFS generate_GENPSB ,
                             generate_GENPSO did_it DSETPFX
/*-------*/
arg DD DD2 DD3 DD4 DD5 DD6 DD7 ndx

my_rc=0

TOJCL=""
O.1=" SET TO ENVIRONMENT PROD STAGE P SYSTEM "  ,
      SC.ndx  " SUBSYSTEM BASE ."
O.2=" SET OPTIONS CCID 'LMSMIGR' OVERRIDE SIGNOUT "
O.3="     BYPASS GENERATE PROCESSOR UPDATE ."
c=3
d=0
PP.1="//S"  left(ndx,7)  " EXEC PGM=IEBCOPY,COND=(5,LT)"
PP.2="//SYSPRINT DD SYSOUT=*"
PP.0=2
QQ.1="//SYSIN   DD *"
QQ.0=1
P.0=0
Q.0=0
iebc=0
jclc=0
dmfs=0
dpsb=0
dpso=0
dcode=0
last_jfrom=""
fromndx=0
last_cfrom=""
do kk=SC.ndx.CMAX to 0 by -1
   generate_me=0
   if SC.ndx.CGENO<>0 then generate_me=1
   if kk=0 then do
      c=c+1
      O.c=" SET OPTIONS CCID 'LMSMIGR' UPDATE ."
   end
   x=right(kk,2,'0')
   c=c+1
   O.c=" SET FROM DSNAME '"  SC.ndx.CLPFX  x  "' ."
   if kk=0 then do
      this_jfrom=SC.ndx.CLPFX  x
      if this_jfrom<>last_jfrom then do
         jclc=jclc+1
         fromndx=fromndx+1
         P.jclc="//F"  left(fromndx,7)  " DD DISP=SHR,DSN="this_jfrom
         last_jfrom=this_jfrom
      end
   end
   do jj=1 to MASTER.0
      if MASTER.jj.SKIPADD then iterate
      if strip(MASTER.jj.MTYP)="" then MASTER.jj.MTYP=SC.ndx.CETYP
      if strip(MASTER.jj.MPRC)="" then MASTER.jj.MPRC=SC.ndx.CEPRC
      if strip(MASTER.jj.MPRC)="DEACT" then MASTER.jj.MPRC=SC.ndx.CEPRC
      if SC.ndx.CTYP<>"SRC" then do
         MASTER.jj.MTYP=SC.ndx.CETYP
         MASTER.jj.MPRC=SC.ndx.CEPRC
      end
      if strip(MASTER.jj.MTYP)="ASM" then MASTER.jj.MPRC="COMPILE"
      if strip(MASTER.jj.MTYP)="CLD" then MASTER.jj.MPRC="CLD"
      wp=wordpos(x,MASTER.jj.FND)
      if wp=0 then iterate
      m=word(MASTER.jj.MODDATE,wp)  " "  word(MASTER.jj.MODTIME,wp)
      if kk=0 then do
         if wordpos(MASTER.jj.MTYP,TOJCL)=0 then do
            TOJCL=TOJCL  " "  MASTER.jj.MTYP
            jclc=jclc+1
            P.jclc="//"left(MASTER.jj.MTYP,8)  " DD DISP=SHR,DSN="  ,
                   DSETPFX  SC.ndx  "."  MASTER.jj.MTYP
         end
         cfrom=" COPY INDD=((F"  strip(fromndx)  ,
               ",R)),OUTDD="  MASTER.jj.MTYP
         if last_cfrom<>cfrom then do
            iebc=iebc+1
            Q.iebc=cfrom
            last_cfrom=cfrom
         end
         iebc=iebc+1
         Q.iebc=" S M="  MASTER.jj
      end
      c=c+1
      O.c="* S M="  MASTER.jj  " "  MASTER.jj.MTYP
      c=c+1
      O.c=" ADD ELEMENT "  MASTER.jj  " TO TYPE "  MASTER.jj.MTYP
      c=c+1
      O.c="   OPTIONS PROCESSOR GROUP= "  MASTER.jj.MPRC
      c=c+1
      O.c='   COMMENTS "LMSTOEND: '  MASTER.jj  ' '  m  '". '
      if generate_me & \MASTER.jj.DEACT & \MASTER.jj.SKIP then do
       peedle=" "  SC.ndx  "-"  MASTER.jj.MTYP  "-"  MASTER.jj  " "
       if pos(peedle,did_it)=0 then do
         did_it=did_it  peedle
         TTT.1=' GENERATE ELEMENT "'  MASTER.jj  '"'
         TTT.2=' FROM ENVIRONMENT "'  SC.ndx.CGENV  '"'
         TTT.3='   SYSTEM "'  SC.ndx  '" SUBSYSTEM "BASE"'
         TTT.4='   TYPE "'  MASTER.jj.MTYP  ,
               '" STAGE "'  SC.ndx.CSTAGE  '"'
         TTT.5="   OPTIONS COMMENT 'LMSTOEND Initial Generation'"
         TTT.6='           CCID "LMSMIGR" OVERRIDE SIGNOUT'
         TTT.7='           PROCESSOR GROUP "'  MASTER.jj.MPRC  '"'
         TTT.8='           SEARCH COPYBACK .'
         TTT.0=8
         select
           when wordpos(MASTER.jj.MTYP,generate_GENPSO)<>0 then do
              do kkk=1 to TTT.0
                 dpso=dpso+1
                 APSO.dpso=TTT.kkk
              end
           end
           when wordpos(MASTER.jj.MTYP,generate_GENPSB)<>0 then do
              do kkk=1 to TTT.0
                 dpsb=dpsb+1
                 APSB.dpsb=TTT.kkk
              end
           end
           when wordpos(MASTER.jj.MTYP,generate_GENMFS)<>0 then do
              do kkk=1 to TTT.0
                 dmfs=dmfs+1
                 AMFS.dmfs=TTT.kkk
              end
           end
           when wordpos(MASTER.jj.MTYP,generate_GENCODE)<>0 then do
              do kkk=1 to TTT.0
                 dcode=dcode+1
                 ACODE.dcode=TTT.kkk
              end
           end
           otherwise do
              TTT.2=' FROM ENVIRONMENT "PROD"'
              TTT.4='   TYPE "'  MASTER.jj.MTYP  ,
                    '" STAGE "P"'
              do kkk=1 to TTT.0
                 d=d+1
                 G.d=TTT.kkk
              end
           end
         end
       end
      end
   end
end
do jj=1 to MASTER.0
   if MASTER.jj.SKIPADD then iterate
   c=c+1
   O.c=" SET FROM ENVIRONMENT PROD STAGE P SYSTEM "  SC.ndx  ,
       " SUBSYSTEM BASE ."
   c=c+1
   O.c=" SIGNIN ELEMENT "  MASTER.jj  " FROM TYPE "  ,
       MASTER.jj.MTYP  " ."
end
O.0=c
G.0=d
APSB.0=dpsb
APSO.0=dpso
AMFS.0=dmfs
ACODE.0=dcode
P.0=jclc
Q.0=iebc
if O.0=0 then do
   O.0=1
   O.1="*"
end
if G.0=0 then do
   G.0=1
   G.1="*"
end
if APSB.0=0 then do
   APSB.0=1
   APSB.1="*"
end
if APSO.0=0 then do
   APSO.0=1
   APSO.1="*"
end
if AMFS.0=0 then do
   AMFS.0=1
   AMFS.1="*"
end
if ACODE.0=0 then do
   ACODE.0=1
   ACODE.1="*"
end


aparm.1="EXECIO "O.0" DISKW "  DD  " (STEM O."
aparm.2="EXECIO "G.0" DISKW "  DD2  " (STEM G."
aparm.3="EXECIO "ACODE.0" DISKW "  DD3  " (STEM ACODE."
aparm.4="EXECIO "APSO.0" DISKW "  DD4  " (STEM APSO."
aparm.5="EXECIO "APSB.0" DISKW "  DD5  " (STEM APSB."
aparm.6="EXECIO "AMFS.0" DISKW "  DD6  " (STEM AMFS."
apcnt=6
if P.0>0 then do
   apcnt=apcnt+1
   aparm.apcnt="EXECIO "PP.0" DISKW "  DD7  " (STEM PP."
   apcnt=apcnt+1
   aparm.apcnt="EXECIO "P.0" DISKW "  DD7  " (STEM P."
   apcnt=apcnt+1
   aparm.apcnt="EXECIO "QQ.0" DISKW "  DD7  " (STEM QQ."
   apcnt=apcnt+1
   aparm.apcnt="EXECIO "Q.0" DISKW "  DD7  " (STEM Q."
end
aparm.0=apcnt

do kk=1 to aparm.0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
      my_rc=error_rc
   end
end

   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Writing' O.0     'records to DD' DD
   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Writing' G.0     'records to DD' DD2
   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Writing' ACODE.0 'records to DD' DD3
   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Writing' APSO.0  'records to DD' DD4
   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Writing' APSB.0  'records to DD' DD5
   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Writing' AMFS.0  'records to DD' DD6

   if P.0>0 then
   do
      Say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          'Writing' PP.0   'records to DD' DD7
      Say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          'Writing' P.0    'records to DD' DD7
      Say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          'Writing' QQ.0   'records to DD' DD7
      Say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          'Writing' Q.0    'records to DD' DD7
   end

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_free:    procedure
/*-------*/
arg DD

x=OUTTRAP("msg.")
address "TSO" "FREE FI("DD")"
x=OUTTRAP(OFF)

return 0


/*------*/
do_init:
/*------*/

parse source w1 w2 w3 w4 w5 w6 w7 w8
my_name = w3

   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'do_init: Begin'

chk_dcl=0
error_rc=8
unknown_parms_rc=4
generate_order=,
"DCL CPY INC SEG MAC CPA CPC MPS LCT MFS PSB REX ASM PLI COB"
generate_GENFROM="DCL CPY INC SEG MAC CPA CPC MPS LCT"
generate_0ENCODE="REX ASM PLI COB"
generate_GENMFS="MFS"
generate_GENPSB="PSB"
generate_GENPSO="PSO"

the_DPFX_dflt       = ""
the_FAC_dflt        = ""
the_SCLDD_dflt      = "SCLDD"
the_SPLITS_dflt     = "SPLITS"
the_SKIPDD_dflt     = "SKIPDD"
the_SKIPADD_dflt    = "SKIPADD"
the_TEMPDD_dflt     = "TEMPDD"
the_TEMPDD2_dflt    = "T2MPDD"
the_TEMPDD3_dflt    = "T3MPDD"
the_TEMPDD4_dflt    = "T4MPDD"
the_TEMPDD5_dflt    = "T5MPDD"
the_TEMPDD6_dflt    = "T6MPDD"
the_TEMPDD7_dflt    = "T7MPDD"
the_TEMPDD8_dflt    = "T8MPDD"
the_FLIBDD_dflt     = "FLIBDD"
the_APPMASTR_dflt   = "APPMASTR"
the_LMSTOEND_dflt   = "LMSTOEND"
the_INDEX_dflt      = "INDEX"


                                       /* pull off FAC        */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " FAC(" the_FAC ")" .
my_item = "FAC("the_FAC")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_FAC = strip(the_FAC)
if the_FAC = "" then the_FAC = the_FAC_dflt
if strip(the_FAC) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Parm FAC() required"
   my_rc=error_rc
end

                                   /* output                      */


                                       /* any garbage parms?  */
if strip(my_parms) <> "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Unrecognized parms ignored: "my_parms
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Valid parms are DEBUG() SCLDD() INDEX() DPFX() LMSTOEND() "
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       " SKIPADD() SKIPDD() TEMPDD() TEMPDD2() TEMPDD3() APPMASTR()   "
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       " SPLITS() FAC()   "
   my_rc=unknown_parms_rc
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc

if the_FAC="C" then chk_dcl=1

aparm.1="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_SCLDD       " (STEM SCL. FINIS"
aparm.2="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_INDEX       " (STEM INP. FINIS"
aparm.3="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_APPMASTR    " (STEM APP. FINIS"
aparm.4="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_LMSTOEND    " (STEM INC. FINIS"
aparm.5="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_SKIPDD      " (STEM SKP. FINIS"
aparm.6="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_SKIPADD     " (STEM SKA. FINIS"
aparm.7="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_SPLITS      " (STEM SPL. FINIS"
aparm.8="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_FLIBDD      " (STEM FLIB. FINIS"
aparm.0=8

ENODE=the_FAC
if the_FAC="D" then ENODE="9"
DSETPFX="YourHQL.ENDV.SY"  ENODE  ".PROD."

do kk=1 to aparm.0 while my_rc=0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
      my_rc=error_rc
   end
   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Executing' aparm.kk
end kk
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc

   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Records in DD' "'"the_SCLDD"'"    '=' SCL.0
   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Records in DD' "'"the_INDEX"'"    '=' INP.0
   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Records in DD' "'"the_APPMASTR"'" '=' APP.0
   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Records in DD' "'"the_LMSTOEND"'" '=' INC.0
   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Records in DD' "'"the_SKIPDD"'"   '=' SKP.0
   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Records in DD' "'"the_SKIPADD"'"  '=' SKA.0
   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Records in DD' "'"the_SPLITS"'"   '=' SPL.0
   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Records in DD' "'"the_FLIBDD"'"   '=' FLIB.0

FORDLIB=""
do kk=1 to FLIB.0 while my_rc=0
   if strip(FLIB.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(FLIB.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   FORDLIB=FORDLIB  " "  word(FLIB.kk,1)
end

split_list= "AHIC "  ,
            "APIB "  ,
            "APPP "  ,
            "BAC  "  ,
            "BPCD "  ,
            "BPFA "  ,
            "CSGC "  ,
            "CSPE "  ,
            "CSQS "  ,
            "CSRE "  ,
            "CSRT "  ,
            "CSUD "  ,
            "CSVB "  ,
            "CSWC "  ,
            "CSWP "  ,
            "CSWS "  ,
            "C7CC "  ,
            "C7VL "  ,
            "C7VM "  ,
            "DMAC "  ,
            "ECES "  ,
            "FDAL "  ,
            "FDBD "  ,
            "FDCI "  ,
            "FDCK "  ,
            "FDDF "  ,
            "FDDI "  ,
            "FDDO "  ,
            "FDEI "  ,
            "FDEX "  ,
            "FDFL "  ,
            "FDFO "  ,
            "FDGL "  ,
            "FDMI "  ,
            "FDOE "  ,
            "FDOH "  ,
            "FDOP "  ,
            "FDRA "  ,
            "FDSA "  ,
            "PAGA "  ,
            "PAGT "  ,
            "PAIC "  ,
            "PAMM "  ,
            "PAMO "  ,
            "PAOP "  ,
            "PAPK "  ,
            "PART "  ,
            "RCPR "
do kk=1 to SPL.0
   if strip(SPL.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(SPL.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   if wordpos(word(SPL.kk,1),split_list)=0 then ,
      split_list=split_list  " "  word(SPL.kk,1)  " "
end

acnt=0
do kk=1 to INC.0
   if strip(INC.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(INC.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   acnt=acnt+1
   CMN.acnt=word(INC.kk,1)
   CMN.acnt.ET=word(INC.kk,2)
   CMN.acnt.EP=word(INC.kk,3)
end
CMN.0=acnt
drop INC.

   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Valid Records in DD' "'"the_LMSTOEND"'" 'is' CMN.0

acnt=0


do kk=1 to SCL.0
   if strip(SCL.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(SCL.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   acnt=acnt+1
   ST.acnt       =word(SCL.kk,1)
   ST.acnt.STYP  =word(SCL.kk,2)
   ST.acnt.SMAX  =word(SCL.kk,3)
   ST.acnt.SJOB  =word(SCL.kk,4)
   ST.acnt.SCNTR =word(SCL.kk,5)

   ST.acnt.SLPFX =the_DPFX  "."   ST.acnt  "."  ST.acnt.STYP  ".V"
/*    YourHQL.ENDV.SYQ.CV.D40423.T2140.ECPYMST.V01                         */
   ST.acnt.SLPFX =the_DPFX  "."   ST.acnt  "."  ST.acnt.STYP  ".V"

   ST.acnt.SADSN =the_DPFX  ".#"  ST.acnt  ".ADD2EN(LOADFROM)"
   ST.acnt.SGDSN =the_DPFX  ".#"  ST.acnt  ".ADD2EN(GENFROM)"
   ST.acnt.SGPSB =the_DPFX  ".#"  ST.acnt  ".ADD2EN(GENPSB)"
   ST.acnt.SGPSO =the_DPFX  ".#"  ST.acnt  ".ADD2EN(GENPSO)"
   ST.acnt.SGMFS =the_DPFX  ".#"  ST.acnt  ".ADD2EN(GENMFS)"
   ST.acnt.SGCODE=the_DPFX  ".#"  ST.acnt  ".ADD2EN(GENCODE)"
   ST.acnt.SGCOPY=the_DPFX  ".#"  ST.acnt  ".ADD2EN(COPYEM)"
   ST.acnt.SGENO =0

   do jj=1 to CMN.0
      if ST.acnt.STYP<>CMN.jj then iterate

      ST.acnt.SETYP=CMN.jj.ET
      ST.acnt.SEPRC=CMN.jj.EP
      ST.acnt.SGENO=wordpos(CMN.jj,generate_order)
   end jj

   if ST.acnt.SEPRC = "DEACT" then iterate

   if ST.acnt.SETYP="COB"   ,
      ST.acnt.SETYP="ASM"   ,
      ST.acnt.SETYP="PLI" ,
      then ST.acnt.SEPRC="COMPILE"
end kk

ST.0=acnt
drop SCL.
drop CMN.

   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Valid Records in DD' "'"the_SCLDD"'" 'is' ST.0

acnt=0
do kk=1 to INP.0
   if strip(INP.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(INP.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   acnt=acnt+1
   MB.acnt=word(INP.kk,1)
   MB.acnt.LIB=word(INP.kk,2)
   MB.acnt.ETYP=word(INP.kk,3)
   MB.acnt.EPRC=word(INP.kk,4)
   if MB.acnt.EPRC = "DEACT" then iterate
   if MB.acnt.ETYP="COB"   ,
      MB.acnt.ETYP="ASM"   ,
      MB.acnt.ETYP="PLI" ,
      then MB.acnt.EPRC="COMPILE"
end
MB.0=acnt
drop INP.

   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Valid Records in DD' "'"the_INDEX"'" 'is' MB.0

do kk=1 to ST.0
   do jj= 1 to MB.0
      if ST.kk.STYP<>MB.jj.LIB then iterate
      ST.kk.SEPRC=MB.jj.EPRC
      ST.kk.SGENO=wordpos(MB.jj.ETYP,generate_order)
      leave
   end
end

lapp=""
do kk=1 to ST.0
   if lapp<>ST.kk then do
      if lapp<>"" then do
          do jj=spos to kk-1
             ST.jj.STPOS=spos
             ST.jj.ENPOS=kk-1
          end
      end
      lapp=ST.kk
      spos=kk
   end
end
do jj=spos to ST.0
   ST.jj.STPOS=spos
   ST.jj.ENPOS=ST.0
end

acnt=0
spos=ST.1.STPOS
epos=ST.1.ENPOS
do while epos <= ST.0
   do ii=0 to words(generate_order)
      do kk=spos to epos
         if ST.kk.SGENO<>ii then iterate
         acnt=acnt+1
         SC.acnt=ST.kk
         SC.acnt.CGENO =ST.kk.SGENO
         SC.acnt.CTYP  =ST.kk.STYP
         SC.acnt.CMAX  =ST.kk.SMAX
         SC.acnt.CJOB  =ST.kk.SJOB
         SC.acnt.CCNTR =ST.kk.SCNTR
         SC.acnt.CLPFX =ST.kk.SLPFX
         SC.acnt.CETYP =ST.kk.SETYP
         SC.acnt.CEPRC =ST.kk.SEPRC
         SC.acnt.CADSN =ST.kk.SADSN
         SC.acnt.CGDSN =ST.kk.SGDSN
         SC.acnt.CGCODE=ST.kk.SGCODE
         SC.acnt.CGCOPY=ST.kk.SGCOPY
         SC.acnt.CGPSB =ST.kk.SGPSB
         SC.acnt.CGPSO =ST.kk.SGPSO
         SC.acnt.CGMFS =ST.kk.SGMFS
         SC.acnt.CSTAGE="P"
         SC.acnt.CGENV ="PROD"
      end
   end
   spos=epos+1
   if spos<ST.0 then epos=ST.spos.ENPOS
                else leave
end
SC.0=ST.0
drop ST.

teslafpos=pos(' TESTLoad',APP.1)
if teslafpos=0 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "TESTLoad header column missing in "the_APPMASTR
   my_rc=error_rc
   return error_rc
end
else do
  teslafpos=teslafpos+1
  teslafend=teslafpos
end
ll=length(APP.1)
done=0
do kk=teslafpos to ll while \done
   if substr(APP.1,kk,1)<>" " then teslafend=teslafend+1
                              else done=1
end
teslaflen=teslafend-teslafpos+1

relfafpos=pos(' RELDefined',APP.1)
if relfafpos=0 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "RELDefined header column missing in "the_APPMASTR
   my_rc=error_rc
   return error_rc
end
else do
  relfafpos=relfafpos+1
  relfafend=relfafpos
end
ll=length(APP.1)
done=0
do kk=relfafpos to ll while \done
   if substr(APP.1,kk,1)<>" " then relfafend=relfafend+1
                              else done=1
end
relfaflen=relfafend-relfafpos+1

descfpos=pos(' SysEnvironments',APP.1)
if descfpos=0 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "SysEnvironments header column missing in "the_APPMASTR
   my_rc=error_rc
   return error_rc
end
else do
  descfpos=descfpos+1
  descfend=descfpos
end
ll=length(APP.1)
done=0
do kk=descfpos to ll while \done
   if substr(APP.1,kk,1)<>" " then descfend=descfend+1
                              else done=1
end
descflen=descfend-descfpos+1


do kk= 2 to APP.0
   if strip(APP.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(APP.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   a=word(APP.kk,1)
   curr_env=" "  substr(APP.kk,descfpos,descflen)  " "
   tesl_env=" "  substr(APP.kk,teslafpos,teslaflen)  " "
   if strip(tesl_env)='-' then tesl_env = ""
   curr_env=tesl_env  curr_env
   found=0
   do jj=1 to words(curr_env) while \found
      w=word(curr_env,jj)
      if substr(w,1,4)<>"TEST" then iterate
      if w="TEST1" then st="A"
      if w="TEST2" then st="B"
      if w="TEST3" then st="C"
      if w="TEST4" then st="D"
      if w="TESTI" then st="R"
      found=1
  end
  if found then do
     do ii=1 to SC.0
         if SC.ii<>a then iterate
         SC.ii.CGENV=w
         SC.ii.CSTAGE=st
      end
   end
end
drop APP.

   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'do_init: End'
   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       ' '

return my_rc
./  ADD  NAME=ENDVTSHY

/*********************************************************************/

/* PROGRAM NAME:           'SDTSJPH.REXX.EXEC(ENDEVOR)' EXEC         */

/* SUPPORT ID:             CDBA                                      */

/* PROGRAM FUNCTION:       MOVE CHANGEMAN DATA TO ENDEVOR            */

/*                                                                   */
/* INPUTS/OUTPUTS:         READ  SDTSJPH.JCL.END(APPL)               */
/*                         READ  SDTSJPH.JCL.END(APPLS)              */
/*                         READ  YourHQL.ENDV.SYX.LMSTOEND.EXEC           */
/*                         READ  YourHQL.ENDV.SYX.LMSTOEND.JCL(LMSTOEND)  */
/*                         READ  YourHQL.CHGMAN.PROD.SERNET.TCPIPORT      */
/*                         WRITE XXXXX.ENDEVOR.SYX.JCL               */
/*                         WRITE XXXXX.ENDEVOR.SYX.REPORT            */
/*                         WRITE XXXXX.ENDEVOR.SYX.SCLCC             */
/*                         WRITE XXXXX.ENDEVOR.SYX.DELETE            */
/*                                                                   */
/* CALLING PROGRAMS:       N/A                                       */
/*                                                                   */
/* EXTERNAL CALLS:         SERXMLRC     (SERENA)                     */
/*                         CMNVNSRD     (CHANGEMAN)                  */
/*                                                                   */
/* RETURN/REASON CODES & DIAGNOSTICS: NONE                           */
/*                                                                   */
/* SPECIAL CONSIDERATIONS: USES REXXTOOLS                            */

SAY 'INF000 - SDTSJPH.REXX.EXEC(ENDEVOR)'

/*********************************************************************/
/*  INITIALIZATION                                                   */
/*********************************************************************/

SYSNAME = MVSVAR('SYSNAME')

IF SYSNAME == 'BAMD'   ,
   SYSNAME == 'CAMD' THEN
    FAC = 'Q'
ELSE
IF SYSNAME == 'NEA1'   ,
   SYSNAME == 'NEB1' THEN
    FAC = 'U'
ELSE
IF SYSNAME == 'SYD9' THEN
    FAC = '9'
ELSE
    FAC = SUBSTR(SYSNAME,3,1)

IF INDEX('ABCGH',FAC) > 0 THEN
    JES = 3
ELSE
    JES = 2

IF FAC == 'Q'   ,
   FAC == 'U' THEN
    DO
        JOB_CARD_ACCT  = '(39200),'
        JOB_CARD_PARMS = ',CLASS=Z,REGION=0M,'
    END
ELSE
    DO
        JOB_CARD_ACCT  = '(2,39200,FMCC1484),'
        JOB_CARD_PARMS = ',MSGCLASS=9,REGION=0M,'
    END

WRKHLVL = 'YourHQL.ENDV.SY'    FAC    '.LMSTOEND'

USERID = SYSVAR('SYSUID')

USERID_PFX = SUBSTR(USERID,1,2)

IF USERID_PFX == 'SD' THEN
    USERID_PFX = 'SW'

GLOBAL_MAX_VERSION = 9

                                     /********************************/
                                     /*  SYNCHRONIZED DATE AND TIME  */
                                     /********************************/

PARSE VALUE DATE('S')    TIME()       WITH ,
            CURRENT_DATE CURRENT_TIME
         /* YYYYMMDD     HH:MM:SS      */

TIMESTAMP = 'DATE:' CURRENT_DATE 'TIME:' CURRENT_TIME

DROP JCL.
JCL_CNT = 6

DROP RPT_APCMHI.
RPT_APCMHI_CNT = 0

DROP RPT_APCMLO.

DROP RPT_APDVHI.
RPT_APDVHI_CNT = 0

DROP RPT_APDVLO.

DROP RPT_BADAPL.
RPT_BADAPL_CNT = 0

RPT_BADCMN_CNT = 0

    DO
        SAY 'ERR001 - JCL FILE - JCL ERROR'
        EXIT 16
    END

JCL_DSN = SYSDSNAME

/*********************************************************************/
/*  READ OVERRIDE FILE                                               */
/*********************************************************************/

IF LISTDSI('OVERRIDE FILE RECALL') <> 0 THEN
    DO
        SAY 'ERR002 - OVERRIDE FILE - JCL ERROR'
        EXIT 16
    END

DROP OVERRIDE.

CALL OFF ERROR

'EXECIO * DISKR OVERRIDE (STEM OVERRIDE. FINIS)'

CALL ON ERROR

IF RC <> 0 THEN
    DO
        SAY 'ERR003 - OVERRIDE FILE - READ ERROR'
        EXIT 16
    END

T          = OVERRIDE.0 + 1
OVERRIDE.T = '9999 999'
OVERRIDE.0 = T

CALL STEMSORT 'OVERRIDE.',1,OVERRIDE.0,'(1,8,CH,A)'

IF RC <> 0 THEN
    DO
        SAY 'ERR004 - SORT ERROR - OVERRIDE. - RC:' RC
        EXIT 16
    END

DO I = 1 TO OVERRIDE.0 - 1
    RPT_OVERID.I = SUBSTR(OVERRIDE.I,1,72)
END

RPT_OVERID_CNT = OVERRIDE.0 - 1

DROP OVERAPL.
OVERAPL_CNT = 0

DROP OVERTYP.

HOLD_APL = LEFT(WORD(OVERRIDE.1,1),4)

DO I = 1 TO OVERRIDE.0
    IF LEFT(WORD(OVERRIDE.I,1),4) /== HOLD_APL THEN
        DO
            OVERAPL_CNT         = OVERAPL_CNT + 1
            OVERAPL.OVERAPL_CNT = HOLD_APL
            OVERTYP.OVERAPL_CNT = '999'
            HOLD_APL            = LEFT(WORD(OVERRIDE.I,1),4)
        END
    OVERAPL_CNT         = OVERAPL_CNT + 1
    OVERAPL.OVERAPL_CNT = LEFT(WORD(OVERRIDE.I,1),4)
    OVERTYP.OVERAPL_CNT = LEFT(WORD(OVERRIDE.I,2),3)
END

OVERAPL.0 = OVERAPL_CNT

OVERAPL_CURR = 1

DROP OVERRIDE.

/*********************************************************************/
/*  READ MIGRATION DATA                                              */
/*********************************************************************/

IF LISTDSI('LMSTOEND FILE RECALL') <> 0 THEN
    DO
        SAY 'ERR005 - LMSTOEND FILE - JCL ERROR'
        EXIT 16
    END

DROP LMSTOEND.

'EXECIO * DISKR LMSTOEND (STEM LMSTOEND. FINIS)'

IF RC <> 0 THEN
    DO
        SAY 'ERR006 - LMSTOEND FILE - READ ERROR'
        EXIT 16

IF LMSTOEND.0 = 0 THEN
    DO
        SAY 'ERR007 - EOF LMSTOEND FILE - EXECUTION TERMINATED'
        EXIT 16
    END

/*********************************************************************/
/*  BUILD TYPE STRING TABLE                                          */
/*********************************************************************/

DROP LRECL_TBL.
LRECL_TBL_CNT = 0

TYP_STR = ''

DO I = 1 TO LMSTOEND.0
    IF SUBSTR(LMSTOEND.I,1,1) == '*' THEN
       ITERATE
    TYP_STR                 = TYP_STR WORD(LMSTOEND.I,1)
    LRECL_TBL_CNT           = LRECL_TBL_CNT + 1
    LRECL_TBL.LRECL_TBL_CNT = WORD(LMSTOEND.I,4)

DROP LMSTOEND.

/*********************************************************************/
/*  READ APPLCM DATA - ALL APPL'S IN CHANGEMAN - MANUAL ENTRY        */

/*  ALL X(4)                                                         */

/*********************************************************************/
/*  READ DUMMUYXML - USED IN CASES WHERE XML DOES NOT WORK           */
/*                   (I.E. FAC#D) - MANUAL ENTRY                     */
/*                                                                   */
/*  DERIVED FROM APPLICATION BASE REPORT:                            */
/*      P;CM;A;A APPLICATION ==> SPACES; LINE COMMAND ==> B          */
/*                                                                   */
/*  APPL          WORD(1) - REQUIRED                                 */
/*  TYP           WORD(2) - REQUIRED                                 */
/*  LIBTYPE       WORD(3) - DEFAULT 7                                */
/*  BASELIBNAME00 WORD(4) - DEFAULT ==> YourHQL.CHGMAN.<APPL>.BASE.<TYP>  */
/*  BASELIBNAME01 WORD(5) - DEFAULT ==> <BASELIBNAME00>.DELTA        */
/*********************************************************************/

IF LISTDSI('DUMMYXML FILE RECALL') <> 0 THEN
    DO
        SAY 'ERR012 - DUMMYXML FILE - JCL ERROR'
        EXIT 16
    END

DROP DUMMYXML.

CALL OFF ERROR

'EXECIO * DISKR DUMMYXML (STEM DUMMYXML. FINIS)'

CALL ON ERROR

IF RC <> 0 THEN
    DO
        SAY 'ERR013 - DUMMYXML FILE - READ ERROR'
        EXIT 16
    END

IF DUMMYXML.0 = 0 THEN
    DUMMYXML_FLAG = 'N'
ELSE
    DO
        DUMMYXML_FLAG = 'Y'
        CALL STEMSORT 'DUMMYXML.',1,DUMMYXML.0,'(1,8,CH,A)'
        IF RC <> 0 THEN
            DO
                SAY 'ERR014 - SORT ERROR - DUMMYXML. - RC:' RC
                EXIT 16
            END
        DO I = 1 TO DUMMYXML.0
            TEMP = SUBSTR(DUMMYXML.I,1,92)
            IF WORDS(TEMP) = 5 THEN
                ITERATE
            ELSE
            IF WORDS(TEMP) = 2 THEN
                DO
                    BASE  = 'YourHQL.CHGMAN.'    ,
                            WORD(TEMP,1)    ,
                            '.BASE.'        ,
                            WORD(TEMP,2)
                    DELTA = BASE        ,
                            '.DELTA'
                    DUMMYXML.I = WORD(TEMP,1)   ,
                                 WORD(TEMP,2)   ,
                                 '7'            ,
                                 LEFT(BASE,30)  ,
                                 LEFT(DELTA,30)
                END
           ELSE
                DO
                    SAY 'ERR015 - TEMP:' TEMP
                    SAY 'ERR015 - MORE LOGIC REQUIRED'
                    EXIT 16
                END
        END
    END

/*********************************************************************/
/*  READ APPLDV DATA - ALL APPL'S IN ENDEVOR - MANUAL ENTRY          */
/*                                           - BY FACILITY           */
/*                                                                   */
/*  X(4) ==> APPL ONLY ON 1 FACILITY                                 */

/*                                       - BY FACILITY               */

/*  APPL'S GOING FROM CHANGEMAN TO ENDEVOR                           */
/*                                                                   */

    DO
        SAY 'ERR022 - EOF APPLCN FILE - EXECUTION TERMINATED'
        EXIT 16
    END

CALL STEMSORT 'APPLCN.',1,APPLCN.0,'(1,5,CH,A)'

    APPLCN_W.I = WORD(APPLCN.I,1)
    APPLCN_4.I = SUBSTR(APPLCN_W.I,1,4)
END

APPLCN_W.0 = APPLCN.0
APPLCN_4.0 = APPLCN.0

T          = APPLCN_W.0 + 1
APPLCN_W.T = '99999'

T          = APPLCN_4.0 + 1
APPLCN_4.T = '9999'

/*********************************************************************/
/*  CHECK CONVERSION APPL'S TO WHAT IS IN ENDEVOR                    */
/*********************************************************************/

CURR_APPLCN_W = 1
CURR_APPLDV_W = 1

DO WHILE APPLCN_W.CURR_APPLCN_W /== '99999'   ,
         APPLDV_W.CURR_APPLDV_W /== '99999'
    IF APPLCN_W.CURR_APPLCN_W = APPLDV_W.CURR_APPLDV_W THEN
        DO
            CURR_APPLCN_W = CURR_APPLCN_W + 1
            CURR_APPLDV_W = CURR_APPLDV_W + 1
        END
    ELSE
    IF APPLCN_W.CURR_APPLCN_W < APPLDV_W.CURR_APPLDV_W THEN
        DO
            RPT_APDVLO_CNT            = RPT_APDVLO_CNT + 1
            RPT_APDVLO.RPT_APDVLO_CNT = APPLCN_W.CURR_APPLCN_W
            CURR_APPLCN_W             = CURR_APPLCN_W + 1
        END
    ELSE
        DO
            RPT_APDVHI_CNT            = RPT_APDVHI_CNT + 1
            RPT_APDVHI.RPT_APDVHI_CNT = APPLDV_W.CURR_APPLDV_W
            CURR_APPLDV_W             = CURR_APPLDV_W + 1
        END
END

DROP APPLCN_W.
DROP APPLDV_W.

/*********************************************************************/
/*  CHECK EXTRACTED APPL'S TO WHAT IS IN CHANGEMAN                   */
/*********************************************************************/

CURR_APPLCN_4 = 1
CURR_APPLCM_W = 1

DO WHILE APPLCN_4.CURR_APPLCN_4 /== '9999'   ,
         APPLCM_W.CURR_APPLCM_W /== '9999'
    IF APPLCN_4.CURR_APPLCN_4 = APPLCM_W.CURR_APPLCM_W THEN
        DO
            CURR_APPLCN_4 = CURR_APPLCN_4 + 1
            CURR_APPLCM_W = CURR_APPLCM_W + 1
        END
    ELSE
    IF APPLCN_4.CURR_APPLCN_4 < APPLCM_W.CURR_APPLCM_W THEN
        DO
            RPT_APCMLO_CNT            = RPT_APCMLO_CNT + 1
            RPT_APCMLO.RPT_APCMLO_CNT = APPLCN_4.CURR_APPLCN_4
            CURR_APPLCN_4             = CURR_APPLCN_4 + 1
        END
    ELSE
        DO
            RPT_APCMHI_CNT            = RPT_APCMHI_CNT + 1
            RPT_APCMHI.RPT_APCMHI_CNT = APPLCM_W.CURR_APPLCM_W
            CURR_APPLCM_W             = CURR_APPLCM_W + 1
        END
END

DROP APPLCN_4.
DROP APPLCM_W.

/*********************************************************************/
/*  PROCESS BY APPL                                                  */
/*********************************************************************/

DROP DELETE.

DELETE.1 = 'SET STOPRC 16 .'

DO I = 1 TO APPLCN.0
    CALL S100_PROCESS_APPL WORD(APPLCN.I,1)

DROP APPLCN.

    APPL_FOUND_FLAG = 'Y'

CALL OFF ERROR

'EXECIO * DISKW DELETE (STEM DELETE. FINIS)'

CALL ON ERROR

IF RC <> 0 THEN
    DO
        SAY 'ERR024 - DELETE FILE - WRITE ERROR'
        EXIT 16
    END

DROP DELETE.

/*  WRITE SCL CONTROL CARDS                                          */

CALL OFF ERROR

'EXECIO * DISKW SCLCC (STEM SCLCC. FINIS)'

CALL ON ERROR

IF RC <> 0 THEN
    DO
        SAY 'ERR025 - SCLCC FILE - WRITE ERROR'
        EXIT 16
    END

/*********************************************************************/
/*  REPORT                                                           */
/*********************************************************************/

DROP REPORT.
REPORT_CNT = 0

/*********************************************************************/
/*  PROCESS APCMHI                                                   */
/*********************************************************************/

RPT_APCMHI.0 = RPT_APCMHI_CNT

REPORT_CNT        = REPORT_CNT + 1
REPORT.REPORT_CNT = 'APPLICATIONS FOUND IN MANUAL CHANGEMAN LIST'     ,
                                                    RIGHT(TIMESTAMP,35)

REPORT_CNT        = REPORT_CNT + 1
REPORT.REPORT_CNT = 'BUT NOT IN CONVERSION LIST'

REPORT_CNT        = REPORT_CNT + 1
REPORT.REPORT_CNT = ' '

IF RPT_APCMHI.0 = 0 THEN
    DO
        REPORT_CNT        = REPORT_CNT + 1
        REPORT.REPORT_CNT = 'NONE'
    END
ELSE
    DO
        DO I = 1 TO RPT_APCMHI.0
            REPORT_CNT        = REPORT_CNT + 1
            REPORT.REPORT_CNT = RPT_APCMHI.I
        END
        REPORT_CNT        = REPORT_CNT + 1
        REPORT.REPORT_CNT = ' '
        REPORT_CNT        = REPORT_CNT + 1
        REPORT.REPORT_CNT = 'TOTAL:' RPT_APCMHI.0
    END

DROP RPT_APCMHI.

REPORT_CNT        = REPORT_CNT + 1
REPORT.REPORT_CNT = ' '

REPORT_CNT        = REPORT_CNT + 1
REPORT.REPORT_CNT = '**************************************'

REPORT.REPORT_CNT = ' '

/*********************************************************************/

REPORT.REPORT_CNT = 'APPLICATIONS FOUND IN CONVERSION LIST'

/*********************************************************************/

    DO

                REPORT.REPORT_CNT = '    '                 ,
                                    SUBSTR(RPT_MSCPRB.I,6)
            ELSE

                END
        END
