REPORT_CNT        = REPORT_CNT + 1
REPORT.REPORT_CNT = ' '

/*********************************************************************/
/*  GENERATE MEMBER COUNT REPORT FROM SCLCC'S                        */
/*********************************************************************/

REPORT_CNT        = REPORT_CNT + 1
REPORT.REPORT_CNT = 'MEMBER COUNTS BY APPLICATION/TYPE'

REPORT_CNT        = REPORT_CNT + 1
REPORT.REPORT_CNT = ' '

IF SCLCC.0 = 0 THEN
    DO
        REPORT_CNT        = REPORT_CNT + 1
        REPORT.REPORT_CNT = 'NO APPLICATION - TYPES SELECTED'
    END
ELSE
    DO
        REPORT_CNT        = REPORT_CNT + 1
        REPORT.REPORT_CNT = 'APPL  TYP MBR CNT'
        REPORT_CNT        = REPORT_CNT + 1
        REPORT.REPORT_CNT = '----- --- -------'
        TOTAL             = 0
        SUBTOT            = 0
        DO I = 1 TO SCLCC.0
            TEMP              = SCLCC.I
            IF I = 1 THEN
                HOLD_APPL = WORD(TEMP,1)
            APPL = WORD(TEMP,1)
            MBRS = WORD(TEMP,5)
            IF APPL /== HOLD_APPL THEN
                DO
                    REPORT.REPORT_CNT = REPORT.REPORT_CNT             ,
                                  RIGHT('SUBTOTAL:',12) RIGHT(SUBTOT,7)
                    TOTAL             = TOTAL + SUBTOT
                    SUBTOT            = 0
                    HOLD_APPL         = APPL
                    REPORT_CNT        = REPORT_CNT + 1
                    REPORT.REPORT_CNT = ' '
                END
            REPORT_CNT        = REPORT_CNT + 1
            REPORT.REPORT_CNT = LEFT(APPL,5)            ,
                                LEFT(WORD(TEMP,2),3)    ,
                                RIGHT(MBRS,7)
            SUBTOT            = SUBTOT + MBRS
        END
        REPORT.REPORT_CNT = REPORT.REPORT_CNT                         ,
                                  RIGHT('SUBTOTAL:',12) RIGHT(SUBTOT,7)
        TOTAL             = TOTAL + SUBTOT
        REPORT_CNT        = REPORT_CNT + 1
        REPORT.REPORT_CNT = ' '
        REPORT_CNT        = REPORT_CNT + 1
        REPORT.REPORT_CNT = 'TOTAL:' RIGHT(TOTAL,10)
    END

DROP SCLCC.

/*********************************************************************/
/*  WRITE REPORT                                                     */
/*********************************************************************/

REPORT.0 = REPORT_CNT

CALL OFF ERROR

'EXECIO * DISKW REPORT (STEM REPORT. FINIS)'

CALL ON ERROR

IF RC <> 0 THEN
    DO
        SAY 'ERR026 - REPORT FILE - WRITE ERROR'
        EXIT 16
    END

DROP REPORT.

/*********************************************************************/
/*  IF NO APPLICATIONS FOUND - ABEND JOB                             */
/*********************************************************************/

IF APPL_FOUND_FLAG == 'N' THEN
    DO
        SAY 'ERR027 - NO APPLICATIONS FOUND - TERMINATE PROCESSING'
        EXIT 16
    END

EXIT

/*$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$*/

/*********************************************************************/
/*  FROM MAIN                                                        */
/*                                                                   */
/*  PROCESS APPL                                                     */
/*********************************************************************/

S100_PROCESS_APPL:

PROCEDURE ,                             /* UNEXPOSED VARIABLES LOCAL */
    EXPOSE DELETE.            ,         /* COMMON - BUT SCOPE        */
           DELETE_CNT         ,         /*              DEPENDENT    */
           DUMMYXML.          ,
           DUMMYXML_FLAG      ,
           FAC                ,
           GLOBAL_MAX_VERSION ,
           JCL.               ,
           JCL_CNT            ,
           JCL_DSN            ,
           JES                ,
           JOB_CARD_ACCT      ,
           JOB_CARD_PARMS     ,
           LRECL_TBL.         ,
           OVERAPL.           ,
           OVERAPL_CURR       ,
           OVERTYP.           ,
           RPT_SKPPDS.        ,
           RPT_SKPPDS_CNT     ,
           RPT_NEWTYP.        ,
           RPT_NEWTYP_CNT     ,
           RPT_SKPTYP.        ,
           RPT_SKPTYP_CNT     ,
           RPT_BADAPL.        ,
           RPT_BADAPL_CNT     ,
           RPT_BADCMN.        ,
           RPT_BADCMN_CNT     ,
           RPT_DIFNAM.        ,
           RPT_DIFNAM_CNT     ,
           RPT_MISMEM.        ,
           RPT_MISMEM_CNT     ,
           RPT_MSCPRB.        ,
           RPT_MSCPRB_CNT     ,
           RPT_NO_CAT.        ,
           RPT_NO_CAT_CNT     ,
           RPT_NO_MEM.        ,
           RPT_NO_MEM_CNT     ,
           SCLCC.             ,
           SCLCC_CNT          ,
           TIMESTAMP          ,
           TYP_STR            ,
           USERID             ,
           USERID_PFX         ,
           WRKHLVL

ARG APPL                                            /* CALL BY VALUE */

APPL_1_4 = SUBSTR(APPL,1,4)

IF DUMMYXML_FLAG == 'N' THEN
    DO
        XML.              = ''
        STEM              = 'XML.'
        XML.SUBSYS        = FAC
        XML.PRODUCT       = 'CMN'
        XML.USERID        = USERID
        XML.APPLNAME      = APPL_1_4
        XML.SERVICE       = 'BASELIB'
        XML.SCOPE         = 'SERVICE'
        XML.MESSAGE       = 'LIST'
        RC = 0
        CALL OFF ERROR
        ADDRESS LINKMVS 'SERXMLRC STEM'
        CALL ON ERROR
        IF RC > 0 THEN
            DO
                RPT_BADAPL_CNT            = RPT_BADAPL_CNT + 1
                RPT_BADAPL.RPT_BADAPL_CNT = APPL_1_4
                RETURN
            END
    END
ELSE
    DO
        DROP XML.RESULT.
        DROP XML.LIBTYPE.
        DROP XML.BASELIBSTORAGEMEANS.
        DROP XML.BASELIBNAME00.
        DROP XML.BASELIBNAME01.
        DO I = 1 TO DUMMYXML.0 ,
           WHILE LEFT(WORD(DUMMYXML.I,1),4) /== APPL_1_4
        END
        IF I > DUMMYXML.0 THEN
            DO
                RPT_BADAPL_CNT            = RPT_BADAPL_CNT + 1
                RPT_BADAPL.RPT_BADAPL_CNT = APPL_1_4
                RETURN
            END
        K = 0
        DO J = I TO DUMMYXML.0 ,
           WHILE LEFT(WORD(DUMMYXML.J,1),4) == APPL_1_4
            K                         = K + 1
            XML.LIBTYPE.K             = WORD(DUMMYXML.J,2)
            XML.BASELIBSTORAGEMEANS.K = WORD(DUMMYXML.J,3)
            XML.BASELIBNAME00.K       = WORD(DUMMYXML.J,4)
            XML.BASELIBNAME01.K       = WORD(DUMMYXML.J,5)
        END
        XML.RESULT.0 = J - I
    END

APPL_1_4_IDX1 = 0
APPL_1_4_IDX2 = 39

DO I = 1 TO XML.RESULT.0
    J = WORDPOS(XML.LIBTYPE.I,TYP_STR)
    IF J > 0 THEN
        IF (XML.BASELIBSTORAGEMEANS.I = 7)        ,
           (FAC                       == 'A'    & ,
            APPL_1_4                  == 'CPSE' & ,
            XML.LIBTYPE.I             == 'SEG'  & ,
            XML.BASELIBSTORAGEMEANS.I  = 6)     THEN
            CALL S110_PROCESS_APPL_ACTIVE XML.LIBTYPE.I       ,
                                          XML.BASELIBNAME00.I ,
                                          XML.BASELIBNAME01.I
        ELSE
        IF XML.BASELIBSTORAGEMEANS.I = 6 THEN
            DO
                RPT_SKPPDS_CNT            = RPT_SKPPDS_CNT + 1
                RPT_SKPPDS.RPT_SKPPDS_CNT = APPL_1_4      ,
                                            XML.LIBTYPE.I
            END
        ELSE
            DO
                RPT_NEWTYP_CNT            = RPT_NEWTYP_CNT + 1
                RPT_NEWTYP.RPT_NEWTYP_CNT = APPL_1_4      ,
                                            XML.LIBTYPE.I
            END
    ELSE
        DO
            RPT_SKPTYP_CNT            = RPT_SKPTYP_CNT + 1
            RPT_SKPTYP.RPT_SKPTYP_CNT = APPL_1_4      ,
                                        XML.LIBTYPE.I
        END
END

/*********************************************************************/
/*  CREATE ENDEVOR DELETE LOGIC                                      */
/*********************************************************************/

DELETE_CNT        = DELETE_CNT + 1
DELETE.DELETE_CNT = 'TRANSFER ELEMENT ''*'''

DELETE_CNT        = DELETE_CNT + 1
DELETE.DELETE_CNT = '  FROM ENVIRONMENT ''PROD'' SYSTEM '''    ,
                    APPL                                       ,
                    ''' SUBSYSTEM ''BASE'''

DELETE_CNT        = DELETE_CNT + 1
DELETE.DELETE_CNT = '    TYPE ''*'' STAGE P'

DELETE_CNT        = DELETE_CNT + 1
DELETE.DELETE_CNT = '  TO DDNAME DUMMY'

DELETE_CNT        = DELETE_CNT + 1
DELETE.DELETE_CNT = '  OPTIONS BYPASS DELETE PROCESSOR'

DELETE_CNT        = DELETE_CNT + 1
DELETE.DELETE_CNT = '          IGNORE GENERATE FAILED'

DELETE_CNT        = DELETE_CNT + 1
DELETE.DELETE_CNT = '          OVERRIDE SIGNOUT'

DELETE_CNT        = DELETE_CNT + 1
DELETE.DELETE_CNT = '          CCID     ''ADMIN DELETE'''

DELETE_CNT        = DELETE_CNT + 1
DELETE.DELETE_CNT = '          COMMENTS ''DELETE PROD INVENTORY'''

DELETE_CNT        = DELETE_CNT + 1
DELETE.DELETE_CNT = ' .'

RETURN

/*$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$*/

/*********************************************************************/
/*  FROM S100                                                        */
/*                                                                   */
/*  MONTHLY REPORT                                                   */
/*********************************************************************/

S110_PROCESS_APPL_ACTIVE:

PROCEDURE ,                             /* UNEXPOSED VARIABLES LOCAL */
    EXPOSE APPL               ,         /* COMMON - BUT SCOPE        */
           APPL_1_4           ,         /*              DEPENDENT    */
           APPL_1_4_IDX1      ,
           APPL_1_4_IDX2      ,
           FAC                ,
           GLOBAL_MAX_VERSION ,
           JCL.               ,
           JCL_CNT            ,
           JCL_DSN            ,
           JES                ,
           JOB_CARD_ACCT      ,
           JOB_CARD_PARMS     ,
           LRECL_TBL.         ,
           OVERAPL.           ,
           OVERAPL_CURR       ,
           OVERTYP.           ,
           RPT_BADAPL.        ,
           RPT_BADAPL_CNT     ,
           RPT_BADCMN.        ,
           RPT_BADCMN_CNT     ,
           RPT_DIFNAM.        ,
           RPT_DIFNAM_CNT     ,
           RPT_MISMEM.        ,
           RPT_MISMEM_CNT     ,
           RPT_MSCPRB.        ,
           RPT_MSCPRB_CNT     ,
           RPT_NO_CAT.        ,
           RPT_NO_CAT_CNT     ,
           RPT_NO_MEM.        ,
           RPT_NO_MEM_CNT     ,
           SCLCC.             ,
           SCLCC_CNT          ,
           TIMESTAMP          ,
           TYP_STR            ,
           USERID_PFX         ,
           WRKHLVL

ARG TYP    ,                                        /* CALL BY VALUE */
    CMNBAS ,
    CMNDLT

BASE = 'YourHQL.CHGMAN.'           ,
       STRIP(APPL_1_4,'T')    ,
       '.BASE.'               ,
       TYP

IF CMNBAS /== BASE THEN
    DO
        RPT_DIFNAM_CNT            = RPT_DIFNAM_CNT + 1
        RPT_DIFNAM.RPT_DIFNAM_CNT = APPL_1_4        ,
                                    TYP             ,
                                    LEFT(CMNBAS,35) ,
                                    '- BASE'
    END

DELTA = BASE        ,
        '.DELTA'

IF CMNDLT /== DELTA THEN
    DO
        RPT_DIFNAM_CNT            = RPT_DIFNAM_CNT + 1
        RPT_DIFNAM.RPT_DIFNAM_CNT = APPL_1_4        ,
                                    TYP             ,
                                    LEFT(CMNDLT,35) ,
                                    '- DELTA'
    END

DSN_PROBLEM = 'N'

MAX_VERSION = 0

STEP = 100

CALL S120_PROCESS_V00

IF DSN_PROBLEM == 'Y' THEN
    RETURN

DO WHILE LEFT(OVERAPL.OVERAPL_CURR,4) << APPL_1_4
    OVERAPL_CURR = OVERAPL_CURR + 1
END

IF APPL_1_4 == LEFT(OVERAPL.OVERAPL_CURR,4) THEN
    DO
        DO I = OVERAPL_CURR TO OVERAPL.0 ,
           WHILE APPL_1_4 == LEFT(OVERAPL.I,4)
            IF TYP = OVERTYP.I THEN
                DO
                    CALL S900_WRITE_JCL
                    RETURN
                END
            IF OVERTYP.I == '999' THEN
                LEAVE
        END
        IF I > OVERAPL.0 THEN
            DO
                SAY 'ERR110 - LOGIC ERROR - APPL:' APPL_1_4 ,
                    '- TYP:' TYP
                EXIT 16
            END
    END

IF LISTDSI(''''CMNDLT''' RECALL') <> 0 THEN
    DO
        IF SYSREASON = 5 THEN
            DO
                RPT_NO_CAT_CNT            = RPT_NO_CAT_CNT + 1
                RPT_NO_CAT.RPT_NO_CAT_CNT = APPL_1_4        ,
                                            LEFT(CMNDLT,35) ,
                                            '- DELTA'
                CALL S900_WRITE_JCL
                RETURN
            END
        ELSE
            DO
                SAY 'ERR111 - LOGIC ERROR - APPL:' APPL_1_4 ,
                    '- DSN:' CMNDLT '- SYSREASON:' SYSREASON
                EXIT 16
            END
    END

CALL OFF ERROR

'ALLOC F(DELTALIB) DA('''    CMNDLT    ''') SHR REUSE'

CALL ON ERROR

IF RC > 0 THEN
    DO
        SAY 'ERR112 - ALLOC DELTSLIB ERROR - RC:' RC
        EXIT 16
    END

IF LISTDSI('SYSPRIN1 FILE RECALL') <> 0 THEN
    DO
        SAY 'ERR113 - SYSPRIN1 FILE - JCL ERROR'
        EXIT 16
    END

SYSPRIN1_DSN = SYSDSNAME

CALL OFF ERROR

'ALLOC F(SYSPRINT) DA('''SYSPRIN1_DSN''') SHR REUSE'

CALL ON ERROR

IF RC <> 0 THEN
    DO
        SAY 'ERR114 - SYSPRINT - ALLOC - RC:' RC
        EXIT 16
    END

PARM = 'VERSION(-0),STATS,ALLMEM'

CALL OFF ERROR

'CALL ''YourHQL.CHGMAN.PROD.VENDOR.LINKLIB.V5(CMNVNSRD)''' ,
          '''VERSION(-0),STATS,ALLMEM'''

CALL ON ERROR

IF RC > 0 THEN
    DO
        RPT_BADCMN_CNT            = RPT_BADCMN_CNT + 1
        RPT_BADCMN.RPT_BADCMN_CNT = APPL_1_4                    ,
                                    LEFT(CMNDLT,35)             ,
                                    '- DELTA - CMNVNSRD RC:' RC
        'ALLOC F(SYSPRINT) DA(*) SHR REUSE'
        CALL S900_WRITE_JCL
        RETURN
    END
ELSE
IF RC < 0 THEN
    DO
        SAY 'ERR115 - CMNVNSRD FAILED - RC:' RC
        SAY 'ERR115 - ADD:' APPL_1_4 TYP
        SAY 'ERR115 - TO THE OVERRIDE FILE'
        EXIT 16
    END

CALL OFF ERROR

'ALLOC F(SYSPRINT) DA(*) SHR REUSE'

CALL ON ERROR

IF RC <> 0 THEN
    DO
        SAY 'ERR116 - SYSPRINT - ALLOC - RC:' RC
        EXIT
    END

DROP SYSPRIN1.

CALL OFF ERROR

'EXECIO * DISKR SYSPRIN1 (STEM SYSPRIN1. FINIS)'

CALL ON ERROR

IF RC <> 0 THEN
    DO
        SAY 'ERR117 - SYSPRIN1 FILE - READ ERROR'
        EXIT 16
    END

IF SYSPRIN1.0 = 0 THEN
    DO
        SAY 'ERR118 - EOF SYSPRIN1 FILE - EXECUTION TERMINATED'
        EXIT 16
    END

DROP MEMBER_VER.
MEMBER_VER_CNT = 0

DO I = 1 TO SYSPRIN1.0
    TEMP = SYSPRIN1.I
    IF SUBSTR(TEMP,1,1) == '0' THEN
        ITERATE
    IF WORD(TEMP,1) == 'CMNVN25I' THEN
        HOLD_MEMBER = WORD(TEMP,7)
    ELSE
    IF WORD(TEMP,1) == 'CMNVN68I' THEN
        DO
            MEMBER_VER_CNT = MEMBER_VER_CNT + 1
            MEMBER_VER.MEMBER_VER_CNT = LEFT(HOLD_MEMBER,10)          ,
                                        TRANSLATE(WORD(TEMP,7),'0','-')
        END
END

MEMBER_VER.0 = MEMBER_VER_CNT

MISSING_MEMBER = 'N'

DO I = 1 TO MEMBER_VER.0
    IF WORDPOS(WORD(MEMBER_VER.I,1),MEM) > 0 THEN
        ITERATE
    RPT_MISMEM_CNT            = RPT_MISMEM_CNT + 1
    RPT_MISMEM.RPT_MISMEM_CNT = APPL_1_4                 ,
                                LEFT(CMNBAS,35)          ,
                                '- BASE MISSING MEMBER:' ,
                                WORD(MEMBER_VER.I,1)
    MISSING_MEMBER = 'Y'
END

IF MISSING_MEMBER == 'Y' THEN
    DO
        CALL S900_WRITE_JCL
        RETURN
    END

I = WORDPOS(TYP,TYP_STR)

IF I = 0 THEN
    DO
        SAY 'ERR119 - DATA ERROR - TYP:' TYP
        EXIT 16
    END

LRECL = LRECL_TBL.I

DO I = 1 TO MEMBER_VER.0
    VERSION = WORD(MEMBER_VER.I,2) + 0
    IF MAX_VERSION < VERSION THEN
        MAX_VERSION = VERSION
END

IF MAX_VERSION > GLOBAL_MAX_VERSION THEN
    MAX_VERSION = GLOBAL_MAX_VERSION

DO I = 1 TO MAX_VERSION
    CALL S130_PROCESS_V01_VXX I
END

CALL S900_WRITE_JCL

RETURN

/*$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$*/

/*********************************************************************/
/*  FROM S110                                                        */
/*                                                                   */
/*  PROCESS APPL - V00                                               */
/*********************************************************************/

S120_PROCESS_V00:

PROCEDURE ,                             /* UNEXPOSED VARIABLES LOCAL */
    EXPOSE APPL_1_4       ,             /* COMMON - BUT SCOPE        */
           CMNBAS         ,             /*              DEPENDENT    */
           DSN_PROBLEM    ,
           JCL.           ,
           JCL_CNT        ,
           MEM            ,
           MEMCNT         ,
           RPT_MSCPRB.    ,
           RPT_MSCPRB_CNT ,
           RPT_NO_CAT.    ,
           RPT_NO_CAT_CNT ,
           RPT_NO_MEM.    ,
           RPT_NO_MEM_CNT ,
           SPACE_DIRBLKS  ,
           SPACE_SECONDS  ,
           SPACE_UNITS    ,
           SPACE_USED     ,
           STEP           ,
           TYP            ,
           WRKHLVL

IF LISTDSI(''''CMNBAS''' DIRECTORY RECALL') <> 0 THEN
    IF SYSREASON = 5 THEN
        DO
            RPT_NO_CAT_CNT            = RPT_NO_CAT_CNT + 1
            RPT_NO_CAT.RPT_NO_CAT_CNT = APPL_1_4        ,
                                        LEFT(CMNBAS,35) ,
                                        '- BASE'
            DSN_PROBLEM               = 'Y'
            RETURN
        END
    ELSE
        DO
            SAY 'ERR120 - LOGIC ERROR - APPL:' APPL_1_4 ,
                '- DSN:' CMNBAS '- SYSREASON:' SYSREASON
            EXIT 16
        END

PARSE VALUE LISTM(''''CMNBAS'''') WITH RC MEMCNT MEM

IF RC <> 0 THEN
    DO
        RPT_MSCPRB_CNT = RPT_MSCPRB_CNT + 1
        IF RC = 8 THEN
            RPT_MSCPRB.RPT_MSCPRB_CNT = APPL_1_4             ,
                                        LEFT(CMNBAS,35)      ,
                                        '- RACF PROBLEM (?)'
        ELSE
            DO
                SAY 'ERR121 - LOGIC ERROR - APPL:' APPL_1_4 ,
                    '- DSN:' CMNBAS '- LISTM RC:' RC
                EXIT 16
            END
        DSN_PROBLEM = 'Y'
        RETURN
    END

IF MEMCNT = 0 THEN
    DO
        RPT_NO_MEM_CNT            = RPT_NO_MEM_CNT + 1
        RPT_NO_MEM.RPT_NO_MEM_CNT = APPL_1_4 ,
                                    CMNBAS
        DSN_PROBLEM = 'Y'
        RETURN
    END

IF SYSUNITS == 'CYLINDER' THEN
    SPACE_UNITS = 'CYL'
ELSE
IF SYSUNITS == 'TRACK' THEN
    SPACE_UNITS = 'TRK'
ELSE
IF SYSUNITS == 'BLOCK' THEN
    SPACE_UNITS = SYSBLKSIZE
ELSE
    DO
        SAY 'ERR122 - LOGIC ERROR - APPL:' APPL_1_4 ,
            '- DSN:' CMNBAS '- SYSUNITS:' SYSUNITS
        EXIT 16
    END

IF SYSUSED == 'N/A' THEN
    SPACE_USED = SYSALLOC + 1
ELSE
    SPACE_USED = SYSUSED + 1

SPACE_SECONDS = SYSSECONDS

IF SYSUDIRBLK == 'N/A' THEN
    SPACE_DIRBLKS = ((MEMCNT % 6 + 1) % 45 + 1) * 45 - 1
ELSE
    SPACE_DIRBLKS = SYSUDIRBLK + 1

OUTDD_DSN = WRKHLVL                ,
            '.'                    ,
            STRIP(APPL_1_4,'T')    ,
            '.'                    ,
            TYP                    ,
            '.V00'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//*'

STEP = STEP + 1

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//STEP'                                              ,
              LEFT(STEP,4)                                          ,
              'EXEC PGM=IEFBR14,COND=(0,NE)               ALLOC'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//DD1      DD DSN='    ,
              OUTDD_DSN               ,
              ','

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//             SPACE=(1,1),DISP=(MOD,CATLG)'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//*'

STEP = STEP + 1

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//STEP'                                               ,
              LEFT(STEP,4)                                           ,
              'EXEC PGM=IEFBR14,COND=(0,NE)               DELETE'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//DD1      DD DSN='    ,
              OUTDD_DSN               ,
              ','

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//             DISP=(OLD,DELETE)'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//*'

STEP = STEP + 1

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//STEP'                   ,
              STEP                       ,
              'EXEC PGM=IEBCOPY,COND=(0,NE),PARM=''WORK=4M'''

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//SYSPRINT DD SYSOUT=*'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//SYSUT3   DD UNIT=SYSDA,SPACE=(CYL,(10,10))'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//SYSUT4   DD UNIT=SYSDA,SPACE=(CYL,(10,10))'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//INDD     DD DSN='    ,
              CMNBAS                  ,
              ',DISP=SHR'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//OUTDD    DD DSN='    ,
              OUTDD_DSN               ,
              ','

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//            UNIT=SYSDA,MGMTCLAS=ENDV1,'    ,
              'DISP=(NEW,CATLG),'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//            SPACE=('    ,
              SPACE_UNITS                ,
              ',('                       ,
              SPACE_USED                 ,
              ','                        ,
              SPACE_SECONDS              ,
              ','                        ,
              SPACE_DIRBLKS              ,
              '),RLSE),DCB=*.INDD'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//SYSIN    DD *'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '  COPY I=INDD,O=OUTDD'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '/*'

RETURN

/*$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$*/

/*********************************************************************/
/*  FROM S110                                                        */
/*                                                                   */
/*  PROCESS APPL - V01 THRU V-MAX-VERSION                            */
/*********************************************************************/

S130_PROCESS_V01_VXX:

PROCEDURE ,                             /* UNEXPOSED VARIABLES LOCAL */
    EXPOSE APPL_1_4       ,             /* COMMON - BUT SCOPE        */
           CMNBAS         ,             /*              DEPENDENT    */
           CMNDLT         ,
           JCL.           ,
           JCL_CNT        ,
           LRECL          ,
           MEMBER_VER.    ,
           RPT_NO_CAT.    ,
           RPT_NO_CAT_CNT ,
           SPACE_DIRBLKS  ,
           SPACE_SECONDS  ,
           SPACE_UNITS    ,
           SPACE_USED     ,
           STEP           ,
           TYP            ,
           WRKHLVL

ARG VERSION                                         /* CALL BY VALUE */

STAGELIB_DSN = WRKHLVL                 ,
               '.'                     ,
               STRIP(APPL_1_4,'T')     ,
               '.'                     ,
               TYP                     ,
               '.V'                    ,
               RIGHT(VERSION,2,'0')

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//*'

STEP = STEP + 1

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//STEP'                                              ,
              LEFT(STEP,4)                                          ,
              'EXEC PGM=IEFBR14,COND=(0,NE)               ALLOC'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//DD1      DD DSN='    ,
              STAGELIB_DSN            ,
              ','

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//             SPACE=(1,1),DISP=(MOD,CATLG)'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//*'

STEP = STEP + 1

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//STEP'                                               ,
              LEFT(STEP,4)                                           ,
              'EXEC PGM=IEFBR14,COND=(0,NE)               DELETE'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//DD1      DD DSN='    ,
              STAGELIB_DSN            ,
              ','

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//             DISP=(OLD,DELETE)'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//*'

STEP = STEP + 1

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//STEP'                                                ,
              LEFT(STEP,4)                                            ,
              'EXEC PGM=IEFBR14,COND=(0,NE)               REALLOC'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//DD1      DD DSN='    ,
              STAGELIB_DSN            ,
              ','

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//            UNIT=SYSDA,MGMTCLAS=ENDV1,'    ,
              'DISP=(NEW,CATLG),'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//            SPACE=('      ,
              SPACE_UNITS                  ,
              ',('                         ,
              SPACE_USED                   ,
              ','                          ,
              SPACE_SECONDS                ,
              ','                          ,
              SPACE_DIRBLKS                ,
              '),RLSE),RECFM=FB,LRECL='    ,
              LRECL

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//*'

STEP = STEP + 1

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//STEP'                            ,
              LEFT(STEP,4)                        ,
              'EXEC PGM=CMNUPDAT,COND=(0,NE),'    ,
              'PARM=''COPY,VERSION(-'             ,
              RIGHT(VERSION,2,'0')                ,
              ')'''

HOLD_STEP_JCL_CNT = JCL_CNT

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//STEPLIB  DD'                                 ,
              'DSN=YourHQL.CHGMAN.PROD.VENDOR.LINKLIB.V5,DISP=SHR'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//STAGELIB DD DSN='    ,
              STAGELIB_DSN            ,
              ',DISP=SHR'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//BASELIB  DD DSN='    ,
              CMNBAS                  ,
              ',DISP=SHR'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//DELTALIB DD DSN='    ,
              CMNDLT                  ,
              ',DISP=SHR'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//CMNUPDAT DD DUMMY'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//SYSPRINT DD SYSOUT=*'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//SYSIN    DD *'

HOLD_SYSIN_JCL_CNT = JCL_CNT

MEMBER_CNT     = 0
STEP_ALPHA_CNT = 0

DO I = 1 TO MEMBER_VER.0
    IF WORD(MEMBER_VER.I,2) >= VERSION THEN
        DO
            MEMBER_CNT = MEMBER_CNT + 1
            IF MEMBER_CNT > 5000 THEN
                DO
                    JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
                    JCL.JCL_CNT = '/*'
                    JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
                    JCL.JCL_CNT = '//*'
                    STEP_ALPHA_CNT = STEP_ALPHA_CNT + 1
                    TEMP           = JCL.HOLD_STEP_JCL_CNT
                    JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
                    JCL.JCL_CNT = SUBSTR(TEMP,1,9)                    ,
                                  SUBSTR('BCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ', ,
                                          STEP_ALPHA_CNT,1)           ,
                                  SUBSTR(TEMP,11)
                    DO J = HOLD_STEP_JCL_CNT + 1 TO HOLD_SYSIN_JCL_CNT
                        JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
                        JCL.JCL_CNT = JCL.J
                    END
                    MEMBER_CNT = 1
                END
            JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
            JCL.JCL_CNT = '   ' WORD(MEMBER_VER.I,1)
        END
END

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '/*'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//*'

STEP = STEP + 1

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//STEP'                                          ,
              LEFT(STEP,4)                                      ,
              'EXEC PGM=IKJEFT1B,COND=(0,NE),PARM=''RLSE''' ,
              'RLSE SPACE'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//STEPLIB  DD DSN=SYSSD.REXX.EXEC.ENDEVOR.LOAD,DISP=SHR'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//SYSPRINT DD SYSOUT=*'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//SYSTSPRT DD SYSOUT=*'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//SYSTSIN  DD DUMMY'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//DDNAME   DD DSN='    ,
              STAGELIB_DSN            ,
              ','

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//            DISP=SHR,SPACE=(0,0,RLSE)'

RETURN

/*$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$*/

/*********************************************************************/
/*  FROM  100                                                        */
/*                                                                   */
/*  WRITE JCL                                                        */
/*********************************************************************/

S900_WRITE_JCL:

PROCEDURE ,                             /* UNEXPOSED VARIABLES LOCAL */
    EXPOSE APPL           ,             /* COMMON - BUT SCOPE        */
           APPL_1_4       ,             /*              DEPENDENT    */
           APPL_1_4_IDX1  ,
           APPL_1_4_IDX2  ,
           DSN_PROBLEM    ,
           JCL.           ,
           JCL_CNT        ,
           JCL_DSN        ,
           JES            ,
           JOB_CARD_ACCT  ,
           JOB_CARD_PARMS ,
           MAX_VERSION    ,
           MEMCNT         ,
           SCLCC.         ,
           SCLCC_CNT      ,
           TIMESTAMP      ,
           TYP            ,
           USERID_PFX

IF APPL_1_4_IDX2 > 38 THEN
    DO
        APPL_1_4_IDX2 = 0
        APPL_1_4_IDX1 = APPL_1_4_IDX1 + 1
        IF APPL_1_4_IDX1 > 38 THEN
            DO
                SAY 'ERR900 - NEED TO INCREASE JOB CHARACTERS'
                EXIT 16
            END
    END

APPL_1_4_IDX2 = APPL_1_4_IDX2 + 1

SUFFIX = SUBSTR('ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ0123456789#$@',            ,
                                                  APPL_1_4_IDX1,1)    ,
         SUBSTR('ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ0123456789#$@',            ,
                                                  APPL_1_4_IDX2,1)

IF SUFFIX == 'AA' THEN
    SUFFIX = 'A'

IF DSN_PROBLEM == 'Y' THEN
    JOB_NAME = 'SX'                   ,
               STRIP(APPL_1_4,'T')    ,
               SUFFIX
ELSE
    JOB_NAME = USERID_PFX             ,
               STRIP(APPL_1_4,'T')    ,
               SUFFIX

SAY 'INF900 -' APPL_1_4 TYP '- MAX VERSION:' MAX_VERSION ,
                            '- JOB NAME:' JOB_NAME

SCLCC_CNT       = SCLCC_CNT + 1
SCLCC.SCLCC_CNT = LEFT(APPL,5) TYP MAX_VERSION LEFT(JOB_NAME,8) ,
                  RIGHT(MEMCNT,7)

JCL.1  = '//'                   ,
         LEFT(JOB_NAME,8)       ,
         'JOB'                  ,
         JOB_CARD_ACCT          ,
         STRIP(APPL_1_4,'T')    ,
         JOB_CARD_PARMS

JCL.2  = '//         NOTIFY=&SYSUID'
JCL.3  = '//*'

IF JES = 3 THEN
    JCL.4  = '//*MAIN LINES=(100,W)'
ELSE
    JCL.4  = '/*JOBPARM LINES=999'

JCL.5  = '//*'
JCL.6  = '//*        APPL:' APPL_1_4 'TYPE:' TYP RIGHT(TIMESTAMP,35)

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//*'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//CHECKCC  EXEC PGM=IEFBR14,COND=(0,NE)'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//*'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//ABENDCC  EXEC PGM=WTOABEND,COND=(0,EQ,CHECKCC),'

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//             PARM=''CONDITION CODE(S) NOT = ZEROES'''

JCL_CNT     = JCL_CNT + 1
JCL.JCL_CNT = '//'

JCL.0 = JCL_CNT

CALL OFF ERROR

'ALLOC F(DUMMY) DA('''    JCL_DSN    '('    JOB_NAME    ')'')' ,
       'SHR REUSE'

CALL ON ERROR

IF RC <> 0 THEN
    DO
        SAY 'ERR901 - ALLOC JCL - RC =' RC
        EXIT 16
    END

CALL OFF ERROR

'EXECIO * DISKW DUMMY (STEM JCL. FINIS)'

CALL ON ERROR

IF RC <> 0 THEN
    DO
        SAY 'ERR902 - WRITE JCL - RC =' RC
        EXIT 16
    END

DROP JCL.
JCL_CNT = 6

RETURN
./  ADD  NAME=ENDVTSIF
/* REXX */
/*======================================================*/
/*===  name   : ENDVCVIF                             ===*/
/*===  purpose: I copy off inflight members and      ===*/
/*===           create endevor statements for loads  ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*===           I am the merger of two of Lanier's   ===*/
/*===           rexx execs                           ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*===  parms  : DEBUG      debug flag   Y/N          ===*/
/*===                      N is default              ===*/
/*===           INFLIGHT   INFLIGHT DD name          ===*/
/*===                      INFLIGHT is default       ===*/
/*===           ENODE      node to add to CMSTG?     ===*/
/*===                      for YourHQL.CHGMAN...          ===*/
/*===           DPFX       dataset prefix            ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*======================================================*/
parse upper arg my_parms
numeric digits 10
my_parms = " "  my_parms  " "    /* add spaces 4 parsing*/
my_rc = 0

                                       /* pull off debug parm */
                                       /* default is no debug */
                                       /* trace if debug=Y    */
parse var my_parms " DEBUG(" debug ")" .
my_item = "DEBUG("debug")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
debug = strip(debug)
if debug = "" then debug = "N"
if debug = "Y" then trace r
call do_init

if my_rc=0 then do
   cmac    = '0'
   cnt     = '0'

   last_appl=""
   do i = 1 to INF.0 while my_rc=0
      if INF.i = '*' then iterate
      if substr(INF.i,1,1) = '*' then iterate
      if strip(INF.i)="" then iterate
      cmappl=strip(word(INF.i,1));pacnum = strip(word(INF.i,2))
      wtest=strip(word(INF.i,4));wstage = strip(word(INF.i,5))
      wrest=delword(INF.i,1,5)
      if last_appl<>"" & last_appl<>cmappl then do
         my_rc=do_close(the_TEMPDD)
         if my_rc<>0 then iterate
      end
      if last_appl<>cmappl then do
         pprm=the_TEMPDD  " "  ,
              the_DPFX  ".#"  cmappl  ".ADD2EN(INFLIGHT)"
         my_rc=do_open(pprm)
         if my_rc<>0 then iterate
      end
      last_appl=cmappl
      prcpds=LIBPFX  "."  cmappl  "."  middle  the_ENODE  ".#"  pacnum
      call process_members
   end
end
if last_appl<>"" then do
    xx_rc=do_close(the_TEMPDD)
    if xx_rc>my_rc then my_rc=xx_rc
end

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    "RC="my_rc

return my_rc


Process_Members:,

 x = outtrap('lib.')
  "listcat level("prcpds")"
 x = outtrap('off')

 do z=1 to lib.0 while my_rc=0
    chklib = lib.z
    if pos('IN-CAT',lib.z) = 0 then do
       chklib = word(lib.z,3)
       chkdsn = translate(chklib,' ','.')
       nodes  = words(chkdsn)

       if nodes  = '6' then do
          call verify_PRCTYPE
          if DNP = 'N' & EMPTY_dataset = 'N' then do
             my_rc=do_inf2(chklib)
             if my_rc=0 then do
                dataline = copies(" ",80)
                dataline = overlay(chklib,dataline,1)
                dataline = overlay('*Processed*',dataline,50)
                chklib   = dataline
                cnt=cnt+1;dslst.cnt=chklib
             end
             else do
                Say ''
                Say 'Error Processing Library :'prcpds
                Say '.....No Record Processed.....'
                Say ''
             end
          end
       end
    end
 end

 drop lib.

Return

Verify_PRCTYPE:,

 DNP        =  'N'

 cmptypa    = strip(word(chkdsn,6))
 cmptypb    = substr(cmptypa,1,2)
 cmptypc    = substr(cmptypb,1,1)

 if pos('BKP',cmptypa) <> 0  then DNP='Y'
 if pos('BKUP',cmptypa) <> 0 then DNP='Y'

 if cmptypa = 'PACKAGE' ,
    cmptypa = 'IMPACT'  ,
    cmptypa = 'SRCBKP'  ,
    cmptypa = 'SRCBKUP' ,
    cmptypa = 'FMT'     ,
    cmptypa = 'LSA'     ,
    cmptypa = 'LOD'     ,
    cmptypa = 'LDM'     ,
    cmptypa = 'LDP'     ,
    cmptypa = 'LDI'     ,
    cmptypa = 'GRP'     ,
    cmptypa = 'LSI'     ,
    cmptypa = 'LOU'     ,
    cmptypa = 'DM1'     ,
    cmptypa = 'LSJ'     ,
    cmptypa = 'LDC'     ,
    cmptypa = 'LST'     ,
    cmptypa = 'PKG'     ,
    cmptypa = 'PSL'     ,
    cmptypa = 'DBL'     ,
    cmptypa = 'DBB'     ,
    cmptypa = 'DBR'     ,
    cmptypa = 'MFR'     ,
    cmptypb = 'WM'      ,
    cmptypb = 'WS'      ,
    cmptypb = 'IM'      ,
    cmptypb = 'IS'      ,
    cmptypb = 'NM'      ,
    cmptypb = 'NS'      ,
    cmptypc = '$'  then do
        DNP =  'Y'
 end
 else do
    Call Check_EMPTY
 end

Return

Check_EMPTY:,

 empty_dataset ='N'

 x = outtrap('chk.')
  "listds '"chklib"' members"
 x = outtrap('off')

 if chk.0 = 6 then do
    dataline = copies(" ",80)
    dataline = overlay(chklib,dataline,1)
    dataline = overlay('*EMPTY*',dataline,50)
    chklib   = dataline
    cnt=cnt+1;dslst.cnt=chklib
    empty_dataset ='Y'
 end

 drop chk.

Return

/*-------*/
do_open: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc
/*-------*/
arg DD DSN
my_rc=0

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" "FREE FI("DD")"
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)

aparm.1="ALLOC FI("  DD  ") DA('"  DSN  "') SHR REUSE"
aparm.2="EXECIO 0 DISKW "  DD
aparm.0=2

do kk=1 to aparm.0 while my_rc=0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
      my_rc = error_rc
   end
end

return my_rc

/*-------*/
do_write: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc rcds.
/*-------*/
arg DD
my_rc=0

aparm.1="EXECIO "rcds.0" DISKW "  DD  " (STEM rcds."
aparm.0=1

do kk=1 to aparm.0 while my_rc=0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
      my_rc = error_rc
   end
end

return my_rc

/*-------*/
do_close: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc
/*-------*/
arg DD
my_rc=0
queue "*"

aparm="EXECIO 1 DISKW "  DD  " (FINIS"
x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
io_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
if io_rc > 4 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm
   do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          omsg.i
   end
   my_rc = error_rc
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc

return my_rc

/*-------*/
do_inf2: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc the_DPFX the_TEMPDD ,
                 the_FAC wtest wstage NDX. SKP. wrest pacnum SKA. SPL.,
                 split_list
/*-------*/
arg prcdsn

my_rc=0
dsnodes = translate(prcdsn,' ','.')
cmappl  = strip(word(dsnodes,3))
cmatyp  = strip(word(dsnodes,6))
inflib  = the_DPFX  "."  cmappl  "."  strip(word(dsnodes,5))  "."  ,
          cmatyp

dl =0
squ="'"
dqu='"'
cnt=0
ctr=0

Say ''
Say '.... Processing INFLIGHT Library: 'prcdsn
Say ''
Say ''

vfydsn = sysdsn("'"inflib"'")

if my_rc=0 then call Load_Inflight_Members
if my_rc=0 then Call Build_ENDEVOR_Load_Records

return my_rc


Load_Inflight_Members:,

oldpds = prcdsn
newpds = inflib

                                           /* call IEBCOPY */
                                           /* individual copy fails */
                                           /* for FMT               */
x = OUTTRAP("msg.")
address "TSO" "FREE FI(SYSUT1)"
address "TSO" "FREE FI(SYSUT2)"
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)

say "Copying "oldpds" to "newpds

aparm.1="ALLOC FI(SYSUT1) DA('"oldpds"') SHR REUSE"
aparm.2="ALLOC FI(SYSUT2) DA('"newpds"') LIKE('"oldpds"') REUSE"
aparm.0=2

do kk=1 to aparm.0 while my_rc=0
   x = OUTTRAP("msg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   my_rc=RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if my_rc<>0 then do
      say "ERROR RC="my_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to msg.trapped
         say msg.i
      end
      return
   end
end

x = OUTTRAP("msg.")
"TSOEXEC  IEBCOPY"
copy_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
say "TSOEXEC IEBCOPY RC="copy_rc
do i = 1 to msg.trapped
   say msg.i
end
my_rc = copy_rc
if my_rc>4 then return
my_rc=0

x = OUTTRAP("msg.")
address "TSO" "FREE FI(SYSUT1)"
address "TSO" "FREE FI(SYSUT2)"
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)

   m = outtrap('infmem.')
      "listds '"prcdsn"' members"
   m = outtrap('off')

    do i=7 to infmem.0 while my_rc=0
       member = strip(infmem.i)
       member_l=length(member)
       good_member=1
       do zz=1 to member_l while good_member
          z1=substr(member,zz,1)
          if datatype(z1,'U') then iterate
          if datatype(z1,'W') & zz<> 1 then iterate
          if z1="$"   z1="@"   z1="#"  then iterate
          good_member=0
       end
       cnt=cnt+1;infelm.cnt=member
       infelm.cnt.OK=good_member
   /*  copy "'"oldpds'('member')'"'" "'"newpds'('member')'"'" nonum */
       my_rc = rc
       if good_member then do
          Say 'Valid Member: 'member
       end
       else do
          Say 'Invalid Member: 'member
       end
    end

Return

Build_ENDEVOR_Load_Records:,
  wtest="TESTI"
  wstage="R"

 lne0  = "SET TO ENVIRONMENT '"  wtest  "' STAGE '"  wstage  "'"
 lne1  = " SYSTEM '"  cmappl  "' SUBSYSTEM 'BASE' ."
 lne2  = "SET OPTIONS CCID 'CMNMIGR'"
 lne3  = 'OVERRIDE SIGNOUT'
 lne4  = "SET FROM DSNAME '"  newpds  "' ."
 dataline = copies(" ",80)
 dataline = overlay(lne0,dataline,2);dl=dl+1
 rcds.dl  = dataline
 dataline = copies(" ",80)
 dataline = overlay(lne1,dataline,2);dl=dl+1
 rcds.dl  = dataline
 dataline = copies(" ",80)
 dataline = overlay(lne2,dataline,2);dl=dl+1
 rcds.dl  = dataline
 dataline = copies(" ",80)
 dataline = overlay(lne3,dataline,6);dl=dl+1
 rcds.dl  = dataline
 dataline = copies(" ",65)
 dataline = overlay('UPDATE .',dataline,6);dl=dl+1
 rcds.dl  = dataline
 dataline = copies(" ",80)
 dataline = overlay(lne4,dataline,2);dl=dl+1
 rcds.dl  = dataline

lastndx=1
 do s = 1 to cnt
    if \infelm.s.OK then iterate
    pmem  = strip(infelm.s)
    skip_this_add=0
    i_care=0
    if the_FAC="C" & wordpos(cmatyp,split_list)<>0 then i_care=1
    do yy=1 to SPL.0 while \skip_this_add & cmatyp="DCL" & i_care
       if word(SPL.yy,1)>cmappl        then leave
       if cmappl<>word(SPL.yy,1)       then iterate
       if word(SPL.yy,2)>cmatyp        then leave
       if cmatyp<>word(SPL.yy,2)       then iterate
       if word(SPL.yy,3)=pmem          then leave
       if word(SPL.yy,3)<pmem          then iterate
       skip_this_add=1
       say 'Will skip add of 'pmem' App:'appcode' not app DCLGEN'
    end
    skip_this_add=0
    do yy=1 to SKA.0 while \skip_this_add
       if word(SKA.yy,1)>cmappl        then leave
       if cmappl<>word(SKA.yy,1)       then iterate
       if word(SKA.yy,2)>pmem          then leave
       if pmem<>word(SKA.yy,2)         then iterate
       skip_this_add=1
       say 'Will skip add of 'pmem' App:'appcode
    end
    ctr=ctr+1;lrec.ctr=pmem
    usetyp=cmatyp
    if cmatyp="SRC" then do
       do nn=1 to NDX.0
          if pmem=word(NDX.nn,1) then do
             usetyp=word(NDX.nn,3)
             leave
          end
       end
    end
    if usetyp="SRC" then usetyp="COB"
    useprc=usetyp
    if usetyp="COB"   usetyp="PLI" then useprc="COMPILE"
    if usetyp="ASM" then useprc="COMPILE"
    skip_this_one=0
    skip_this_one=1   /* do not generate any of inflight */
    do yy=lastndx to SKP.0 while \skip_this_one
       if word(SKP.yy,1)>cmappl        then leave
       if cmappl<>word(SKP.yy,1)       then iterate
       if word(SKP.yy,2)>usetyp        then leave
       if usetyp<>word(SKP.yy,2)       then iterate
       if word(SKP.yy,3)>pmem          then leave
       if pmem<>word(SKP.yy,3)         then iterate
       skip_this_one=1
       say 'Will skip generate of 'pmem' Type:'usetyp' App:'appcode
    end
    lastndx=yy

    /* Line 1 */
    dataline = copies(" ",80)
    sysrec1  = '*  S M='pmem
    dataline = overlay(sysrec1,dataline,1)
    dataline = overlay(usetyp,dataline,17);dl=dl+1
    rcds.dl   = dataline

    /* Line 2 */
    dataline = copies(" ",80)
    sysrec2  = 'ADD ELEMENT 'pmem
    sysrec2a = ' TO TYPE 'usetyp
    dataline = overlay(sysrec2,dataline,2)
    dataline = overlay(sysrec2a,dataline,22);dl=dl+1
    rcds.dl  = dataline

    /* Line 3 */
    dataline = copies(" ",80)
    sysrec3  = 'OPTIONS PRO GRO = 'useprc
    if useprc="COMPILE"   skip_this_one then ,
       sysrec3=sysrec3  " BYPASS GENERATE PROCESSOR "
    dataline = overlay(sysrec3,dataline,6);dl=dl+1
    rcds.dl  = dataline

    /* Line 4 */
    dataline = copies(" ",80)
    qqcom='LMSTOEND: '  pmem  ' '  date('U')  ' @ '  time('N')
    if strip(wrest)<>'' then do
       parse var wrest 'Status='qqstatus ' Creator=' qqcreator ,
                       ' Phone='qqphone 'Type=' qqtype ,
                       ' Start='qqstart 'Last Prom Date=' qqprom ,
                       qqmore ' Title='qqtitle
       qqcom='CM#'  pacnum  '-'  ,
             qqstatus  ' '  strip(qqtitle)  "-"qqcreator  "-"  qqstart
    end
    qqcom=translate(qqcom," ",'"')
    dataline= ' COMMENTS "'  left(qqcom,40)  '".'
    dl=dl+1
    rcds.dl=dataline

 end

 /*Write Final CTL/SYSIN Records*/
 dataline = copies(" ",80)
 sysrecf  = ,
 'SET FROM ENVIRONMENT '  wtest  ' STAGE '  wstage  ,
         ' SYSTEM '  cmappl  ' SUBSYSTEM BASE.'
 dataline = overlay(sysrecf,dataline,2);dl=dl+1
 rcds.dl  = dataline

 do q = 1 to ctr
    lpmem = strip(lrec.q)
    skip_this_add=0
    if the_FAC="C" & wordpos(cmatyp,split_list)<>0 then i_care=1
    do yy=1 to SPL.0 while \skip_this_add & cmatyp="DCL" & i_care
       if word(SPL.yy,1)>cmappl        then leave
       if cmappl<>word(SPL.yy,1)       then iterate
       if word(SPL.yy,2)>cmatyp        then leave
       if cmatyp<>word(SPL.yy,2)       then iterate
       if word(SPL.yy,3)=lpmem         then leave
       if word(SPL.yy,3)<lpmem         then iterate
       skip_this_add=1
       say 'Will skip add of 'lpmem' App:'appcode' not app DCLGEN'
    end
    skip_this_add=0
    do yy=1 to SKA.0 while \skip_this_add
       if word(SKA.yy,1)>cmappl        then leave
       if cmappl<>word(SKA.yy,1)       then iterate
       if word(SKA.yy,2)>lpmem         then leave
       if lpmem<>word(SKA.yy,2)        then iterate
       skip_this_add=1
       say 'Will skip signin of 'lpmem' App:'appcode
    end
    /* Line 5*/
    dataline = copies(" ",80)
    sysrec5  = 'SIGNIN ELEMENT 'lpmem
    sysrec5a = 'FROM TYPE 'usetyp' .'
    dataline = overlay(sysrec5,dataline,2)
    dataline = overlay(sysrec5a,dataline,26);dl=dl+1
    rcds.dl  = dataline
 end
 rcds.0=dl

 my_rc=do_write(the_TEMPDD)
 drop rcds.


return



/*------*/
do_init:
/*------*/

parse source w1 w2 w3 w4 w5 w6 w7 w8
my_name = w3

error_rc        =8
unknown_parms_rc=4
PKGS.0          =0
middle          ="CMSTG"
LIBPFX          ="YourHQL.CHGMAN"
LIBPFX_l        =length(LIBPFX)
the_INFLIGHT_dflt="INFLIGHT"
the_INDEX_dflt   ="INDEX"
the_FAC_dflt    =""
the_DPFX_dflt   =""
the_ENODE_dflt  =""
the_TEMPDD_dflt ="CVIFDD"
the_SPLITS_dflt ="SPLITS"
the_SKIPDD_dflt ="SKIPDD"
the_SKIPADD_dflt ="SKIPADD"



                                       /* pull off FAC        */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " FAC(" the_FAC ")" .
my_item = "FAC("the_FAC")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_FAC = strip(the_FAC)
if the_FAC = "" then the_FAC = the_FAC_dflt
if strip(the_FAC) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm FAC() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end



                                       /* pull off SPLITS     */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " SPLITS(" the_SPLITS ")" .
my_item = "SPLITS("the_SPLITS")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_SPLITS = strip(the_SPLITS)
if the_SPLITS = "" then the_SPLITS = the_SPLITS_dflt
if strip(the_SPLITS) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm SPLITS() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end



                                       /* pull off SKIPDD     */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " SKIPDD(" the_SKIPDD ")" .
my_item = "SKIPDD("the_SKIPDD")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_SKIPDD = strip(the_SKIPDD)
if the_SKIPDD = "" then the_SKIPDD = the_SKIPDD_dflt
if strip(the_SKIPDD) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm SKIPDD() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end



                                       /* pull off SKIPADD    */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " SKIPADD(" the_SKIPADD ")" .
my_item = "SKIPADD("the_SKIPADD")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_SKIPADD = strip(the_SKIPADD)
if the_SKIPADD = "" then the_SKIPADD = the_SKIPADD_dflt
if strip(the_SKIPADD) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm SKIPADD() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end



                                       /* pull off TEMPDD     */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " TEMPDD(" the_TEMPDD ")" .
my_item = "TEMPDD("the_TEMPDD")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_TEMPDD = strip(the_TEMPDD)
if the_TEMPDD = "" then the_TEMPDD = the_TEMPDD_dflt
if strip(the_TEMPDD) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm TEMPDD() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end

                                       /* pull off ENODE      */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " ENODE(" the_ENODE ")" .
my_item = "ENODE("the_ENODE")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_ENODE = strip(the_ENODE)
if the_ENODE = "" then the_ENODE = the_ENODE_dflt
if strip(the_ENODE) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm ENODE() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end
                                       /* pull off INFLIGHT   */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " INFLIGHT(" the_INFLIGHT ")" .
my_item = "INFLIGHT("the_INFLIGHT")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_INFLIGHT = strip(the_INFLIGHT)
if the_INFLIGHT = "" then the_INFLIGHT = the_INFLIGHT_dflt
if strip(the_INFLIGHT) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm INFLIGHT() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end
                                       /* pull off INDEX      */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " INDEX(" the_INDEX ")" .
my_item = "INDEX("the_INDEX")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_INDEX = strip(the_INDEX)
if the_INDEX = "" then the_INDEX = the_INDEX_dflt
if strip(the_INDEX) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm INDEX() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end


                                       /* pull off DPFX       */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " DPFX(" the_DPFX ")" .
my_item = "DPFX("the_DPFX")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_DPFX = strip(the_DPFX)
if the_DPFX = "" then the_DPFX = the_DPFX_dflt
if strip(the_DPFX) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm DPFX() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end




                                       /* any garbage parms?  */
if strip(my_parms) <> "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Unrecognized parms ignored: "my_parms
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Valid parms are DEBUG() INFLIGHT() DPFX() ENODE() TEMPDD() ",
       "INDEX() SKIPDD() SKIPADD() SPLITS() FAC()"
   my_rc=unknown_parms_rc
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc


aparm.1="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_INFLIGHT  " (STEM INF. FINIS"
aparm.2="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_INDEX  " (STEM NDX. FINIS"
aparm.3="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_SKIPDD  " (STEM SKP. FINIS"
aparm.4="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_SKIPADD  " (STEM SKA. FINIS"
aparm.5="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_SPLITS  " (STEM SPL. FINIS"
aparm.0=5
do kk=1 to aparm.0 while my_rc=0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
      my_rc = error_rc
   end
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc


split_list= "AHIC "  ,
            "APIB "  ,
            "APPP "  ,
            "BAC  "  ,
            "BPCD "  ,
            "BPFA "  ,
            "CSGC "  ,
            "CSPE "  ,
            "CSQS "  ,
            "CSRE "  ,
            "CSRT "  ,
            "CSUD "  ,
            "CSVB "  ,
            "CSWC "  ,
            "CSWP "  ,
            "CSWS "  ,
            "C7CC "  ,
            "C7VL "  ,
            "C7VM "  ,
            "DMAC "  ,
            "ECES "  ,
            "FDAL "  ,
            "FDBD "  ,
            "FDCI "  ,
            "FDCK "  ,
            "FDDF "  ,
            "FDDI "  ,
            "FDDO "  ,
            "FDEI "  ,
            "FDEX "  ,
            "FDFL "  ,
            "FDFO "  ,
            "FDGL "  ,
            "FDMI "  ,
            "FDOE "  ,
            "FDOH "  ,
            "FDOP "  ,
            "FDRA "  ,
            "FDSA "  ,
            "PAGA "  ,
            "PAGT "  ,
            "PAIC "  ,
            "PAMM "  ,
            "PAMO "  ,
            "PAOP "  ,
            "PAPK "  ,
            "PART "  ,
            "RCPR "
do kk=1 to SPL.0
   if strip(SPL.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(SPL.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   if wordpos(word(SPL.kk,1),split_list)=0 then ,
      split_list=split_list  " "  word(SPL.kk,1)  " "
end


return my_rc
./  ADD  NAME=ENDVTSL4
/* REXX */
/*======================================================*/
/*===  name   : ENDVCVL4                             ===*/
/*===  purpose: I populate the appilcation options   ===*/
/*===           conversion datasets with members     ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*===  parms  : DEBUG      debug flag   Y/N          ===*/
/*===                      N is default              ===*/
/*===           TYPDD      TYPES DD name             ===*/
/*===                      TYPDD is default          ===*/
/*===           TEMPDD     DD to use for temp allocs ===*/
/*===                      TEMPDD is default         ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*======================================================*/
parse upper arg my_parms
numeric digits 10
my_parms = " "  my_parms  " "    /* add spaces 4 parsing*/
my_rc = 0

                                       /* pull off debug parm */
                                       /* default is no debug */
                                       /* trace if debug=Y    */
parse var my_parms " DEBUG(" debug ")" .
my_item = "DEBUG("debug")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
debug = strip(debug)
if debug = "" then debug = "N"
if debug = "Y" then trace r

call do_init

/* For each Suffix in LIBSFX.                                         */
do ii = 1 to LIBSFX.0 while my_rc=0
   my_rc=do_alloc(LIBSFX.ii)
   if my_rc=0 then my_rc=do_work(LIBSFX.ii)
   xx_rc=do_free(LIBSFX.ii)
end

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    "RC="my_rc

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_work: procedure expose my_name debug LIBS. error_rc LIBPFX LIBPFX_l,
                          APPList the_TEMPDD
/*-------*/
arg DD

my_rc=0
node=DD

start_element  =".ADDELEMENT"
start_element_l=length(start_element)
end_element    =".ENDELEMENT"
end_element_l  =length(end_element)
in_element=0

/* Read each line from &DPFX..&DSFX..OPTS.                            */
/* Extract lines between pair of .ADDELEMENT and .ENDELEMENT lines.   */
/* Write lines to 'element' in &DPFX..&DSFX..#aaaa.typename(element)  */

eof=0
do while my_rc=0 & \eof
   io_rc=do_read(DD)   /* Read 1 Record */
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      my_rc=error_rc
      iterate
   end

   if io_rc<> 0 then do
      eof=1
      iterate
   end

/* If .ADDELEMENT, Process new member                                 */
   if substr(INREC.1,1,start_element_l)=start_element then do
      in_element=1
      first_one=1
      appcode=word(INREC.1,3)
      element=word(INREC.1,2)
      if DD="SPECIAL" then node=word(INREC.1,5)
      ecnt=0
      drop EMEM.

      EMEM.1 ="*"  copies('=',70)
      EMEM.2 ="* Program Name="  element
      EMEM.3 ="* Application ="  appcode
      EMEM.4 ="* "
      if DD="OPT" then do
         EMEM.5 ="* Program Options "
         EMEM.6 ="*    These are options that are different from the "
         EMEM.7 ="*    System Wide / Facility / Application options"
         EMEM.8 ="* "
         EMEM.9 ="* Converted to Endevor on "  date()  " "  time()
         EMEM.10="* "
         EMEM.11="*"  copies('=',70)
         EMEM.12="* "
         ecnt=12
      end
      if DD="SPPARM" then do
         EMEM.5 ="* Stored Procedure Parameters "
         EMEM.6 ="* "
         EMEM.7 ="* Converted to Endevor on "  date()  " "  time()
         EMEM.8 ="* "
         EMEM.9 ="*"  copies('=',70)
         EMEM.10="* "
         ecnt=10
      end
      if DD="FNPARM" then do
         EMEM.5 ="* UDF Parameters "
         EMEM.6 ="* "
         EMEM.7 ="* Converted to Endevor on "  date()  " "  time()
         EMEM.8 ="* "
         EMEM.9 ="*"  copies('=',70)
         EMEM.10="* "
         ecnt=10
      end
      if DD="SQLPL" then do
         EMEM.5 ="* Native Stored Procedure code body "
         EMEM.6 ="* "
         EMEM.7 ="* Converted to Endevor on "  date()  " "  time()
         EMEM.8 ="* "
         EMEM.9 ="*"  copies('=',70)
         EMEM.10="* "
         ecnt=10
      end

      iterate
   end

/* If .ENDELEMENT, Process member lines read                          */
   if substr(INREC.1,1,end_element_l)=end_element then do
      in_element=0
      EMEM.0=ecnt
      parm=the_TEMPDD  " "  LIBPFX  ".#"  appcode  "."  node  "("  ,
           element  ")"
      my_rc=do_write(parm)
      iterate
   end

/* Process member line in.                                            */
   if in_element then do
      line=strip(INREC.1,'T')
      line_l=length(line)
      last_char=substr(line,line_l,1)
      if last_char<>"+" & DD="OPT" then do
         last_char=""
      end
      if last_char="+" & DD="OPT" then do
         line=substr(line,1,line_l-1)
         line=strip(linke,'T')
         line_l=length(line)
      end
      if first_one & line_l >=5 then do        /* if already has   */
         if substr(line,1,5)="*====" then ecnt=0  /* comment block */
      end                                      /* don't add another*/
      first_one=0
      if (DD="OPT" & line_L <=72)   DD<>"OPT" then do
         ecnt=ecnt+1
         EMEM.ecnt=INREC.1
      end
      else do
         parse var INREC.1 op "=" v

         v=strip(v)
         vfirst=substr(v,1,1)
         if vfirst="'" then v=strip(v,'B',"'")
         if vfirst='"' then v=strip(v,'B','"')

         vlength=length(v)
         olength=length(op)+1
         posslength=68-olength
         if vlength<posslength then posslength=vlength

         comma_break=0
         if op="IEWL"   op="PLI"   op="ASMA90"   op="IGYCRCTL" ,
            then comma_break=1
         puselength=posslength
         if comma_break then do
            do cc=posslength to 1 by -1
               if substr(v,cc,1)="," then leave
               puselength=puselength-1
            end
         end
         ecnt=ecnt+1
         EMEM.ecnt=op  "='"  substr(v,1,puselength)  "'+"
         v=delstr(v,1,puselength)

         do while v<>""
            if length(v)<=69 then do
               ecnt=ecnt+1
               EMEM.ecnt="'"  v  "'"  last_char
               v=""
            end
            else do
               ecnt=ecnt+1
               puselength=69
               if comma_break then do
                  do cc=69 to 1 by -1
                     if substr(v,cc,1)="," then leave
                     puselength=puselength-1
                  end
               end
               EMEM.ecnt="'"  substr(v,1,puselength)  "'+"
               v=delstr(v,1,puselength)
            end
         end
      end
   end
end

hold_rc=do_close(DD)
if hold_rc>my_rc then my_rc=hold_rc

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_read: procedure expose my_name debug INREC. error_rc
/*-------*/
arg DD

aparm="EXECIO 1 DISKR "  DD  " (STEM INREC."

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
io_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
if io_rc > 4 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm
   do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          omsg.i
   end
end

/* say left(my_name,9),                                               */
/*     left(time("L"),16),                                            */
/*     'Reading from DD    =' "'"DD"'"                                */
/* say left(my_name,9),                                               */
/*     left(time("L"),16),                                            */
/*     'Records Read       =' "'"INREC.0"'"                           */

return io_rc

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
io_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
if io_rc > 4 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm
   do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          omsg.i
   end
   my_rc = error_rc
end

return my_rc

/*-------*/
do_alloc: procedure expose my_name debug LIBPFX error_rc
/*-------*/
arg DD

my_rc=0
sfx=DD
if sfx<>"SPECIAL" then sfx=sfx  "S"
DSN=LIBPFX  "."  sfx

aparm.1="ALLOC FILE("  DD  ") DSN('"DSN"') SHR REUSE"
aparm.0=1

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    'Allocating DSN In  =' DSN

x=OUTTRAP("msg.")
address "TSO" "FREE FI("DD")"
x=OUTTRAP(OFF)

do kk=1 to aparm.0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
      my_rc=error_rc
   end
end


return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_write: procedure expose my_name debug EMEM. error_rc
/*-------*/
arg DD DSN

my_rc=0
aparm.1="ALLOC FILE("  DD  ") DSN('"DSN"') SHR REUSE"
aparm.2="EXECIO "  EMEM.0  " DISKW "  DD  " (STEM EMEM. FINIS"
aparm.0=2

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    'Allocating DSN Out =' DSN

x=OUTTRAP("msg.")
address "TSO" "FREE FI("DD")"
x=OUTTRAP(OFF)

do kk=1 to aparm.0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
      my_rc=error_rc
   end
end

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    'Records written    =' "'"EMEM.0"'"

x=OUTTRAP("msg.")
address "TSO" "FREE FI("DD")"
x=OUTTRAP(OFF)


return my_rc


/*------*/
do_init:
/*------*/

parse source w1 w2 w3 w4 w5 w6 w7 w8
my_name = w3

error_rc        =8
unknown_parms_rc=4
interested_in   =" OPT SPPARM FNPARM SQLPL "
LIBSFX.0        =0
the_TEMPDD_dflt ="TEMPDD"
the_TYPDD_dflt  ="TYPDD"



                                       /* pull off TYPDD      */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " TYPDD(" the_TYPDD ")" .
my_item = "TYPDD("the_TYPDD")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_TYPDD = strip(the_TYPDD)
if the_TYPDD = "" then the_TYPDD = the_TYPDD_dflt
if strip(the_TYPDD) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm TYPDD() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end


                                       /* pull off TEMPDD     */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " TEMPDD(" the_TEMPDD ")" .
my_item = "TEMPDD("the_TEMPDD")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_TEMPDD = strip(the_TEMPDD)
if the_TEMPDD = "" then the_TEMPDD = the_TEMPDD_dflt
if strip(the_TEMPDD) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm TEMPDD() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end




                                       /* any garbage parms?  */
if strip(my_parms) <> "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Unrecognized parms ignored: "my_parms
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Valid parms are DEBUG() TYPDD() TEMPDD()"
   my_rc=unknown_parms_rc
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc

TYPDD_dsn=""
x = LISTDSI(the_TYPDD "FILE")
if x <= 4 then do
   TYPDD_dsn = sysdsname
end
TYPDD_dsn=strip(TYPDD_dsn)
if TYPDD_dsn="" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
      "Unable to retrieve dataset name for DD "the_TYPDD
   my_rc=error_rc
end

aparm="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_TYPDD  " (STEM INP. FINIS"
x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
io_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
if io_rc > 4 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm
   do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          omsg.i
   end
   my_rc = error_rc
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc

parse var TYPDD_dsn LIBPFX ".CONVSFX" rest
LIBPFX=strip(LIBPFX)
LIBPFX_l=length(LIBPFX)


l=0
do kk=1 to INP.0
   if strip(INP.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(INP.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   if words(INP.kk) <> 1     then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "line "kk" malformed in "TYPDD_dsn
      my_rc=error_rc
      iterate
   end
   if length(word(INP.kk,1))>8 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "line "kk" malformed in "TYPDD_dsn
      my_rc=error_rc
      iterate
   end
   needle=" "  word(INP.kk,1)  " "
   if pos(needle,interested_in)=0 then iterate
   l=l+1
   LIBSFX.l=word(INP.kk,1)
end
l=l+1
LIBSFX.l="SPECIAL"
LIBSFX.0=l
drop INP.

APPList=""
lcnt=0
x = outtrap('mud.')
"LISTC LVL("LIBPFX")"
x = outtrap(OFF)
do mmm = 1 to mud.trapped
   parse var mud.mmm w1 w2 w3 .
   if strip(w1) = "NONVSAM" then do
      w3tail=translate(delstr(w3,1,LIBPFX_l),' ','.')
      if  words(w3tail) <> 2 then iterate
      w3sfx=word(w3tail,2)
      do kk =1 to LIBSFX.0
         if w3sfx=LIBSFX.kk then do
            lcnt=lcnt+1
            LIBS.lcnt=w3
            needle=" "  word(w3tail,1)  " "
            if pos(needle,APPList)=0 then APPList=APPList  needle
         end
      end
   end
end
drop INP.
LIBS.0=lcnt

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    'APPList            =' "'"APPList"'"

TempLIBSFX = ''
Do s = 1 to  LIBSFX.0
   TempLIBSFX = TempLIBSFX LIBSFX.s
End s
say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    'LIBSfx             =' "'"TempLIBSFX"'"

return my_rc

/*===                      N is default              ===*/
/*===           APPS       APPS  DD name             ===*/
/*===                      APPS  is default          ===*/
/*===           TYPDD      TYPES DD name             ===*/
/*===                      TYPDD is default          ===*/
/*===           TEMPDD     DD to use for temp allocs ===*/
/*===                      TEMPDD is default         ===*/
/*===           TEM2DD     DD to use for temp allocs ===*/
/*===                      TEM2DD is default         ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*======================================================*/

/* 2014.04.23 Stefan                                                  */
/* Added Type TCOBD                                                   */
/* Changed CCID to LMSMIGR                                            */

parse upper arg my_parms
numeric digits 10
my_parms = " "  my_parms  " "    /* add spaces 4 parsing*/
my_rc = 0

                                       /* pull off debug parm */
                                       /* default is no debug */
                                       /* trace if debug=Y    */

my_item = "DEBUG("debug")"

if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
