/*-------*/
do_work: procedure expose my_name debug APPList LIBSfx LIBPfx ,
                          APPList error_rc SKP. SKA. DTypes
/*-------*/
arg DD DD2

my_rc=0

/* For each App */
do kk=1 to words(APPlist) while my_rc=0
   apar=DD2  " "  word(APPlist,kk)
   my_rc=do_alloc2(apar)

   /* For each Suffix */
   do jj=1 to words(LIBSfx) while my_rc=0
      xpar=apar" "  word(LIBSfx,jj)
      my_rc=do_alloc_mem(xpar)
      parm=DD  " "  DD2  " "  word(APPList,kk)  " "  word(LIBSfx,jj)
      my_rc=do_alloc(parm)
      if my_rc=error_rc then iterate
      if my_rc=4 then do
         my_rc=0
         iterate
      end
      if my_rc=0 then do
         my_rc=do_sysins(parm)
      end
   end jj
end kk

xx_rc=do_free(DD)
xx_rc=do_free(DD2)

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_free:  procedure expose my_name debug error_rc
/*-------*/
arg DD

aparm="FREE FI("  DD  ")"

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)

return 0


/*-------*/
do_alloc: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc LIBPfx PGMS.
/*-------*/
arg DD DD2 app sfx

my_rc=do_free(DD)
drop PGMS.
PGMS.0=0

dsn="'"  LIBPfx  ".#"  app  "."  sfx  "'"
if sysdsn(dsn) <> "OK" then return 1

aparm="ALLOC FI("  DD  ") DSN("  dsn  ") SHR REUSE"

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    'Allocating DSN In  =' dsn

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
io_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
if io_rc > 4 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm
   do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          omsg.i
   end
   return error_rc
end

cnt=0
drop mud.
v = outtrap('mud.')
"LISTDS ("dsn") MEMBERS"
v = outtrap(OFF)
do vv = 1 to mud.0 until strip(mud.vv) = "--MEMBERS--"
end
do vvv = vv+1 to mud.0
   found=0
   x=strip(mud.vvv)
   do kk = 1 to PGMS.0 while \found
      if strip(PGMS.kk)=x then found=1
   end
   if \found then do
      cnt=cnt+1
      PGMS.cnt=x
   end
end
PGMS.0=cnt

return 0


/*-------*/
do_alloc2: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc LIBPfx
/*-------*/
arg DD2 app

my_rc=do_free(DD2)

dsn="'"  LIBPfx  ".#"  app  "."  ADD2EN  "'"

aparm="ALLOC FI("  DD2  ") SHR REUSE "  ,
      "DA("  dsn  ")"

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    'Allocating DSN 2   =' dsn

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
io_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
if io_rc > 4 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm
   do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          omsg.i
   end
   return error_rc
end

my_rc=do_free(DD2)


return 0

/*-------*/
do_alloc_mem: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc LIBPfx
/*-------*/
arg DD2 app sfx

my_rc=do_free(DD2)

dsn="'"  LIBPfx  ".#"  app  "."  ADD2EN  "("  sfx  ")'"

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    ' '

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    'Allocating DSN Out =' dsn

aparm="ALLOC FI("  DD2  ") DA("  dsn  ") SHR REUSE"

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
io_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
if io_rc > 4 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm
   do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          omsg.i
   end
   return error_rc
end

return 0


/*-------*/
do_write: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc DATA.
/*-------*/
arg DD

my_rc=0

if DATA.0=0 then do
   DATA.1="* "
   DATA.0=1
end

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    'Records written    =' "'"DATA.0"'"

aparm.1="EXECIO "  DATA.0  " DISKW "  DD  " (STEM DATA. FINIS"
aparm.0=1

do kk=1 to aparm.0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
      my_rc=error_rc
   end
end

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_sysins: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc LIBPfx PGMS. SKP. ,
                            SKA. DTypes
/*-------*/
/** Author: Lanier Tuggle                                             */
arg DD DD2 applcode sfx

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    'Processing SYSIN   =' "'"applcode sfx"'"

prgr=sfx
/* if sfx='COBD'   sfx='ASMD'   sfx='PLID'   sfx='SQLPLD' then ,      */
/*    prgr='CONVERTP'                                                 */

If WordPos( sfx, DTypes) > 0 Then
   prgr='CONVERTP'

my_rc=0
DATA.0=0
if PGMS.0=0 then return do_write(DD2)

lne1  = 'SET TO ENVIRONMENT PROD STAGE P SYSTEM '  applcode  ,
        ' SUBSYSTEM BASE.'
lne2  = 'SET OPTIONS CCID LMSMIGR'

lne3  = 'OVERRIDE SIGNOUT UPDATE .'
if prgr<>sfx then ,
  lne3="OVERRIDE SIGNOUT BYPASS GENERATE PROCESSOR UPDATE ."

lne4  = "SET FROM DSNAME '"  LIBPfx  ".#"  applcode  "."  sfx  "'."

dl=0
dataline = copies(" ",80)
dataline = overlay(lne1,dataline,2);dl=dl+1
DATA.dl  = dataline
dataline = copies(" ",80)
dataline = overlay(lne2,dataline,2);dl=dl+1
DATA.dl  = dataline
dataline = copies(" ",80)
dataline = overlay(lne3,dataline,6);dl=dl+1
DATA.dl  = dataline
dataline = copies(" ",80)
dataline = overlay(lne4,dataline,2);dl=dl+1
DATA.dl  = dataline

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    'Program Count      =' "'"PGMS.0"'"

/* For each Program */
lastndx=1
do s = 1 to PGMS.0
   pmem  = strip(PGMS.s)
   skip_this_one=0
   do yy=1 to SKA.0 while \skip_this_one
      if word(SKA.yy,1)>applcode      then leave
      if applcode<>word(SKP.yy,1)     then iterate
      if word(SKA.yy,2)>pmem          then leave
      if pmem<>word(SKA.yy,2)         then iterate
      skip_this_one=1
      say 'Will skip add of 'pmem' App:'applcode
   end
   if skip_this_one then iterate
   do yy=lastndx to SKP.0 while \skip_this_one
      if word(SKP.yy,1)>applcode      then leave
      if applcode<>word(SKP.yy,1)     then iterate
      if word(SKP.yy,2)>sfx           then leave
      if sfx<>word(SKP.yy,2)          then iterate
      if word(SKP.yy,3)>pmem          then leave
      if pmem<>word(SKP.yy,3)         then iterate
      skip_this_one=1
      say 'Will skip generation of 'pmem' Type:'sfx' App:'applcode
   end
   lastndx=yy

   /* Line 1 */
   dataline = copies(" ",80)
   sysrec1  = '*  S M='  pmem
   dataline = overlay(sysrec1,dataline,1)
   dataline = overlay(sfx,dataline,17);dl=dl+1
   DATA.dl  = dataline

   /* Line 2 */
   dataline = copies(" ",80)
   sysrec2  = 'ADD ELEMENT '  pmem
   sysrec2a = ' TO TYPE '  sfx
   dataline = overlay(sysrec2,dataline,2)
   dataline = overlay(sysrec2a,dataline,22);dl=dl+1
   DATA.dl  = dataline

   cpr="OPTIONS "
   /* Line 3 */
   if prgr=sfx then do
      dataline = copies(" ",80)
      sysrec3  = 'OPTIONS PRO GRO = '  prgr
      dataline = overlay(sysrec3,dataline,6);dl=dl+1
      DATA.dl  = dataline
      cpr="        "
   end
   if skip_this_one then do
      hix=' BYPASS GENERATE PROCESSOR '
      if strip(cpr)<>"" then do
         hix=' OPTIONS '  hix
         cpr="        "
      end
      dl=dl+1
      DATA.dl  = hix
   end

   /* Line 4 */
   dataline = copies(" ",80)
   sysrec4  =cpr  ,
     'COMMENTS "LMSTOEND: '  pmem  " "  date('U')  "@ "  time('N')  ,
     '".'
   dataline =sysrec4;dl=dl+1
   DATA.dl  = dataline

end s

/* Write Final CTL/SYSIN Records */
dataline = copies(" ",80)
sysrecf  ='SET FROM ENVIRONMENT PROD STAGE P SYSTEM '  applcode  ,
          ' SUBSYSTEM BASE .'
dataline = overlay(sysrecf,dataline,2);dl=dl+1
DATA.dl  = dataline

/* For each Program */
do q = 1 to PGMS.0
   lpmem  = strip(PGMS.q)
   skip_this_one=0
   do yy=1 to SKA.0 while \skip_this_one
      if word(SKA.yy,1)>applcode      then leave
      if applcode<>word(SKP.yy,1)     then iterate
      if word(SKA.yy,2)>lpmem         then leave
      if lpmem<>word(SKA.yy,2)        then iterate
      skip_this_one=1
      say 'Will skip add of 'lpmem' App:'applcode
   end
   if skip_this_one then iterate
   /* Line 5*/
   dataline = copies(" ",80)
   sysrec5  = 'SIGNIN ELEMENT '  lpmem
   sysrec5a = 'FROM TYPE '  sfx  '.'
   dataline = overlay(sysrec5,dataline,2)
   dataline = overlay(sysrec5a,dataline,26);dl=dl+1
   DATA.dl  = dataline
end
DATA.0=dl

return do_write(DD2)


/*------*/
do_init:
/*------*/

parse source w1 w2 w3 w4 w5 w6 w7 w8
my_name = w3

error_rc        =8
unknown_parms_rc=4
APPList         =""
LIBSfx          =""
LIBPfx          =""
LIBSFX.0        =0
the_APPS_dflt   ="APPS"
the_TEMPDD_dflt ="TEMPDD"
the_TEM2DD_dflt ="TEM2DD"
the_SKIPADD_dflt ="SKIPADD"
the_SKIPDD_dflt ="SKIPDD"
the_TYPDD_dflt  ="TYPDD"

/* Verifies input DDNAMES + TEMPDD and TEM2DD                         */

                                       /* pull off APPS       */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " APPS(" the_APPS ")" .
my_item = "APPS("the_APPS")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_APPS = strip(the_APPS)
if the_APPS = "" then the_APPS = the_APPS_dflt
if strip(the_APPS) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm APPS() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end

                                       /* pull off TYPDD      */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " TYPDD(" the_TYPDD ")" .
my_item = "TYPDD("the_TYPDD")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_TYPDD = strip(the_TYPDD)
if the_TYPDD = "" then the_TYPDD = the_TYPDD_dflt
if strip(the_TYPDD) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm TYPDD() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end


                                       /* pull off SKIPDD     */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " SKIPDD(" the_SKIPDD ")" .
my_item = "SKIPDD("the_SKIPDD")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_SKIPDD = strip(the_SKIPDD)
if the_SKIPDD = "" then the_SKIPDD = the_SKIPDD_dflt
if strip(the_SKIPDD) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm SKIPDD() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end

                                       /* pull off SKIPADD    */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " SKIPADD(" the_SKIPADD ")" .
my_item = "SKIPADD("the_SKIPADD")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_SKIPADD = strip(the_SKIPADD)
if the_SKIPADD = "" then the_SKIPADD = the_SKIPADD_dflt
if strip(the_SKIPADD) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm SKIPADD() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end


                                       /* pull off TEMPDD     */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " TEMPDD(" the_TEMPDD ")" .
my_item = "TEMPDD("the_TEMPDD")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_TEMPDD = strip(the_TEMPDD)
if the_TEMPDD = "" then the_TEMPDD = the_TEMPDD_dflt
if strip(the_TEMPDD) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm TEMPDD() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end

                                       /* pull off TEM2DD     */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " TEM2DD(" the_TEM2DD ")" .
my_item = "TEM2DD("the_TEM2DD")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_TEM2DD = strip(the_TEM2DD)
if the_TEM2DD = "" then the_TEM2DD = the_TEM2DD_dflt
if strip(the_TEM2DD) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm TEM2DD() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end

                                       /* any garbage parms?  */
if strip(my_parms) <> "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Unrecognized parms ignored: "my_parms
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Valid parms are DEBUG() TYPDD() TEMPDD() TEM2DD() SKIPDD() ",
       " SKIPADD()"
   my_rc=unknown_parms_rc
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc

/* Reads APPS into INA., SKIPDD to SKP., SKIPADD to SKA.              */
aparm.1="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_APPS  " (STEM INA. FINIS"
aparm.2="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_SKIPDD  " (STEM SKP. FINIS"
aparm.3="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_SKIPADD  " (STEM SKA. FINIS"
aparm.0=3
do kk=1 to aparm.0 while my_rc=0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
      my_rc = error_rc
   end
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc

/* Reads INA., adds each application to APPList string                */
do kk=1 to INA.0
   if strip(INA.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(INA.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   needle=" "  word(INA.kk,1)  " "
   if pos(needle,APPList)=0 then APPList=APPList  needle
end
drop INA.


/* Reads TYPDD into INP., adds each line into LIBSfx string           */
aparm="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_TYPDD  " (STEM INP. FINIS"
x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
io_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
if io_rc > 4 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm
   do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          omsg.i
   end
   my_rc = error_rc
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc

do kk=1 to INP.0
   if strip(INP.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(INP.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   needle=" "  word(INP.kk,1)  " "
   if pos(needle,LIBSfx)=0 then LIBSfx=LIBSfx  needle
end
drop INP.

/* Add Type  D types to LIBSfx                                        */
DTypes = " COBD ASMD PLID SQLPLD TCOBD "
LIBSfx=LIBSfx  DTypes


TYPDD_dsn=""
x = LISTDSI(the_TYPDD "FILE")
if x <= 4 then do
   TYPDD_dsn = sysdsname
end
TYPDD_dsn=strip(TYPDD_dsn)
if TYPDD_dsn="" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
      "Unable to retrieve dataset name for DD "the_TYPDD
   my_rc=error_rc
end

parse var TYPDD_dsn LIBPFX ".CONVSFX" rest
LIBPfx=strip(LIBPFX)
LIBPfx_l=length(LIBPFX)

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    'APPList            =' "'"APPList"'"

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    'LIBSfx             =' "'"LIBSfx"'"

return my_rc

/*======================================================*/
./  ADD  NAME=ENDVTSL6
/* REXX */
/*======================================================*/
/*===  name   : ENDVCVL6                             ===*/
/*===  purpose: I create endevor add elements from   ===*/
/*===           existing datasets for all types      ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*===  parms  : DEBUG      debug flag   Y/N          ===*/
/*===                      N is default              ===*/
/*===           APPS       APPS  DD name             ===*/
/*===                      APPS  is default          ===*/
/*===           TYPDD      TYPES DD name             ===*/
/*===                      TYPDD is default          ===*/
/*===           TEMPDD     DD to use for temp allocs ===*/
/*===                      TEMPDD is default         ===*/
/*===           TEM2DD     DD to use for temp allocs ===*/
/*===                      TEM2DD is default         ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*======================================================*/
/**********************************************************************/
/* Version : 14/04/03                                                 */
/* Change  : Changed CMNTOEND to LMSTOEND                             */
/**********************************************************************/
parse upper arg my_parms
numeric digits 10
my_parms = " "  my_parms  " "    /* add spaces 4 parsing*/
my_rc = 0

                                       /* pull off debug parm */
                                       /* default is no debug */
                                       /* trace if debug=Y    */
parse var my_parms " DEBUG(" debug ")" .
my_item = "DEBUG("debug")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
debug = strip(debug)
if debug = "" then debug = "N"
if debug = "Y" then trace r
call do_init

p=the_TEMPDD  " "  the_TEM2DD
if my_rc=0 then my_rc=do_work(p)

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    "RC="my_rc

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_work: procedure expose my_name debug APPList LIBPfx ,
                          APPLS. error_rc SKP. SKA.
/*-------*/
arg DD DD2

my_rc=0

do kk=1 to words(APPlist) while my_rc=0
   apar=DD2  " "  word(APPlist,kk)
   stage=APPLS.kk.STG
   envr=APPLS.kk.ENV
   appcode=word(APPlist,kk)
   my_rc=do_alloc2(apar)
   do jj=1 to 1 while my_rc=0
      xpar=apar  " OPT"
      my_rc=do_alloc_mem(xpar)
      parm=DD  " "  DD2  " "  word(APPlist,kk)  " OPT"
      my_rc=do_alloc(parm)
      if my_rc=error_rc then iterate
      if my_rc=4 then do
         my_rc=0
         iterate
      end
      if my_rc=0 then do
         my_rc=do_sysins(parm)
      end
   end
end
xx_rc=do_free(DD)
xx_rc=do_free(DD2)

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_free:  procedure expose my_name debug error_rc
/*-------*/
arg DD

aparm="FREE FI("  DD  ")"

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)

return 0


/*-------*/
do_alloc: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc LIBPfx PGMS.
/*-------*/
arg DD DD2 app sfx

my_rc=do_free(DD)
drop PGMS.
PGMS.0=0

dsn="'"  LIBPfx  ".#"  app  "."  sfx  "'"
if sysdsn(dsn) <> "OK" then return 1

aparm="ALLOC FI("  DD  ") DSN("  dsn  ") SHR REUSE"

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
io_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
if io_rc > 4 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm
   do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          omsg.i
   end
   return error_rc
end

cnt=0
drop mud.
v = outtrap('mud.')
"LISTDS ("dsn") MEMBERS"
v = outtrap(OFF)
do vv = 1 to mud.0 until strip(mud.vv) = "--MEMBERS--"
end
do vvv = vv+1 to mud.0
   found=0
   x=strip(mud.vvv)
   do kk = 1 to PGMS.0 while \found
      if strip(PGMS.kk)=x then found=1
   end
   if \found then do
      cnt=cnt+1
      PGMS.cnt=x
   end
end
PGMS.0=cnt

return 0


/*-------*/

/*-------*/
arg DD2 app

my_rc=do_free(DD2)

dsn="'"  LIBPfx  ".#"  app  "."  ADD2EN  "'"

aparm="ALLOC FI("  DD2  ") SHR REUSE "  ,
      "DA("  dsn  ")"

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
io_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
if io_rc > 4 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm
   do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          omsg.i
   end
   return error_rc
end

my_rc=do_free(DD2)


return 0

/*-------*/

my_rc=do_free(DD2)

dsn="'"  LIBPfx  ".#"  app  "."  ADD2EN  "(GEN"  sfx  ")'"

          left(time("L"),16),
          omsg.i
   end
   return error_rc
end

return 0


/*-------*/
do_write: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc DATA.
/*-------*/
arg DD

my_rc=0

if DATA.0=0 then do
   DATA.1="* "
   DATA.0=1
end

aparm.1="EXECIO "  DATA.0  " DISKW "  DD  " (STEM DATA. FINIS"
aparm.0=1

do kk=1 to aparm.0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
      my_rc=error_rc
   end
end

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_sysins: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc LIBPfx PGMS. ,
                            stage envr appcode SKP. SKA.
/*-------*/
/** Author: Lanier Tuggle                                          */
arg DD DD2 applcode sfx

my_rc=0
DATA.0=0
dl=0
if PGMS.0=0 then return do_write(DD2)

lastndx=1
do s = 1 to PGMS.0
   pmem  = strip(PGMS.s)
   skip_this_one=0
   do yy=1 to SKA.0 while \skip_this_one
      if word(SKA.yy,1)>appcode       then leave
      if appcode<>word(SKA.yy,1)      then iterate
      if word(SKA.yy,2)>pmem          then leave
      if pmem<>word(SKA.yy,2)         then iterate
      skip_this_one=1
      say 'Will skip add of 'pmem' Type:OPT App:'appcode
   end
   if skip_this_one then iterate
   do yy=lastndx to SKP.0 while \skip_this_one
      if word(SKP.yy,1)>appcode       then leave
      if appcode<>word(SKP.yy,1)      then iterate
      if word(SKP.yy,2)>"OPT"         then leave
      if "OPT"<>word(SKP.yy,2)        then iterate
      if word(SKP.yy,3)>pmem          then leave
      if pmem<>word(SKP.yy,3)         then iterate
      skip_this_one=1
      say 'Will skip generate of 'pmem' Type:OPT App:'appcode
   end
   lastndx=yy
   if skip_this_one then iterate

   dl=dl+1
   DATA.dl=' GENERATE ELEMENT "'  pmem  '"'
   dl=dl+1
 /* DATA.dl=' FROM ENVIRONMENT "'  envr  '"' */
   DATA.dl=' FROM ENVIRONMENT "PROD"'
   dl=dl+1
   DATA.dl='   SYSTEM "'  appcode  '" SUBSYSTEM "BASE"'
   dl=dl+1
 /*  DATA.dl='   TYPE "OPT" STAGE "'  stage  '"' */
   DATA.dl='   TYPE "OPT" STAGE "P"'
   dl=dl+1
   DATA.dl="   OPTIONS COMMENT 'LMSTOEND Initial Generation'"
   dl=dl+1
   DATA.dl='           CCID "LMSMIGR" OVERRIDE SIGNOUT'
   dl=dl+1
   DATA.dl='           PROCESSOR GROUP "OPT"'
   dl=dl+1
   DATA.dl='           SEARCH COPYBACK .'

end
DATA.0=dl

return do_write(DD2)


/*------*/
do_init:
/*------*/

parse source w1 w2 w3 w4 w5 w6 w7 w8
my_name = w3

error_rc        =8
unknown_parms_rc=4
APPlist         =""
LIBSfx          =""
LIBPfx          =""
the_APPS_dflt   ="APPS"
the_APPMASTR_dflt="APPMASTR"
the_TEMPDD_dflt ="TEMPDD"
the_TEM2DD_dflt ="TEM2DD"
the_SKIPADD_dflt ="SKIPADD"
the_SKIPDD_dflt ="SKIPDD"



                                       /* pull off SKIPDD     */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " SKIPDD(" the_SKIPDD ")" .
my_item = "SKIPDD("the_SKIPDD")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_SKIPDD = strip(the_SKIPDD)
if the_SKIPDD = "" then the_SKIPDD = the_SKIPDD_dflt
if strip(the_SKIPDD) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm SKIPDD() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end


                                       /* pull off SKIPADD    */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " SKIPADD(" the_SKIPADD ")" .
my_item = "SKIPADD("the_SKIPADD")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_SKIPADD = strip(the_SKIPADD)
if the_SKIPADD = "" then the_SKIPADD = the_SKIPADD_dflt
if strip(the_SKIPADD) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm SKIPADD() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end

                                       /* pull off APPS       */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " APPS(" the_APPS ")" .
my_item = "APPS("the_APPS")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_APPS = strip(the_APPS)
if the_APPS = "" then the_APPS = the_APPS_dflt
if strip(the_APPS) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm APPS() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end

                                       /* pull off APPMASTR   */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " APPMASTR(" the_APPMASTR ")" .
my_item = "APPMASTR("the_APPMASTR")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_APPMASTR = strip(the_APPMASTR)
if the_APPMASTR = "" then the_APPMASTR = the_APPMASTR_dflt
if strip(the_APPMASTR) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm APPMASTR() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end

                                       /* pull off TEMPDD     */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " TEMPDD(" the_TEMPDD ")" .
my_item = "TEMPDD("the_TEMPDD")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_TEMPDD = strip(the_TEMPDD)
if the_TEMPDD = "" then the_TEMPDD = the_TEMPDD_dflt
if strip(the_TEMPDD) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm TEMPDD() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end

                                       /* pull off TEM2DD     */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " TEM2DD(" the_TEM2DD ")" .
my_item = "TEM2DD("the_TEM2DD")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_TEM2DD = strip(the_TEM2DD)
if the_TEM2DD = "" then the_TEM2DD = the_TEM2DD_dflt
if strip(the_TEM2DD) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm TEM2DD() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end

                                       /* any garbage parms?  */
if strip(my_parms) <> "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Unrecognized parms ignored: "my_parms
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Valid parms are DEBUG() TEMPDD() TEM2DD() APPS() APPMASTR()"
   my_rc=unknown_parms_rc
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc


aparm.1="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_APPMASTR  " (STEM APP. FINIS"
aparm.2="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_APPS  " (STEM INA. FINIS"
aparm.3="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_SKIPDD  " (STEM SKP. FINIS"
aparm.4="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_SKIPADD  " (STEM SKA. FINIS"
aparm.0=4
do kk=1 to aparm.0 while my_rc=0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
      my_rc=error_rc
   end
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc


do kk=1 to INA.0
   if strip(INA.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(INA.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   needle=" "  word(INA.kk,1)  " "
   if pos(needle,APPlist)=0 then APPlist=APPlist  needle
end
drop INA.
do kk=1 to words(APPlist)
   APPLS.kk=word(APPlist,kk)
end
APPLS.0=words(APPlist)

APPS_dsn=""
x = LISTDSI(the_APPS "FILE")
if x <= 4 then do
   APPS_dsn = sysdsname
end
APPS_dsn=strip(APPS_dsn)
if APPS_dsn="" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
      "Unable to retrieve dataset name for DD "the_APPS
   my_rc=error_rc
end

parse var APPS_dsn LIBPFX ".APPS" rest
LIBPfx=strip(LIBPFX)
LIBPfx_l=length(LIBPFX)

descfpos=pos(' SysEnvironments',APP.1)
if descfpos=0 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "SysEnvironments header column missing in "the_APPMASTR
   my_rc=error_rc
   return error_rc
end
else do
  descfpos=descfpos+1
  descfend=descfpos
end
ll=length(APP.1)
done=0
do kk=descfpos to ll while \done
   if substr(APP.1,kk,1)<>" " then descfend=descfend+1
                              else done=1
end
descflen=descfend-descfpos+1


do kk= 2 to APP.0
   if strip(APP.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(APP.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   a=word(APP.kk,1)
   curr_env=" "  substr(APP.kk,descfpos,descflen)  " "
   found=0
   do jj=1 to words(curr_env) while \found
      w=word(curr_env,jj)
      if substr(w,1,4)<>"TEST" then iterate
      if w="TEST1" then st="A"
      if w="TEST2" then st="B"
      if w="TEST3" then st="C"
      if w="TEST4" then st="D"
      if w="TESTI" then st="R"
      found=1
  end
  if found then do
     ww=wordpos(a,APPlist)
     APPLS.ww.ENV=w
     APPLS.ww.STG=st
   end
end
drop APP.

return my_rc
./  ADD  NAME=ENDVTSMA
/* REXX */
/*======================================================*/
/*===  name   : ENDVCVMA                             ===*/
/*===  purpose: I create endevor add MAC from        ===*/
/*===           existing ESYM* datasets              ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*===  parms  : DEBUG      debug flag   Y/N          ===*/
/*===                      N is default              ===*/
/*===           PFX        Dataset pfx               ===*/
/*===           TEMPDD     DD to use for temp allocs ===*/
/*===                      TEMPDD is default         ===*/
/*===           APPS       DD for APPS input dset    ===*/
/*===                      APPS   is default         ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*======================================================*/

/* Changed CMNTOEND to LMSTOEND                                       */

parse upper arg my_parms
numeric digits 10
my_parms = " "  my_parms  " "    /* add spaces 4 parsing*/
my_rc = 0

                                       /* pull off debug parm */
                                       /* default is no debug */
                                       /* trace if debug=Y    */
parse var my_parms " DEBUG(" debug ")" .
my_item = "DEBUG("debug")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
debug = strip(debug)
if debug = "" then debug = "N"
if debug = "Y" then trace r
call do_init

do kk=1 to TODO.0 while my_rc=0
   my_rc=do_work(TODO.kk)
end
xx_rc=do_free(the_TEMPDD)

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    "RC="my_rc

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_work: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc
/*-------*/
arg DD flag app indsn outdsn

my_rc=0

p1=DD  " "  indsn
p2=DD  " "  outdsn
parse var indsn idsn "(" rest
p3=flag  " "  app  " "  strip(idsn)

if my_rc=0 then my_rc=do_alloc(p1)
if my_rc=0 then my_rc=get_mbrs(indsn)
if my_rc=0 then my_rc=do_alloc(p2)
if my_rc=0 then my_rc=gen_data(p3)
if my_rc=0 then my_rc=do_write(DD)

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_free:  procedure expose my_name debug error_rc
/*-------*/
arg DD

aparm="FREE FI("  DD  ")"

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)

return 0


/*-------*/
do_alloc: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc
/*-------*/
arg DD DSN

xx_rc=do_free(DD)

aparm="ALLOC FI("  DD  ") DSN('"  DSN  "') SHR REUSE"

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
io_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
if io_rc > 4 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm
   do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          omsg.i
   end
   return error_rc
end

return 0


/*-------*/
get_mbrs: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc MBRS.
/*-------*/
arg DSN

cnt=0
drop mud.
v = outtrap('mud.')
"LISTDS ('"DSN"') MEMBERS"
xx_rc=RC
if xx_rc>4 then return error_rc
v = outtrap(OFF)
do vv = 1 to mud.0 until strip(mud.vv) = "--MEMBERS--"
end
do vvv = vv+1 to mud.0
   x=strip(mud.vvv)
   cnt=cnt+1
   MBRS.cnt=x
end
MBRS.0=cnt

return 0


/*-------*/
do_write: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc DAT.
/*-------*/
arg DD

my_rc=0

if DAT.0=0 then do
   DAT.1="* "
   DAT.0=1
end

aparm.1="EXECIO "  DAT.0  " DISKW "  DD  " (STEM DAT. FINIS"
aparm.0=1

do kk=1 to aparm.0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
      my_rc=error_rc
   end
end

return my_rc


/*-------*/
gen_data: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc MBRS. DAT.
/*-------*/
parse arg flag app DSN

my_rc=0
dl=1
DAT.dl="SET TO ENVIRONMENT ADMIN STAGE Y SYSTEM ADMIN SUBSYSTEM ADMIN."
dl=dl+1
DAT.dl="SET OPTIONS CCID 'CMNMIGR' OVERRIDE SIGNOUT UPDATE."
dl=dl+1
DAT.dl="SET FROM DSNAME '"  DSN  "'."
do kk=1 to MBRS.0
   pmem=strip(MBRS.kk)
   xmem=translate(pmem,' ','@')
   xmem=translate(xmem,' ','#')
   if flag="Y" & xmem<>app then iterate
   dl=dl+1
   DAT.dl="* S M="  pmem
   dl=dl+1
   DAT.dl="ADD ELEMENT "  pmem  " TO TYPE MAC "
   dl=dl+1
   DAT.dl="   OPTIONS PRO GRO='MAC' "
   dl=dl+1
   DAT.dl=,
    '   COMMENTS "LMSTOEND: '  pmem  " "  date('U')  "@ "  time('N')  ,
    '".'
end

dl=dl+1
DAT.dl=,
"SET FROM ENVIRONMENT ADMIN STAGE Y SYSTEM ADMIN SUBSYSTEM ADMIN."
do kk=1 to MBRS.0
   pmem=strip(MBRS.kk)
   xmem=translate(pmem,' ','@')
   xmem=translate(xmem,' ','#')
   if flag="Y" & xmem<>app then iterate
   dl=dl+1
   DAT.dl="SIGNIN ELEMENT '"  pmem  "' FROM TYPE MAC."
end
DAT.0=dl

return my_rc

do_init:
/*------*/

parse source w1 w2 w3 w4 w5 w6 w7 w8
my_name = w3

error_rc        =8
unknown_parms_rc=4
TODO.0=0

the_PRX_dflt    =""
the_TEMPDD_dflt ="TEMPDD"
the_APPS_dflt   ="APPS"



                                       /* pull off PFX        */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " PFX(" the_PFX ")" .
my_item = "PFX("the_PFX")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_PFX = strip(the_PFX)
if the_PFX = "" then the_PFX = the_PFX_dflt
if strip(the_PFX) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm PFX() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end


                                       /* pull off APPS       */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " APPS(" the_APPS ")" .
my_item = "APPS("the_APPS")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_APPS = strip(the_APPS)
if the_APPS = "" then the_APPS = the_APPS_dflt
if strip(the_APPS) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm APPS() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end

                                       /* pull off TEMPDD     */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " TEMPDD(" the_TEMPDD ")" .
my_item = "TEMPDD("the_TEMPDD")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_TEMPDD = strip(the_TEMPDD)
if the_TEMPDD = "" then the_TEMPDD = the_TEMPDD_dflt
if strip(the_TEMPDD) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm TEMPDD() required"

                                       /* any garbage parms?  */
if strip(my_parms) <> "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Valid parms are DEBUG() PFX() TEMPDD()"
   my_rc=unknown_parms_rc
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc

aparm.1="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_APPS  " (STEM INP. FINIS"
