do kk=1 to aparm.0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
      my_rc=error_rc
   end
end
APPList=""
do kk=1 to INP.0 while my_rc=0
   if substr(INP.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   if strip(INP.kk)="" then iterate
   APPList=APPList  " "  word(INP.kk,1)
end
drop INP.

t=0

do kk=1 to words(APPList) while my_rc=0
   app=word(APPList,kk)
   t=t+1
   TODO.t=the_TEMPDD  " N "  app  " "  the_PFX  ".ESYMS "  ,
          the_PFX  ".#"  app  ".ADD2EN(ALLLIVE)"
   t=t+1
   TODO.t=the_TEMPDD  " N "  app  " "  the_PFX  ".ESYMSPIL "  ,
          the_PFX  ".#"  app  ".ADD2EN(ALLPILOT)"
   t=t+1
   TODO.t=the_TEMPDD  " N "  app  " "  the_PFX  ".ESYMSPRE "  ,
          the_PFX  ".#"  app  ".ADD2EN(ALLPREP)"
   t=t+1
   TODO.t=the_TEMPDD  " Y "  app  " "  the_PFX  ".ESYMS "  ,
          the_PFX  ".#"  app  ".ADD2EN(MACLIVE)"
   t=t+1
   TODO.t=the_TEMPDD  " Y "  app  " "  the_PFX  ".ESYMSPIL "  ,
          the_PFX  ".#"  app  ".ADD2EN(MACPILOT)"
   t=t+1
   TODO.t=the_TEMPDD  " Y "  app  " "  the_PFX  ".ESYMSPRE "  ,
          the_PFX  ".#"  app  ".ADD2EN(MACPREP)"
end
TODO.0=t


return my_rc
./  ADD  NAME=ENDVTSOP
/* REXX */
/*======================================================*/
/*===  name   : ENDVCVOP                             ===*/
/*===  purpose: I consolidate options into an        ===*/
/*===           opt2use file and apppts file         ===*/
/*===           for the conversion process           ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*===  parms  : DEBUG      debug flag   Y/N          ===*/
/*===                      N is default              ===*/
/*===           PFX        Endevor dataset prefix    ===*/
/*===           ADMIN      admin level to search     ===*/
/*===                      D/T/P                     ===*/
/*===           TEMPDD     DD to use for temp allocs ===*/
/*===                      default is TEMPDD         ===*/
/*===           APPS       DD containing APPS to     ===*/
/*===                      convert                   ===*/
/*===                      default is APPS           ===*/
/*===           APPDD      TEMP DD for application   ===*/
/*===                      options write             ===*/
/*===                      default is APPOPT         ===*/
/*===           APMDD      TEMP DD for application   ===*/
/*===                      member options write      ===*/
/*===                      default is APMOPT         ===*/
/*===           OPTDD      DD to write options to    ===*/
/*===                      default is OPT            ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*======================================================*/
parse upper arg my_parms
numeric digits 10
my_parms = " "  my_parms  " "    /* add spaces 4 parsing*/
my_rc = 0

                                       /* pull off debug parm */
                                       /* default is no debug */
                                       /* trace if debug=Y    */
parse var my_parms " DEBUG(" debug ")" .
my_item = "DEBUG("debug")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
debug = strip(debug)
if debug = "" then debug = "N"
if debug = "Y" then trace r

call do_init

aparm=the_TEMPDD  " "  the_APPDD  " "  the_OPTDD  " "  the_APMDD
if my_rc=0 then my_rc=do_work(aparm)

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    "RC="my_rc

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_work: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc OPTA. APPS. the_DPFX
/*-------*/
arg DD APPDD OPTDD APMDD

my_rc=0

                                             /* first write out     */
                                             /* consolidated options*/
if my_rc=0 then my_rc=do_open(OPTDD)

do kk=1 to OPTA.0 while my_rc=0
   if OPTA.kk.APP then iterate
   aparm=DD  " "  OPTA.kk
   my_rc=do_read(aparm)
   if my_rc=0 then my_rc=do_write(OPTDD)
   if my_rc=1 then my_rc=0
end
xx_rc=do_close(OPTDD)
junk_rc=do_free(OPTDD)
if xx_rc>my_rc then my_rc=xx_rc
if my_rc <> 0 then return my_rc


                                             /* now write out each  */
                                             /* app options         */
do jj = 1 to APPS.0 while my_rc=0
   zz_rc=error_rc
   apfx=the_DPFX  ".#"  APPS.jj
   lparm=APPDD  " "  the_DPFX  ".#"  APPS.jj  ".OPT2USE"
   if my_rc=0 then my_rc=do_free(APPDD)
   if my_rc=0 then my_rc=do_alloc(lparm)
   if my_rc=0 then my_rc=do_open(APPDD)
   done=0
   do kk=OPTA.0 to 1 by -1 while my_rc=0 & \done
      if \OPTA.kk.APP then iterate
      aparm=DD  " "  OPTA.kk  APPS.jj  ")"
      if my_rc=0 then my_rc=do_read(aparm)
      if my_rc=0 & OPTA.kk.APP then do
         done=1
         ax=INREC.0+1
         INREC.ax="ConvertPrefix="  apfx
         INREC.0=ax
         my_rc=do_write(APPDD)
         if my_rc=0 then do
            if xx_rc > my_rc then my_rc=xx_rc
         end
         zz_rc=0
      end
      if my_rc=1 then my_rc=0
   end
   xx_rc=do_close(APPDD)
   junk_rc=do_free(APPDD)
   if xx_rc>my_rc then my_rc=xx_rc
   if my_rc=0 & zz_rc=error_rc then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "Application conversion OPT member #C#"APPS.jj" not found"
      my_rc=zz_rc
   end
end
if my_rc <> 0 then return my_rc


                                             /* now write out each  */
                                             /* app options         */
do jj = 1 to APPS.0 while my_rc=0
   zz_rc=error_rc
   apfx=the_DPFX  ".#"  APPS.jj
   mparm=APMDD  " "  the_DPFX  ".#"  APPS.jj  ".OPT("  APPS.jj  ")"
   if my_rc=0 then my_rc=do_free(APMDD)
   if my_rc=0 then my_rc=do_alloc(mparm)
   done=0
   do kk=OPTA.0 to 1 by -1 while my_rc=0 & \done
      if \OPTA.kk.APP then iterate
      aparm=DD  " "  OPTA.kk  APPS.jj  ")"
      if my_rc=0 then my_rc=do_read(aparm)
      if my_rc=0 & OPTA.kk.APP then do
         done=1
         ax=INREC.0+1
         INREC.ax="ConvertPrefix="  apfx
         INREC.0=ax
         my_rc=do_write(APMDD)
         xx_rc=do_close(APMDD)
         if xx_rc > my_rc then my_rc=xx_rc
         zz_rc=0
      end
      if my_rc=1 then my_rc=0
   end
   junk_rc=do_free(APMDD)
   if xx_rc>my_rc then my_rc=xx_rc
end

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_alloc: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc
/*-------*/
arg DD DSN

my_rc=0
aparm="ALLOC FILE("  DD  ") DSN('"DSN"') SHR REUSE"

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
io_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
if io_rc > 4 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm
   do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          omsg.i
   end
   my_rc = error_rc
end

   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Allocating DD' "'"DD"'" 'to DSN' "'"DSN"'"

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_free: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc
/*-------*/
arg DD

aparm="FREE FI("  DD  ")"

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)

return 0

/*-------*/
do_open: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc
/*-------*/
arg DD

my_rc=0
aparm="EXECIO 0 DISKW "  DD

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
io_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
if io_rc > 4 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm
   do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          omsg.i
   end
   my_rc = error_rc
end

return my_rc

/*-------*/
do_write: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc INREC.
/*-------*/
arg DD

my_rc=0
aparm="EXECIO "  INREC.0  " DISKW "  DD  " (STEM INREC."

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
io_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
if io_rc > 4 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm
   do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          omsg.i
   end
   my_rc = error_rc
end

   Say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Records written to DD' "'"DD"'" '=' INREC.0

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_close: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc
/*-------*/
arg DD

my_rc=0

aparm="EXECIO 0 DISKW "  DD  " (FINIS"
x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
io_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
if io_rc > 4 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm
   do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          omsg.i
   end
   my_rc = error_rc
end

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_read: procedure expose my_name debug INREC. error_rc
/*-------*/
arg DD DSN

my_rc=0

qdset="'"  DSN  "'"
if sysdsn(qdset)<>"OK" then return 1

aparm.1="ALLOC FILE("  DD  ") DSN('"DSN"') SHR REUSE"
aparm.2="EXECIO * DISKR "  DD  " (STEM INREC. FINIS"
aparm.0=2

x=OUTTRAP("msg.")
address "TSO" "FREE FI("DD")"
x=OUTTRAP(OFF)

do kk=1 to aparm.0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
      my_rc=error_rc
   end
end

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Allocating DSN =' "'"DSN"'"
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Records Read   =' "'"INREC.0"'"

x=OUTTRAP("msg.")
address "TSO" "FREE FI("DD")"
x=OUTTRAP(OFF)


return my_rc


/*------*/
do_init:
/*------*/

parse source w1 w2 w3 w4 w5 w6 w7 w8
my_name = w3

error_rc        =8
unknown_parms_rc=4
interested_in   =" OPT "
LIBSFX.0        =0
the_TEMPDD_dflt ="TEMPDD"
the_APPDD_dflt  ="APPDD"
the_APMDD_dflt  ="APMDD"
the_OPTDD_dflt  ="OPT2USE"
the_APPS_dflt   ="APPS"
the_DPFX_dflt   =""
the_PFX_dflt    =""
the_ADMIN_dflt  =""
the_ADMIN_values=" D T P "



                                       /* pull off APPS       */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " APPS(" the_APPS ")" .
my_item = "APPS("the_APPS")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_APPS = strip(the_APPS)
if the_APPS = "" then the_APPS = the_APPS_dflt
if strip(the_APPS) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm APPS() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end





                                       /* pull off APPDD      */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " APPDD(" the_APPDD ")" .
my_item = "APPDD("the_APPDD")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_APPDD = strip(the_APPDD)
if the_APPDD = "" then the_APPDD = the_APPDD_dflt
if strip(the_APPDD) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm APPDD() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end


                                       /* pull off APMDD      */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " APMDD(" the_APMDD ")" .
my_item = "APMDD("the_APMDD")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_APMDD = strip(the_APMDD)
if the_APMDD = "" then the_APMDD = the_APMDD_dflt
if strip(the_APMDD) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm APMDD() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end

                                       /* pull off OPTDD      */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " OPTDD(" the_OPTDD ")" .
my_item = "OPTDD("the_OPTDD")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_OPTDD = strip(the_OPTDD)
if the_OPTDD = "" then the_OPTDD = the_OPTDD_dflt
if strip(the_OPTDD) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm OPTDD() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end


                                       /* pull off DPFX       */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " DPFX(" the_DPFX ")" .
my_item = "DPFX("the_DPFX")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_DPFX = strip(the_DPFX)
if the_DPFX = "" then the_DPFX = the_DPFX_dflt
if strip(the_DPFX) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm DPFX() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end

                                       /* pull off PFX        */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " PFX(" the_PFX ")" .
my_item = "PFX("the_PFX")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_PFX = strip(the_PFX)
if the_PFX = "" then the_PFX = the_PFX_dflt
if strip(the_PFX) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm PFX() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end



                                       /* pull off ADMIN      */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " ADMIN(" the_ADMIN ")" .
my_item = "ADMIN("the_ADMIN")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_ADMIN = strip(the_ADMIN)
if the_ADMIN = "" then the_ADMIN = the_ADMIN_dflt
if strip(the_ADMIN) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm ADMIN() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end
else do
   needle=" "  the_ADMIN  " "
   if pos(needle,the_ADMIN_values)=0 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time('L'),16),
          "Parm ADMIN() must be one of "the_ADMIN_values
      my_rc = error_rc
   end
end


                                       /* pull off TEMPDD     */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " TEMPDD(" the_TEMPDD ")" .
my_item = "TEMPDD("the_TEMPDD")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_TEMPDD = strip(the_TEMPDD)
if the_TEMPDD = "" then the_TEMPDD = the_TEMPDD_dflt
if strip(the_TEMPDD) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm TEMPDD() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end




                                       /* any garbage parms?  */
if strip(my_parms) <> "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Unrecognized parms ignored: "my_parms
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Valid parms are DEBUG() PFX() TEMPDD() ADMIN() APPS() DPFX()"
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "                OPTDD() APPDD() APMDD()                     "
   my_rc=unknown_parms_rc
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc

                                         /* fill in OPTA array with */
                                         /* datasets to search for  */
                                         /* options                 */
                                         /* ordering will be        */
                                         /* Prod, Test, ADMIND  */
                                         /* the ADMIN() parm tells  */
                                         /* us the lowest level to  */
                                         /* search                  */

                                         /* the order is important  */
                                         /* as the last value wins  */

ocnt =0
l    =length(the_PFX)
enode=substr(the_PFX,l,1)

                                         /* first the DEFAULT option*/
p=wordpos(the_ADMIN,the_ADMIN_values)
do kk = words(the_ADMIN_values) to p by -1
   ocnt=ocnt+1
   OPTA.ocnt=the_PFX  ".ADMIN"  word(the_ADMIN_values,kk)  ,
             ".OPT(DEFAULT)"
   OPTA.ocnt.APP=0
end
                                         /* next the facility option*/
do kk = words(the_ADMIN_values) to p by -1
   ocnt=ocnt+1
   OPTA.ocnt=the_PFX  ".ADMIN"  word(the_ADMIN_values,kk)  ,
             ".OPT(DEFAULT"  enode  ")"
   OPTA.ocnt.APP=0
end
                                         /* next the app conversion */
                                         /* option                  */
do kk = words(the_ADMIN_values) to p by -1
   ocnt=ocnt+1
   OPTA.ocnt=the_PFX  ".ADMIN"  word(the_ADMIN_values,kk)  ,
             ".OPT(#C#"
   OPTA.ocnt.APP=1
end
OPTA.0=ocnt

   Do o = 1 to OPTA.0
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          'OPTA.'o '=' "'"OPTA.o"'"
   End o

aparm="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_APPS  " (FINIS STEM INP."

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
io_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
if io_rc > 4 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm
   do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          omsg.i
   end
   my_rc = error_rc
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc

cnt=0
do kk=1 to INP.0
   if strip(INP.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(INP.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   cnt=cnt+1
   APPS.cnt=word(INP.kk,1)
end
APPS.0=cnt

   Do a = 1 to APPS.0
      Say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          'APPS.'a '=' "'"APPS.a"'"
   End a

return my_rc
./  ADD  NAME=ENDVTSWC
/* REXX */
/*======================================================*/
/*===  name   : ENDVTSWC                             ===*/
/*===  purpose: used endevor conversion process      ===*/
/*===           to generate SCL to delete all types  ===*/
/*===           subsystems and systems               ===*/
/*===           ... ugly and cheap way out...        ===*/
/*===           ... was hitting abends and           ===*/
/*===               inconsistent output using api    ===*/
/*===  parms  : DEBUG()   - debug flag Y/N N=deflt   ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*======================================================*/

/* Replaced hard-coded Environments and Stage 2 ID values with file   */
/* EXTRSTG                                                            */

parse upper arg my_parms
numeric digits 10
my_parms = " "  my_parms  " "    /* add spaces 4 parsing*/
my_rc = 0

                                       /* pull off debug parm */
                                       /* default is no debug */
                                       /* trace if debug=Y    */
parse var my_parms " DEBUG(" debug ")" .
my_item = "DEBUG("debug")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
debug = strip(debug)
if debug = "" then debug = "N"
if debug = "Y" then trace r

call do_init

if my_rc=0 then my_rc=do_work(the_OUTDD)

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    "RC="my_rc

return my_rc

/**********************************************************************/
/*-------*/
do_work: procedure expose my_name error_rc the_APP env_list typ_list,
   e s
/*-------*/
arg DD

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'do_work: Begin'

my_rc=0

ocnt=0
/* For each Environment in this App ...                               */
do kk=1 to words(env_list) while my_rc=0
   envr = word(env_list,kk)
   ww   = wordpos(envr,e)
   if ww=0 then iterate

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       '   Processing' the_APP 'Environment' "'"envr"'"

   stage=word(s,ww)
/* For each Type in Endevor, build a Delete Type.                     */
   do jj=1 to words(typ_list) while my_rc=0
      typ=word(typ_list,jj)
      ocnt=ocnt+1
      O.ocnt=" DELETE TYPE '"  typ  "' FROM ENVIRONMENT '"  envr  "'"
      ocnt=ocnt+1
      O.ocnt="  SYSTEM '"  the_APP  "' STAGE ID '"  stage  "' ."
      ocnt=ocnt+1
      O.ocnt=" DELETE TYPE '"  typ  "' FROM ENVIRONMENT '"  envr  "'"
      ocnt=ocnt+1
      O.ocnt="  SYSTEM '"  the_APP  "' STAGE NUMBER 1 ."
      ocnt=ocnt+1
      O.ocnt=" DELETE TYPE '"  typ  "' FROM ENVIRONMENT '"  envr  "'"
      ocnt=ocnt+1
      O.ocnt="  SYSTEM '"  the_APP  "' STAGE NUMBER 2 ."
   end jj

/* For each Subsytem, build a Delete Subsytem                         */
   ocnt=ocnt+1
   O.ocnt=" DELETE SUBSYSTEM 'BASE' FROM ENVIRONMENT '"  envr  ,
          "' SYSTEM '"  the_APP  "' ."

/* For each TEST* Environment, build a Delete Subsytem for REL*       */
   if substr(envr,1,4)='TEST' then do
      ocnt=ocnt+1
      O.ocnt=" DELETE SUBSYSTEM 'REL1' FROM ENVIRONMENT '"  envr  ,
             "' SYSTEM '"  the_APP  "' ."
      ocnt=ocnt+1
      O.ocnt=" DELETE SUBSYSTEM 'REL2' FROM ENVIRONMENT '"  envr  ,
             "' SYSTEM '"  the_APP  "' ."
      ocnt=ocnt+1
      O.ocnt=" DELETE SUBSYSTEM 'REL3' FROM ENVIRONMENT '"  envr  ,
             "' SYSTEM '"  the_APP  "' ."
      ocnt=ocnt+1
      O.ocnt=" DELETE SUBSYSTEM 'REL4' FROM ENVIRONMENT '"  envr  ,
             "' SYSTEM '"  the_APP  "' ."
   end

/* Build a Delete System                                              */
   ocnt=ocnt+1
   O.ocnt=" DELETE SYSTEM '"  the_APP  "' FROM ENVIRONMENT '"  envr  ,
         "' ."
end
O.0=ocnt

my_rc=0
aparm="EXECIO "  O.0  " DISKW "  DD  " (STEM O. FINIS"

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
io_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
if io_rc > 4 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm
   do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          omsg.i
   end
   my_rc=error_rc
end

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       ' '
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       '   Records Written to DD' DD '=' O.0

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'do_work: End  '

return my_rc

/**********************************************************************/
/*------*/
do_init:
/*------*/

parse source w1 w2 w3 w4 w5 w6 w7 w8
my_name = w3

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'do_init: Begin'

error_rc=8
unknown_parms_rc=4

app_list=""
the_APP_dflt        = ""
the_OUTDD_dflt      = "OUTDD"
the_TYPWACK_dflt    = "TYPWACK"
the_EXTRSYS_dflt    = "EXTRSYS"
the_EXTRSTG_dflt    = "EXTRSTG"


                                       /* pull off TYPWACK    */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " TYPWACK(" the_TYPWACK ")" .
my_item = "TYPWACK("the_TYPWACK")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_TYPWACK = strip(the_TYPWACK)
if the_TYPWACK = "" then the_TYPWACK = the_TYPWACK_dflt
if strip(the_TYPWACK) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Parm TYPWACK() required"
   my_rc=error_rc
end


                                       /* pull off EXTRSYS    */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " EXTRSYS(" the_EXTRSYS ")" .
my_item = "EXTRSYS("the_EXTRSYS")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_EXTRSYS = strip(the_EXTRSYS)
if the_EXTRSYS = "" then the_EXTRSYS = the_EXTRSYS_dflt
if strip(the_EXTRSYS) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Parm EXTRSYS() required"
   my_rc=error_rc
end
                                       /* pull off OUTDD      */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " OUTDD(" the_OUTDD ")" .
my_item = "OUTDD("the_OUTDD")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_OUTDD = strip(the_OUTDD)
if the_OUTDD = "" then the_OUTDD = the_OUTDD_dflt
if strip(the_OUTDD) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Parm OUTDD() required"
   my_rc=error_rc
end

                                       /* pull off APP        */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " APP(" the_APP ")" .
my_item = "APP("the_APP")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_APP = strip(the_APP)
if the_APP = "" then the_APP = the_APP_dflt
if strip(the_APP) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Parm APP() required"
   my_rc=error_rc
end

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Processing APP               =' "'"the_APP"'"

/* Begin EXTRSTG                                                      */
                                       /* pull off EXTRSTG    */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " EXTRSTG(" the_EXTRSTG ")" .
my_item = "EXTRSTG("the_EXTRSTG")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_EXTRSTG = strip(the_EXTRSTG)
if the_EXTRSTG = "" then the_EXTRSTG = the_EXTRSTG_dflt
if strip(the_EXTRSTG) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Parm EXTRSTG() required"
   my_rc=error_rc
end
/* End   EXTRSTG                                                      */

                                       /* any garbage parms?  */
if strip(my_parms) <> "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Unrecognized parms ignored: "my_parms
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "Valid parms are DEBUG() APP() EXTRSYS() TYPWACK() EXTRSTG()"
   my_rc=unknown_parms_rc
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc


aparm.1="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_EXTRSYS  " (STEM INS. FINIS "
aparm.2="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_TYPWACK  " (STEM INT. FINIS "
aparm.3="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_EXTRSTG  " (STEM STG. FINIS "
aparm.0=3

do kk=1 to aparm.0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
      my_rc=error_rc
      return error_rc
   end
end

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Records Read from DD' the_EXTRSYS '=' INS.0
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Records Read from DD' the_TYPWACK '=' INT.0
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Records Read from DD' the_EXTRSTG '=' STG.0

env_list=""
typ_list=""
do kk=1 to INS.0 while my_rc=0
   if strip(INS.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(INS.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   if the_APP=word(INS.kk,1) then do
      env_list=env_list  " "  word(INS.kk,2)  " "
   end
   if the_APP<word(INS.kk,1) then leave
end
drop INS.

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Environments in' the_APP '=' Words( env_list)
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Environments in' the_APP '=' "'"env_list"'"

do kk=1 to INT.0 while my_rc=0
   if strip(INT.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(INT.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   typ_list=typ_list  " "  word(INT.kk,1)  " "
end
drop INT.

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Types in Endevor         =' Words( typ_list)

/* Build Environment Names and Stage 2 IDs                            */
   stg_list=""
   sid_list=""
   do kk=1 to STG.0 while my_rc=0
      if strip(STG.kk)=""       then iterate
      if substr(STG.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate

/*    Extract Environment Name */
      stg_list = stg_list    " "    word( STG.kk, 1)   " "

/*    Extract Stage 2 ID       */
      sid_list = sid_list    " "    Word( STG.kk, 4)   " "

   end kk
   drop STG.

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Environments in Endevor  =' Words( stg_list)

   e = stg_list
   s = sid_list

   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Environments in Endevor  =' "'"e"'"
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'Stage 2 IDs  in Endevor  =' "'"s"'"


   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       'do_init: End'
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       ' '

return my_rc

/**********************************************************************/
./  ADD  NAME=ENDVTSXM
/* REXX */
/*======================================================*/
/*===  name   : ENDVCVXM                             ===*/
/*===  purpose: I create dummyxml , apps in format   ===*/
/*===           for hallahan hidden code ,           ===*/
/*===           recall datasets                      ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*===  parms  : DEBUG      debug flag   Y/N          ===*/
/*===                      N is default              ===*/
/*===           APPS       APPS  DD name             ===*/
/*===                      APPS  is default          ===*/
/*===           APPSO      DD to rewrite APPS to     ===*/
/*===                      APPSO is default          ===*/
/*===           DUMMYXML   DD to write DUMMYXML to   ===*/
/*===                      DUMMYXML is default       ===*/
/*===           DPFX       dataset prefix            ===*/
/*===           ENODE      Endevor node              ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*======================================================*/
parse upper arg my_parms
numeric digits 10
my_parms = " "  my_parms  " "    /* add spaces 4 parsing*/
my_rc = 0

                                       /* pull off debug parm */
                                       /* default is no debug */
                                       /* trace if debug=Y    */
parse var my_parms " DEBUG(" debug ")" .
my_item = "DEBUG("debug")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
debug = strip(debug)
if debug = "" then debug = "N"
if debug = "Y" then trace r
call do_init

do jj=1 to words(APPlist) while my_rc=0
   typ_list=""
   ap=word(APPlist,jj)
   aphold=ap
   if length(ap)>4 then aphold=substr(ap,1,4)
   write_parm=the_DUMMYXML  " "  ap
   write_parm2=the_APPSTYPE  " "  ap
   libpfx="YourHQL.CHGMAN."  aphold  ".BASE"
   libpfx_l=length(libpfx)
   x = outtrap('mud.')
   "LISTC LVL("libpfx")"
   lc_rc=RC
   x = outtrap(OFF)
   if lc_rc > 4 then do
      my_rc=error_r
      iterate
   end
   do mmm = 1 to mud.trapped
      parse var mud.mmm w1 w2 w3 .
      if strip(w1) = "NONVSAM" then do
         w3tail=translate(delstr(w3,1,libpfx_l),' ','.')
         if words(w3tail)=1 then do
            my_rc=do_recall(w3)
            if word(w3tail,1)="PSB"   word(w3tail,1)="PSL" then do
               needle=" PSO "
               if pos(needle,typ_list)=0  then,
                  typ_list=typ_list  needle
            end
            if word(w3tail,1)="MFS" then do
               needle=" MFR "
               if pos(needle,typ_list)=0  then,
                  typ_list=typ_list  needle
            end
            needle=" "  word(w3tail,1)  " "
            if pos(needle,typ_list)<>0    then iterate
            if pos(needle,exclude_typ)<>0 then iterate
            if pos(needle,valid_typ)=0    then iterate
            typ_list=typ_list  needle
         end
      end
   end
   my_rc=do_write(write_parm2)
   if write_XML then my_rc=do_write(write_parm)
end

xx_rc=do_close(the_APPSTYPE)
if xx_rc>my_rc then my_rc=xx_rc
if write_XML then do
   xx_rc=do_close(the_DUMMYXML)
   if xx_rc>my_rc then my_rc=xx_rc
end

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    "RC="my_rc

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_recall:  procedure expose my_name debug error_rc
/*-------*/
arg dsn

my_rc = 0

x = "'"  strip(dsn)  "' RECALL"
r = "HRECALL DSNAME('"  strip(dsn)  "') WAIT"
if LISTDSI(x) = 0 then return my_rc
say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    r
x = outtrap('mud.')
address TSO r
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_write: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc typ_list
/*-------*/
arg DD app

c=0
do kk=1 to words(typ_list)
   c=c+1
   CC.c=left(app,9)  left(word(typ_list,kk),9)
end
CC.0=c

aparm="EXECIO "  CC.0  " DISKW "  DD  " (STEM CC."

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
io_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
if io_rc > 4 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm
   do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          omsg.i
   end
   return error_rc
end
return 0


/*-------*/
do_close: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc
/*-------*/
arg DD

my_rc=0

aparm="EXECIO 0 DISKW "  DD  " (FINIS"
x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
io_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
if io_rc > 4 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm
   do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          omsg.i
   end
   my_rc = error_rc
end

return my_rc



/*------*/
do_init:
/*------*/

parse source w1 w2 w3 w4 w5 w6 w7 w8
my_name = w3

error_rc        =8
unknown_parms_rc=4
APPlist         =""
XML_list        =""
exclude_typ     =" DELTA PKG DBB $BC "
valid_typ       =""
write_XML       =0

the_LMSTOEND_dflt="LMSTOEND"
the_APPS_dflt    ="APPS"
the_APPSO_dflt   ="APPSO"
the_APPSTYPE_dflt="APPSTYPE"
the_DUMMYXML_dflt="DUMMYXML"
the_DPFX_dflt    =""
the_ENODE_dflt   =""



                                       /* pull off LMSTOEND   */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " LMSTOEND(" the_LMSTOEND ")" .
my_item = "LMSTOEND("the_LMSTOEND")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_LMSTOEND = strip(the_LMSTOEND)
if the_LMSTOEND = "" then the_LMSTOEND = the_LMSTOEND_dflt
if strip(the_LMSTOEND) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm LMSTOEND() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end

                                       /* pull off APPS       */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " APPS(" the_APPS ")" .
my_item = "APPS("the_APPS")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_APPS = strip(the_APPS)
if the_APPS = "" then the_APPS = the_APPS_dflt
if strip(the_APPS) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm APPS() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end

                                       /* pull off APPSTYPE   */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " APPSTYPE(" the_APPSTYPE ")" .
my_item = "APPSTYPE("the_APPSTYPE")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_APPSTYPE = strip(the_APPSTYPE)
if the_APPSTYPE = "" then the_APPSTYPE = the_APPSTYPE_dflt
if strip(the_APPSTYPE) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm APPSTYPE() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end



                                       /* pull off APPSO      */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " APPSO(" the_APPSO ")" .
my_item = "APPSO("the_APPSO")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_APPSO = strip(the_APPSO)
if the_APPSO = "" then the_APPSO = the_APPSO_dflt
if strip(the_APPSO) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm APPSO() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end



                                       /* pull off DUMMYXML   */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " DUMMYXML(" the_DUMMYXML ")" .
my_item = "DUMMYXML("the_DUMMYXML")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_DUMMYXML = strip(the_DUMMYXML)
if the_DUMMYXML = "" then the_DUMMYXML = the_DUMMYXML_dflt
if strip(the_DUMMYXML) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm DUMMYXML() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end



                                       /* pull off ENODE      */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " ENODE(" the_ENODE ")" .
my_item = "ENODE("the_ENODE")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_ENODE = strip(the_ENODE)
if the_ENODE = "" then the_ENODE = the_ENODE_dflt
if strip(the_ENODE) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm ENODE() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end





                                       /* any garbage parms?  */
if strip(my_parms) <> "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Unrecognized parms ignored: "my_parms
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Valid parms are DEBUG() APPS() APPSO() ENODE() DUMMYXML()"
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "               LMSTOEND() APPSTYPE()"
   my_rc=unknown_parms_rc
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc

needle=" "  the_ENODE  " "
if pos(needle,XML_list)<>0 then write_XML=1

aparm.1="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_APPS  " (STEM INP. FINIS"
aparm.0=1

do kk=1 to aparm.0 while my_rc=0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
      my_rc = error_rc
   end
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc

AO.0=0
APPList=""
HALList=""
do kk=1 to INP.0
   if strip(INP.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(INP.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   needle=" "  word(INP.kk,1)  " "
   if pos(needle,APPList)<>0 then iterate
   APPlist=APPlist  needle
   ac=word(INP.kk,1)
   if length(ac)=5 then needle=" "  substr(ac,1,4)  " "
   if pos(needle,HALList)<>0 then iterate
   HALlist=HALlist  needle
   a=AO.0+1
   AO.a=strip(needle)
   AO.0=a
end
drop INP.

                                  /* write apps left justified + */
                                  /* no comments so hallahans    */
                                  /* hidden code does not choke  */
aparm.1="EXECIO * DISKW "  the_APPSO  " (STEM AO. FINIS"
aparm.0=1

do kk=1 to aparm.0 while my_rc=0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
      my_rc = error_rc
   end
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc
drop AO.

aparm.1="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_LMSTOEND  " (STEM INT. FINIS"
aparm.0=1

do kk=1 to aparm.0 while my_rc=0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
      my_rc = error_rc
   end
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc

do kk=1 to INT.0
   if strip(INT.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(INT.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   needle=" "  word(INT.kk,1)  " "
   if pos(needle,valid_typ)<>0 then iterate
   valid_typ=valid_typ  needle
end
drop INT.


return my_rc
./  ADD  NAME=ENDVTSXX
/* REXX */
/*======================================================*/
/*===  name   : ENDVCVXX                             ===*/
/*===  purpose: I fix apps types list from 100 rpt   ===*/
/*===           extracts                             ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*===  parms  : DEBUG      debug flag   Y/N          ===*/
/*===                      N is default              ===*/
/*===           APPS       APPS    DD name           ===*/
/*===                      APPS  is default          ===*/
/*===           APPSTYPE   APPSTYPE DD name          ===*/
/*===                      APPSTYPE  is default      ===*/
/*===           RPT100C    RPT100C DD name           ===*/
/*===                      RPT100C is default        ===*/
/*===           RPT100D    RPT100D DD name           ===*/
/*===                      RPT100D is default        ===*/
/*===           RPT100E    RPT100E DD name           ===*/
/*===                      RPT100E is default        ===*/
/*===                                                ===*/
/*======================================================*/
parse upper arg my_parms
numeric digits 10
my_parms = " "  my_parms  " "    /* add spaces 4 parsing*/
my_rc = 0

                                       /* pull off debug parm */
                                       /* default is no debug */
                                       /* trace if debug=Y    */
parse var my_parms " DEBUG(" debug ")" .
my_item = "DEBUG("debug")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
debug = strip(debug)
if debug = "" then debug = "N"
if debug = "Y" then trace r
call do_init

if my_rc=0 then my_rc=do_write(the_APPSTYPE)

say left(my_name,9),
    left(time("L"),16),
    "RC="my_rc

return my_rc


/*-------*/
do_write: procedure expose my_name debug error_rc curr_types ,
                           exclude_typ exclude_pfx full_types
/*-------*/
arg DD

c=0
do kk=1 to words(curr_types)
   x=translate(word(curr_types,kk),' ','-')
   app=word(x,1)
   typ=word(x,2)
   ty2=substr(typ,1,2)
 say left(app,8)' 'left(typ,8)
   if wordpos(typ,exclude_typ)<>0 then iterate
   if wordpos(ty2,exclude_pfx)<>0 then iterate
   if substr(typ,1,1)='$'         then iterate
   c=c+1
   CC.c=left(app,9)  left(typ,9)
   needle=word(curr_types,kk)  "-"
   p=pos(needle,full_types)
   if p=0 then iterate
   l=length(needle)
   if p<>1 then holds=delstr(full_types,1,p-1)
   x=translate(word(holds,1),' ','-')
   if words(x) < 5 then iterate
   lt=word(x,3)
   lb=word(x,4)
   ld=word(x,5)
   CC.c=CC.c  left(lt,9)  left(lb,45)  left(ld,45)
end
CC.0=c

aparm="EXECIO "  CC.0  " DISKW "  DD  " (STEM CC. FINIS"

x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
address "TSO" aparm
io_rc = RC
x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
if io_rc > 4 then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time("L"),16),
       "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm
   do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          omsg.i
   end
   return error_rc
end
return 0



/*------*/
do_init:
/*------*/

parse source w1 w2 w3 w4 w5 w6 w7 w8
my_name = w3

error_rc        =8
unknown_parms_rc=4
APPlist         =""
no_XML_list     =" A C Z "
no_XML_list     =" "
exclude_typ     =" DELTA PKG DBB $BC DBR LDP LDI LOD MFR FMT PSL "  ,
                 "LSA LDM LSI LSJ LST DBL MFR GRP SRU DM1 LOU"
exclude_pfx     =" IM IS NM NS WM WS "
valid_typ       =""
curr_types      =""
write_XML       =0

the_LMSTOEND_dflt="LMSTOEND"
the_APPS_dflt    ="APPS"
the_APPSTYPE_dflt="APPSTYPE"
the_RPT100C_dflt ="RPT100C"
the_RPT100D_dflt ="RPT100D"
the_RPT100E_dflt ="RPT100E"



                                       /* pull off LMSTOEND   */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " LMSTOEND(" the_LMSTOEND ")" .
my_item = "LMSTOEND("the_LMSTOEND")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_LMSTOEND = strip(the_LMSTOEND)
if the_LMSTOEND = "" then the_LMSTOEND = the_LMSTOEND_dflt
if strip(the_LMSTOEND) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm LMSTOEND() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end

                                       /* pull off APPS       */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " APPS(" the_APPS ")" .
my_item = "APPS("the_APPS")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_APPS = strip(the_APPS)
if the_APPS = "" then the_APPS = the_APPS_dflt
if strip(the_APPS) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm APPS() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end

                                       /* pull off APPSTYPE   */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " APPSTYPE(" the_APPSTYPE ")" .
my_item = "APPSTYPE("the_APPSTYPE")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_APPSTYPE = strip(the_APPSTYPE)
if the_APPSTYPE = "" then the_APPSTYPE = the_APPSTYPE_dflt
if strip(the_APPSTYPE) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm APPSTYPE() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end

                                       /* pull off RPT100C    */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " RPT100C(" the_RPT100C ")" .
my_item = "RPT100C("the_RPT100C")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_RPT100C = strip(the_RPT100C)
if the_RPT100C = "" then the_RPT100C = the_RPT100C_dflt
if strip(the_RPT100C) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm RPT100C() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end

                                       /* pull off RPT100D    */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " RPT100D(" the_RPT100D ")" .
my_item = "RPT100D("the_RPT100D")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_RPT100D = strip(the_RPT100D)
if the_RPT100D = "" then the_RPT100D = the_RPT100D_dflt
if strip(the_RPT100D) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm RPT100D() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end

                                       /* pull off RPT100E    */
                                       /* parm.               */
parse var my_parms " RPT100E(" the_RPT100E ")" .
my_item = "RPT100E("the_RPT100E")"
my_ndx = wordpos(my_item,my_parms)
if my_ndx > 0 then my_parms = delword(my_parms,my_ndx,1)
the_RPT100E = strip(the_RPT100E)
if the_RPT100E = "" then the_RPT100E = the_RPT100E_dflt
if strip(the_RPT100E) = "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Parm RPT100E() required"
   my_rc = error_rc
end





                                       /* any garbage parms?  */
if strip(my_parms) <> "" then do
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Unrecognized parms ignored: "my_parms
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "Valid parms are DEBUG() APPS() APPSTYPE() RPT100D()"
   say left(my_name,9),
       left(time('L'),16),
       "               LMSTOEND() RPT100D() RPT100E()"
   my_rc=unknown_parms_rc
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc


aparm.1="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_APPS  " (STEM INP. FINIS"
aparm.2="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_APPSTYPE  " (STEM APT. FINIS"
aparm.3="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_RPT100D  " (STEM R1D. FINIS"
aparm.4="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_RPT100E  " (STEM R1E. FINIS"
aparm.5="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_RPT100C  " (STEM R1C. FINIS"
aparm.6="EXECIO * DISKR "  the_LMSTOEND  " (STEM INT. FINIS"
aparm.0=6

do kk=1 to aparm.0 while my_rc=0
   x = OUTTRAP("omsg.")
   address "TSO" aparm.kk
   io_rc = RC
   x = OUTTRAP(OFF)
   if io_rc > 4 then do
      say left(my_name,9),
          left(time("L"),16),
          "ERROR RC="io_rc" for "aparm.kk
      do i = 1 to omsg.trapped
         say left(my_name,9),
             left(time("L"),16),
             omsg.i
      end
      my_rc = error_rc
   end
end
if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc

APPList=""
do kk=1 to INP.0
   if strip(INP.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(INP.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   needle=" "  word(INP.kk,1)  " "
   if pos(needle,APPList)<>0 then iterate
   APPlist=APPlist  needle
end
drop INP.

if my_rc > 4 then return my_rc
drop AO.

do kk=1 to INT.0
   if strip(INT.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(INT.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   needle=" "  word(INT.kk,1)  " "
   if pos(needle,valid_typ)<>0 then iterate
   valid_typ=valid_typ  needle
end
drop INT.

do kk=1 to APT.0
   if strip(APT.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(APT.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   needle=" "  word(APT.kk,1)  "-"  word(APT.kk,2)  " "
   if pos(needle,curr_types)<>0 then iterate
   curr_types=curr_types  needle
end
drop APT.

do kk=1 to R1C.0
   if strip(R1C.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(R1C.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   needle=" "  word(R1C.kk,1)
   if pos(needle,APPList)=0 then iterate
   needle=" "  word(R1C.kk,3)
   if pos(needle,valid_typ)=0 then iterate
   needle=" "  word(R1C.kk,1)  "-"  word(R1C.kk,3)  " "
   if pos(needle,curr_types)<>0 then iterate
   curr_types=curr_types  needle
end
drop R1C.

full_types=' '
do kk=1 to R1D.0
   if strip(R1D.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(R1D.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   needle=" "  word(R1D.kk,1)
   if pos(needle,APPList)=0 then iterate
   needle=" "  word(R1D.kk,2)
   if pos(needle,valid_typ)=0 then iterate
   if substr(word(R1D.kk,3),1,1)<>'&' then ,
     full_types=full_types  " "  word(R1D.kk,1)  "-"  word(R1D.kk,2)  ,
                "-7-"  word(R1D.kk,3)  "-"  word(R1D.kk,3)  ".DELTA "
   needle=" "  word(R1D.kk,1)  "-"  word(R1D.kk,2)  " "
   if pos(needle,curr_types)<>0 then iterate
   curr_types=curr_types  needle
end
drop R1D.

do kk=1 to R1E.0
   if strip(R1E.kk)=""       then iterate
   if substr(R1E.kk,1,1)="*" then iterate
   needle=" "  word(R1E.kk,1)
   if pos(needle,APPList)=0 then iterate
   needle=" "  word(R1E.kk,2)
   if pos(needle,valid_typ)=0 then iterate
   needle=" "  word(R1E.kk,1)  "-"  word(R1E.kk,2)  " "
   if pos(needle,curr_types)<>0 then iterate
   curr_types=curr_types  needle
end
drop R1E.

return my_rc

./  ADD  NAME=ENDLDFLT
/*    REXX     */
    TRACE o ;
/*                                                                   */
/* Determine the Defaults table name for the system we are on        */
/*                                                                   */
   glid = mvsVAR('symdef','GLBLID')
   if glid = 'SY1' then,
      glid = 'SYT'
/* This is a temporary Changes made 05/07/12 LAT to Correct LPAR */
   if glid = 'SYD9' then,
      glid = 'SY9'
   MyDefaultsTable = 'C1DEF'    glid ;
/*                                                                   */
   Queue "*Envname  Stg1ID Stg1nme   Stg2ID Stg2nme  Entrystg#",
          "AdminEnv "

/*                                                                   */
 ADDRESS LINKMVS 'LOADTABL' 'MyDefaultsTable'
 C1DEFLTS_ADDR = C2X(TBLADDR) ;
 SAY "C1DEFLTS_ADDR =" C1DEFLTS_ADDR ;
 POINTER_ADDR = D2X(    X2D(C1DEFLTS_ADDR) + X2D(055)      )
 NUMBER_OF_ENVIRONMENTS = C2D(STORAGE(POINTER_ADDR,01));
 POINTER_ADDR = D2X(    X2D(C1DEFLTS_ADDR) + X2D(22E)      )
 SITE_SYMBOLICS_TABLE_NAME = STORAGE(POINTER_ADDR,08) ;
 SAY "SITE_SYMBOLICS_TABLE_NAME =" SITE_SYMBOLICS_TABLE_NAME ;
/*                                                                   */
 POINTER_ADDR = D2X(    X2D(C1DEFLTS_ADDR) + X2D(400)      )
 NDVR_MAP    = " " ;
 NDVR_STGIDS = " " ;
 NDVR_STAGES = " " ;
/*                                                                   */
 DO CNT = 1 TO NUMBER_OF_ENVIRONMENTS
    ENV_NAME_ADDR = D2X(    X2D(POINTER_ADDR) + X2D(074)      )
    NEXT_ENV_ADDR = D2X(    X2D(POINTER_ADDR) + X2D(07C)      )
    NEXT_STG_ADDR = D2X(    X2D(POINTER_ADDR) + X2D(073)      )
    C1STAGE1_ADDR = POINTER_ADDR
    C1STAGE2_ADDR = D2X(    X2D(POINTER_ADDR) + X2D(08A)      )
    C1STGID1_ADDR = D2X(    X2D(POINTER_ADDR) + X2D(0BE)      )
    C1STGID2_ADDR = D2X(    X2D(POINTER_ADDR) + X2D(0D3)      )
    ENTRY@S1_ADDR = D2X(    X2D(POINTER_ADDR) + X2D(0F0)      )
    ENTRY@S2_ADDR = D2X(    X2D(POINTER_ADDR) + X2D(0F1)      )
    ENV_NAME   = STORAGE(ENV_NAME_ADDR,08) ;
    NEXT_ENV   = STORAGE(NEXT_ENV_ADDR,08) ;
    NEXT_STG   = STORAGE(NEXT_STG_ADDR,01) ;
    C1STAGE1   = STORAGE(POINTER_ADDR,08) ;
    C1STAGE2   = STORAGE(C1STAGE2_ADDR,08) ;
    C1STGID1   = STORAGE(C1STGID1_ADDR,01) ;
    C1STGID2   = STORAGE(C1STGID2_ADDR,01) ;
    ENTRY@1    = STORAGE(ENTRY@S1_ADDR,01) ;
    ENTRY@2    = STORAGE(ENTRY@S2_ADDR,01) ;

    DetailLine = Copies(' ',100)
    DetailLine = Overlay(ENV_NAME,DetailLine,02);
    DetailLine = Overlay(C1STGID1,DetailLine,11);
    DetailLine = Overlay(C1STAGE1,DetailLine,18);
    DetailLine = Overlay(C1STGID2,DetailLine,28);
    DetailLine = Overlay(C1STAGE2,DetailLine,35);
    If ENTRY@1 = 'Y' then Entrystg# = '1'
    Else                  Entrystg# = '2'
    DetailLine = Overlay(Entrystg#,DetailLine,44);
    If Substr(ENV_NAME,1,3) = 'ADM' then,
       DetailLine = Overlay('Y',DetailLine,54);
    Queue DetailLine ;

    NDVR_MAP    =  NDVR_MAP ENV_NAME"/1" ENV_NAME"/2"
    SAY "NDVR_MAP= " NDVR_MAP ;
    NDVR_STGIDS = NDVR_STGIDS C1STGID1 C1STGID2 ;
    SAY "NDVR_STGIDS =" NDVR_STGIDS
    NDVR_STAGES = NDVR_STAGES C1STAGE  C1STAGE2 ;
    SAY "NDVR_STAGES =" NDVR_STAGES
    SAY "ENTRY_STAGE =" ENV_NAME ENTRY@1 ENTRY@2

    POINTER_ADDR = D2X(    X2D(POINTER_ADDR) + X2D(100)      )
 END  /* DO CNT = 1 TO NUMBER_OF_ENVIRONMENTS */

 "EXECIO" QUEUED() "DISKW ENVIRONS (Finis"
