./  ADD  NAME=ENDLTYPE
/* REXX                                                               */
/**********************************************************************/
/* Name    : ENDLTYP                                                  */
/* Desc    : Read All Lines of the dataset in edit and process.       */
/* Version : 14/05/16                                                 */
/**********************************************************************/

/**********************************************************************/
/* Read the uploaded CSV file of members extracted from Librarian.    */
/*                                                                    */
/* Extract all of the Unique Types for each Application and write     */
/* them to the APPSTYP file.                                          */
/*                                                                    */
/* Extract all of the Unique Types for the Converting Application and */
/* write them to the APPSTYPE file.                                   */
/*                                                                    */
/**********************************************************************/

   ADDRESS ISPEXEC
   'ISREDIT MACRO (Argin)'

   Parse Source . . ExecName . .

   Say ' '
   Say ' Executing Edit Macro      :' ExecName

   DebugSw = 1
   DebugSw = 0

   If SYSVAR(SYSENV) \= 'BACK' Then
      Signal EOJ

/* Build list of Converting Applications from APPS input file         */
   Call GCA_GetConvertingApps

   'ISREDIT (CurrLine) = LINENUM .ZF'
   'ISREDIT (LastLine) = LINENUM .ZL'

   If DebugSw Then
   Do
      Say '   CurrLine =' CurrLine
      Say '   LastLine =' LastLine
   End

/* Extract List of Types from CSV File                                */
   Call GML_GetMemberList

/* Copy Unique Sets from MbrLines. to Uniq.                           */
   Call GUS_GetUniqueSets

/* Build Output of Types for all Apps                                 */
   Call BAA_BuildAllApps

/* Build Output of Types for Converting App                           */
   Call PCA_PullConvertApps

   ADDRESS TSO "EXECIO * DISKW APPSTYP  ( Stem AllApp. Finis"
   ADDRESS TSO "EXECIO * DISKW APPSTYPE ( Stem CvtApp. Finis"

   Say ' '

EOJ:
   If SYSVAR(SYSENV) = 'BACK' Then
      'ISREDIT END'

   Exit 0

/**********************************************************************/
/*                     S U B P R O C E D U R E S                      */
/**********************************************************************/
GCA_GetConvertingApps: Procedure Expose DebugSw ListApps apps.

   ADDRESS TSO "EXECIO * DISKR APPS (STEM apps. Finis"

   ListApps = ''
   Do app# = 2 to apps.0
      ListApps = ListApps Word( apps.app#, 1)
   End app#

   Say ' These Apps are Converting :' "'"ListApps"'"

   Return

/**********************************************************************/
GML_GetMemberList: Procedure Expose DebugSw MbrLines. CurrLine,
   LastLine apps.

/* Extract Appl Type DB2-parm from each member                        */
/* Add Endevor Types to each App which do not exist in Librarian      */

   MbrLines. = ''
   h = 0

   MaxLines = '99999'

/* Read each line of CSV File */
   Do While CurrLine <= LastLine
      If CurrLine > LastLine Then
         Leave

      'ISREDIT (LineText) = LINE' CurrLine

      If DebugSw Then
         Say '   Line Read ('CurrLine') =' "'"LineText"'"

   /* Bypass Comments */
      If Substr( LineText, 1, 1) = '*' Then
      Do
         CurrLine = CurrLine + 1
         If CurrLine > LastLine Then
            Leave

         If CurrLine > MaxLines Then
            Leave

         Iterate
      End

   /* Bypass Title Line */
      If Substr( LineText, 2, 8) = 'LIBRMEMR' Then
      Do
         CurrLine = CurrLine + 1
         If CurrLine > LastLine Then
            Leave

         If CurrLine > MaxLines Then
            Leave

         Iterate
      End

   /* Bypass Garbage */
      If Substr( LineText, 1, 1) \= ' ' Then
      Do
         CurrLine = CurrLine + 1
         If CurrLine > LastLine Then
            Leave

         If CurrLine > MaxLines Then
            Leave

         Iterate
      End

   /* Parse the Comma-Delimited Values */
      Parse Value LineText,
         With LibrMemr ',' ApplName ',' TypeIn ',' ModDesc,
         ',' AddDate ',' UpDate  ',' RecsIn ',' LangIn,
         ',' ProcIn  ',' PrgmrIn ',' LibrIn ',' BatOnl ',' ImsIn,
         ',' DB2In   ',' PgmTab  ',' RestStr

   /* Bypass Unwanted Types */
      If TypeIn = 'DELETE' Then
      Do
         CurrLine = CurrLine + 1
         If CurrLine > LastLine Then
            Leave

         If CurrLine > MaxLines Then
            Leave

         Iterate
      End

   /* Strip of Leading and Trailing Blanks */
      LibrMemr = Strip( LibrMemr, B)
      ApplName = Strip( ApplName, B)
      TypeIn   = Strip( TypeIn  , B)
      ModDesc  = Strip( ModDesc , B)
      AddDate  = Strip( AddDate , B)
      UpDate   = Strip( UpDate  , B)
      RecsIn   = Strip( RecsIn  , B)
      LangIn   = Strip( LangIn  , B)
      ProcIn   = Strip( ProcIn  , B)
      PrgmrIn  = Strip( PrgmrIn , B)
      LibrIn   = Strip( LibrIn  , B)
      BatOnl   = Strip( BatOnl  , B)
      ImsIn    = Strip( ImsIn   , B)
      DB2In    = Strip( DB2In   , B)
      PgmTab   = Strip( PgmTab  , B)
      PgmTab   = Strip( PgmTab  , B)
      RestStr  = Strip( RestStr , B)

      If DebugSw Then
      Do
         Say 'LibrMemr =' "'"LibrMemr"'"
         Say 'ApplName =' "'"ApplName"'"
         Say 'TypeIn   =' "'"TypeIn"'"
         Say 'ModDesc  =' "'"ModDesc"'"
         Say 'AddDate  =' "'"AddDate"'"
         Say 'UpDate   =' "'"UpDate"'"
         Say 'RecsIn   =' "'"RecsIn"'"
         Say 'LangIn   =' "'"LangIn"'"
         Say 'ProcIn   =' "'"ProcIn"'"
         Say 'PrgmrIn  =' "'"PrgmrIn"'"
         Say 'LibrIn   =' "'"LibrIn"'"
         Say 'BatOnl   =' "'"BatOnl"'"
         Say 'ImsIn    =' "'"ImsIn"'"
         Say 'DB2In    =' "'"DB2In"'"
         Say 'PgmTab   =' "'"PgmTab"'"
         Say 'RestStr  =' "'"RestStr"'"
      End

      h = h + 1
      MbrLines.h = ApplName TypeIn DB2In

      CurrLine = CurrLine + 1
      If CurrLine > LastLine Then
         Leave

      If CurrLine > MaxLines Then
         Leave
   End
/* Read each line - End */

/* Add Endevor Types to each App which do not exist in Librarian      */
   Do app# = 2 to apps.0
      h = h + 1
      MbrLines.h = Word( apps.app#, 1) 'OPT'
      h = h + 1
      MbrLines.h = Word( apps.app#, 1) 'SPPARM'
      h = h + 1
      MbrLines.h = Word( apps.app#, 1) 'LCT'
   End app#

   MbrLines.0 = h

   If DebugSw Then
   Do h = 1 to MbrLines.0
      Say '   Mbr  Line.'h '=' "'"MbrLines.h"'"
   End h

   Say ' Lines Read from File      :' MbrLines.0

   Return

/**********************************************************************/
GUS_GetUniqueSets: Procedure Expose DebugSw MbrLines. Uniq.

/* Read each set of Appl Type DB2-parm from MbrLines.                 */
/* Write Unique Sets to Uniq.                                         */

   Uniq. = ''; u = 0; Uniq.0 = u

   Do h = 1 to MbrLines.0
      If DebugSw Then
         Say '   Mbr  Line.'h '=' MbrLines.h

      NeedIt = 1
      Do t = 1 to Uniq.0
         If Uniq.t = MbrLines.h Then
         Do
            NeedIt = 0
            Leave t
         End
      End t

   /* New pair - save it */
      If NeedIt Then
      Do
         u = u + 1
         Uniq.u = MbrLines.h
         Uniq.0 = u
      End
   End h

   Uniq.0 = u

   Say 'Unique Sets Found          :' Uniq.0
   Do u = 1 to Uniq.0
      Say '  'u'. =' "'"Uniq.u"'"
   End u

   Return

/**********************************************************************/
BAA_BuildAllApps: Procedure Expose DebugSw Uniq. AllApp.

/* Extract Unique APP-Type Strings                                    */
/* For each Appl-Type pair not in AllApp., add it                     */

   AllApp. = ''; a = 0; AllApp.0 = a

   PgmTypes = 'COB TCOB ASM PLI SQLPL'

   Do u = 1 to Uniq.0
      If DebugSw Then
         Say '   Uniq Line.'u '=' Uniq.u

      UniqAppl  = Word( Uniq.u, 1)
      UniqType  = Word( Uniq.u, 2)
      UniqDB2In = Word( Uniq.u, 3)

   /* If a Program Type and DB2, add the "D" Type */
      NeedIt = 1
      If WordPos( UniqType, PgmTypes) > 0,
       & UniqDB2In = 'DB2' Then   /* Check Type "D" */
      Do
         Do t = 1 to AllApp.0
            If Word( AllApp.t, 1) = UniqAppl,
             & Word( AllApp.t, 2) = UniqType    "D" Then
            Do
               NeedIt = 0
               Leave t
            End
         End t

      /* New pair - save it */
         If NeedIt Then
         Do
            a = a + 1
            AllApp.a = Left( UniqAppl, 8) UniqType    "D"
            AllApp.0 = a
         End
      End

   /* Check other Types */
      NeedIt = 1
      Do t = 1 to AllApp.0
         If Word( AllApp.t, 1) = UniqAppl,
          & Word( AllApp.t, 2) = UniqType Then
         Do
            NeedIt = 0
            Leave t
         End
      End t

   /* New pair - save it */
      If NeedIt Then
      Do
         a = a + 1
         AllApp.a = Left( UniqAppl, 8) UniqType
         AllApp.0 = a
      End
   End u

   Say ' All Unique Appl-Type Pairs:' AllApp.0
   Do a = 1 to AllApp.0
      Say '  'a'. =' "'"AllApp.a"'"
   End a

   Return

/**********************************************************************/
PCA_PullConvertApps: Procedure Expose DebugSw AllApp. CvtApp. ListApps

/* Copy Converting Apps from AllApp. to CvtApp.                       */

   CvtApp. = ''; c = 0; CvtApp.0 = c

   Do a = 1 to AllApp.0
      If WordPos( Word( AllApp.a, 1), ListApps) > 0 Then
      Do
         c = c + 1
         CvtApp.c = AllApp.a
         CvtApp.0 = c
      End
   End a

   Say 'Converting Appl-Type Pairs:' CvtApp.0
   Do c = 1 to CvtApp.0
      Say '  'c'. =' "'"CvtApp.c"'"
   End c

   Return

/**********************************************************************/
./  ADD  NAME=ENDLTYP8
/*    REXX     */
/*    Find all the unique values given to type  */
/*    Save the list of values in ....           */
   'ISREDIT MACRO '
   ADDRESS ISREDIT;
   TRACE O;
/* Build list of converting applications from APPS input file      */
   ADDRESS TSO "EXECIO * DISKR APPS (STEM apps. Finis"
   ListApps = ''
   Do app# = 2 to apps.0
      ListApps = ListApps Word(apps.app#,1) ;
   End
   convertapp.0  = 0

/* The TYPE column appears in cols 18 - 25                           */
/* Find the unique values ..................                         */
   "SORT 11 25 A"
   START_COL = 11
   STOP_COL  = 25
   IF START_COL < 1 THEN START_COL = 1 ;
   IF STOP_COL  < 1 THEN STOP_COL = 80 ;
   IF STOP_COL  < START_COL THEN STOP_COL = START_COL ;
   LEN = STOP_COL - START_COL + 1;
   RC = 0;
   LASTLINE = '' ;
    "FIND P'=' 1 FIRST "
   DO UNTIL RC > 0
     "(LP CP)=CURSOR"
     "(DATALINE)=LINE" LP
     IF SUBSTR(LASTLINE,START_COL,LEN) =,
        SUBSTR(DATALINE,START_COL,LEN) THEN,
        "EXCLUDE P'=' "
    LASTLINE = DATALINE ;
    "FIND P'=' 1 NX NEXT"
   END;

/* Eliminate the Heading  ..................                         */
    "EXCLUDE 'TYPE----' ALL"
    "EXCLUDE './' 1     ALL"
    "EXCLUDE '*'  1     ALL"
    "DELETE ALL X"
    "CHANGE ',' ' ' ALL"
    "CHANGE P'=' ' ' 1 10 ALL"
    "CHANGE P'=' ' ' 26 100 ALL"

    IF SYSVAR(SYSENV) /= BACK THEN EXIT

    /* Save in APPSTYPE  dd name                */
    "CURSOR = 1 1 " ;
    Do Forever
       "Find p'=' 11 NEXT "
       If RC > 0 then Leave;
       ADDRESS ISREDIT  "BNDS  1  *"
       ADDRESS ISREDIT  "SHIFT ( .ZCSR 10 "
       ADDRESS ISREDIT  "BNDS  6  *"
       ADDRESS ISREDIT  "SHIFT ) .ZCSR  2 "
       ADDRESS ISREDIT  "BNDS  1  *"
       ADDRESS ISREDIT  "(LP CP)=CURSOR"
       ADDRESS ISREDIT  "(DATALINE)=LINE" LP

       TypeUsed = Word(Substr(DATALINE,10),1)
       If TypeUsed /= 'DELETED' &,
          TypeUsed /= 'UNKNOWN' then,
          Do
          Queue DATALINE ;
          /* If Appl is listed in the list of converting Applications */
          /* Save it to write to APPLTYPE                             */
          Appl = Word(DATALINE,1);
          If WordPos(Appl,ListApps) > 0 then,
             Do
             cvt# =  convertapp.0  + 1;
             convertapp.cvt# =  DATALINE;
             convertapp.0 = cvt# ;
             End;  /* If WordPos(Appl,ListApps) > 0 */
          End /* If TypeUsed /= 'DELETED' ... */
    End  /* Do Forever */

    ADDRESS TSO "EXECIO" QUEUED() "DISKW APPSTYP  ( Finis"
    ADDRESS TSO "EXECIO * DISKW APPSTYPE ( Stem convertapp. Finis"

/* Cancel out from the member being edited.                          */
   IF SYSVAR(SYSENV) = BACK THEN ,
      DO
      ADDRESS ISREDIT " CANCEL "
      END
   EXIT 0

./  ADD  NAME=LIB#LIST
/*     REXX   */
/*                                                                    */
   "ISREDIT MACRO" ;
   /* WRITTEN BY DAN WALTHER */
   TRACE  o  ;
   /* Get the last node of the original dataset name */
   "EXECIO 1 DISKR LASTNODE ( FINIS"
   Pull Lastnode ;
   Lastnode = Strip(Lastnode) ;
   Say 'Lastnode=' Lastnode

     ADDRESS ISREDIT;
     " CURSOR = 1 1 " ;
     "EXCLUDE ALL"
     "FIND 'DATE=' FIRST   " ;
     if RC > 0 then Signal SaveAndExit;
     "CHANGE P'==' '**' 1 NX FIRST"
     "CHANGE P'=MODULE   ' ' LIBRMEMR ' FIRST "
     "CHANGE 'PSWD  '",
            "'-APPL-' FIRST"
     "CHANGE 'MODULE DESCRIPTION            '",
            "'MODULE_DESCRIPTION------------' FIRST"
     "CHANGE ' ADDED  '",
            "'-ADDED--' FIRST"
     "CHANGE '    UPDATED    '",
            "'----UPDATED----' FIRST "
     "CHANGE P'========='",
             "'Librarian' 125 .ZCSR .ZCSR"
     "CHANGE P'======='",
             "'BAT_ONL' 136 .ZCSR .ZCSR"
     "CHANGE P'======'",
             "'IMS---' 146 .ZCSR .ZCSR"
     "CHANGE P'====='",
             "'DB2--' 155 .ZCSR .ZCSR"
     "CHANGE P'==============================='",
             "'PGMTAB2------------------------' 166 .ZCSR .ZCSR"

     "FIND '/' 51 ALL       " ;
     "EXCLUDE 'DATE=' FIRST"
     "DELETE ALL X          " ;
     "EXCLUDE ALL"
     "FIND '/' 51 ALL       " ;
     "CHANGE P'====' '    ' 11 ALL NX"
     "CHANGE P'========='",
             "'"Lastnode"' 125 ALL NX"
     "RESET"

     " CURSOR = 1 1 " ;
     "BNDS  17 250 "
     DO FOREVER
        " FIND  P'=' 40 NEXT"
        IF RC >0 THEN LEAVE;
        "BNDS  17 250 "
        "SHIFT ) .ZCSR 9  "
        "BNDS  1  250 "
        ADDRESS ISREDIT " (LPOS1,CPOS1) = CURSOR " ;
        ADDRESS ISREDIT " (DLINE) = LINE "LPOS1
        " CURSOR = "LPOS1 1
        MEMBER = Substr(DLINE,2,8);
        IF Substr(DLINE,1,1) /= '*' then,
           Do
           If Substr(Lastnode,1,1) = 'H' then,
              C1SystemPrefix = 'FC'
           Else,
              C1SystemPrefix = 'FE'
           APPL = C1SystemPrefix    Substr(MEMBER,1,2)
           "CHANGE P'====' '"APPL"' 11 .ZCSR .ZCSR "
           End /*  IF Substr(DLINE,1,1) /= '*' */
        " CURSOR = "LPOS1 80
     END;
     "BNDS  1  250 "

     "CHANGE '-APPL-         '",
            "'-APPL- TYPE----' FIRST "

     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 10 10 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 17 17 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 26 26 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 57 57 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 66 66 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 83 83 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 92 92 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 103 103 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 114 114 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 132 132 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 144 144 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 154 154 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 163 163 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 173 173 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 206 206 all "

     "CHANGE '11'X ' ' 1 ALL     "
     "CHANGE  ',' ' ' 27 56 all  "

      ADDRESS ISREDIT " (MEMBER) = MEMBER " ;
      ADDRESS ISREDIT " (DATASET) = DATASET " ;
      tmp = Translate(DATASET," ",".");
      TYPE = SUBSTR(MEMBER,2,3) ;
      if Word(tmp,Words(tmp)) = 'COPYLIB' then TYPE = 'CPY'
      if Substr(MEMBER,4)     = '#COPY' then TYPE = 'CPY'
      "CHANGE '   ' '"TYPE"' 18 ALL NX"
      "CHANGE '   ' '"APPL"' 11 ALL NX"
      "EXCLUDE ALL"
      "FIND 'TO BE DELETED' 27 all "
      "CHANGE P'========' 'DELETED ' 18 ALL NX"

SaveAndExit:
     /* SAVE & EXIT */
     IF SYSVAR(SYSENV) = BACK THEN ,
        DO
        ADDRESS ISREDIT " SAVE"
        ADDRESS ISREDIT " CANCEL"
        END

   EXIT 0
./  ADD  NAME=LIB#SRCE
/*     REXX   */
/*                                                                    */
   "ISREDIT MACRO" ;
   /* WRITTEN BY DAN WALTHER */
   TRACE  o  ;
   /* Get the last node of the original dataset name */
   "EXECIO 1 DISKR LASTNODE ( FINIS"
   Pull Lastnode ;
   Lastnode = Strip(Lastnode) ;
   Say 'Lastnode=' Lastnode

     ADDRESS ISREDIT;
     " CURSOR = 1 1 " ;
     "EXCLUDE ALL"
     "FIND 'DATE=' FIRST   " ;
     if RC > 0 then Signal SaveAndExit;
     "CHANGE P'==' '**' 1 NX FIRST"
     "CHANGE P'=MODULE   ' ' LIBRMEMR ' FIRST "
     "CHANGE 'PSWD  '",
            "'-APPL-' FIRST"
     "CHANGE 'MODULE DESCRIPTION            '",
            "'MODULE_DESCRIPTION------------' FIRST"
     "CHANGE ' ADDED  '",
            "'-ADDED--' FIRST"
     "CHANGE '    UPDATED    '",
            "'----UPDATED----' FIRST "
     "CHANGE P'========='",
             "'Librarian' 125 .ZCSR .ZCSR"
     "CHANGE P'======='",
             "'BAT_ONL' 136 .ZCSR .ZCSR"
     "CHANGE P'======'",
             "'IMS---' 146 .ZCSR .ZCSR"
     "CHANGE P'====='",
             "'DB2--' 155 .ZCSR .ZCSR"
     "CHANGE P'==============================='",
             "'PGMTAB2------------------------' 166 .ZCSR .ZCSR"

     "FIND '/' 51 ALL       " ;
     "EXCLUDE '**' 1 FIRST  ";
     "EXCLUDE 'DATE=' FIRST"
     "DELETE ALL X          " ;

     "EXCLUDE ALL"
     "FIND '/' 51 ALL       " ;
     "CHANGE P'====' '    ' 11 ALL NX"
     "CHANGE P'========='",
             "'"Lastnode"' 125 ALL NX"
     "RESET"

     ADDRESS ISREDIT " (LIBRLIST) = MEMBER " ;
     DefaultTYPE = SUBSTR(LIBRLIST,2,3) ;
     ADDRESS ISREDIT " (DATASET) = DATASET " ;
     " CURSOR = 1 1 " ;
     DO FOREVER
        " FIND  P'=' 40 NEXT"
        IF RC >0 THEN LEAVE;
        "BNDS  17 250 "
        "SHIFT ) .ZCSR 9  "
        "BNDS  1  150 "
        ADDRESS ISREDIT " (LPOS1,CPOS1) = CURSOR " ;
        ADDRESS ISREDIT " (DLINE) = LINE "LPOS1
        " CURSOR = "LPOS1 1
        MEMBER = Substr(DLINE,2,8);
        IF Substr(DLINE,1,1) /= '*' then,
           Do
           If Substr(Lastnode,1,1) = 'H' then,
              C1SystemPrefix = 'FC'
           Else,
              C1SystemPrefix = 'FE'
           APPL = C1SystemPrefix    Substr(MEMBER,1,2)
           "CHANGE P'====' '"APPL"' 11 .ZCSR .ZCSR "
           "FIND 'TO BE DELETED' .ZCSR .ZCSR "
           If RC = 0 then,
              TYPE = 'DELETED'
           Else,
              CALL AnalyzeForType ;
           If TYPE = ' ' then,
              TYPE= DefaultTYPE
           "CHANGE P'===' '"TYPE"' 18 .ZCSR .ZCSR "
           "CHANGE P'=======' '"BAT#ONL"' 145 .ZCSR .ZCSR "
           "CHANGE P'=======' '"IMS"' 155 .ZCSR .ZCSR "
           "CHANGE P'=======' '"DB2"' 164 .ZCSR .ZCSR "
           "CHANGE P'=======' '"PGMTAB2"' 174 .ZCSR .ZCSR "
           End /*  IF Substr(DLINE,1,1) /= '*' */
        " CURSOR = "LPOS1 80
     END;

     "CHANGE '-APPL-         '",
            "'-APPL- TYPE----' FIRST "

     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 10 10 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 17 17 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 26 26 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 57 57 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 66 66 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 83 83 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 92 92 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 103 103 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 114 114 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 132 132 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 144 144 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 154 154 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 163 163 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 173 173 all "
     "CHANGE ' ' ',' 206 206 all "

     "CHANGE '11'X ' ' 1 ALL     "
     "CHANGE  ',' ' ' 27 56 all  "

SaveAndExit:
     /* SAVE & EXIT */
     IF SYSVAR(SYSENV) = BACK THEN ,
        DO
        ADDRESS ISREDIT " SAVE"
        ADDRESS ISREDIT " CANCEL"
        END

   EXIT 0

AnalyzeForType :

   ADDRESS TSO
   "ALLOC F(SYSIN) LRECL(80) BLKSIZE(800) SPACE(5,5)",
          "RECFM(F B) TRACKS ",
          "NEW UNCATALOG REUSE "     ;
   Push './  REPRO NEW=PS,NAME='MEMBER
   "EXECIO 1 DISKW SYSIN (Finis "

   /* SYSUT2, the output, is allocated DISP=OLD in the JCL */
   ADDRESS LINK 'IEBUPDTE'
   my_rc = RC;
   If my_rc > 0 then,
      Do
      TYPE = DefaultTYPE
      say "Trouble" MEMBER ;
      Return
      End

   Push  MEMBER
   ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMINIT DATAID(DDID) DDNAME(SYSUT2)"
   ADDRESS ISPEXEC "VIEW DATAID(&DDID) MACRO(ANL#VIEW)"
   ADDRESS ISPEXEC "LMFREE DATAID(&DDID)"

   /* Get the Type value from the edit macro */
   PULL TYPE BAT#ONL IMS DB2 PGMTAB2
   SA= MEMBER TYPE BAT#ONL IMS DB2 PGMTAB2

   Return


./  ADD  NAME=FTDF
//*  Telon Design Facility (TDF) Generate processor
//*
//**=================================================================** 00240000
//FTDF PROC PROCNAME=FTDF,                                              00250000
//          TDFLVL=SDPROD.TELON.R51
//**   SEE W#E0.COMPILE.SKELS(TELALLOC)
//**********************************************************************
//*   copied and tailored from   W#E02X.ENDEVOR.COMPILE.JCL(E4BMPPCO)
//**********************************************************************
//*      IEBUPDTE USING SCREEN DEFINITION MEMBER AS INPUT              *
//**********************************************************************
//*
//*
//*   THIS JCL SUBMITS A COMPILE; AND/OR LINK ONLY; AND/OR BDT
//**********************************************************************
//* CATALOG ALL NEW DATASETS                                           *
//**********************************************************************
//*
//CATALOG  EXEC PGM=BC1PDSIN
//*
//CAT1     DD  DSN=&&XPDS,DISP=(,PASS),
//             UNIT=DISK,SPACE=(TRK,(50,10,10),RLSE),
//             DSORG=PO,DSNTYPE=PDS,
//             DCB=(RECFM=FB,LRECL=80,BLKSIZE=6160)
//*
//CAT2     DD  DSN=&&MODLIB,DISP=(,PASS),
//             UNIT=DISK,SPACE=(TRK,(40,15,10)),
//             DSORG=PO,DSNTYPE=PDS,
//             DCB=(RECFM=FB,LRECL=80,BLKSIZE=6160)
//*
//CAT3     DD  DSN=&&SCRNDEF,DISP=(,PASS),
//             UNIT=DISK,SPACE=(TRK,(40,10)),
//             DCB=(RECFM=FB,LRECL=80,BLKSIZE=3600)
//*
//CAT4     DD  DSN=&&TEMP,DISP=(,PASS),
//             UNIT=DISK,SPACE=(TRK,(40,10)),
//             DCB=(RECFM=FB,LRECL=80,BLKSIZE=6160)
//*
//CAT5     DD  DSN=&&GENPR,UNIT=DISK,SPACE=(TRK,(30,30)),
//             DISP=(,PASS),DCB=(LRECL=121,BLKSIZE=1210)
//*
//CAT6     DD  DSN=&&UPDLIB,DISP=(,PASS),
//             UNIT=DISK,SPACE=(TRK,(50,10,20)),
//             DSORG=PO,DSNTYPE=PDS,
//             DCB=(RECFM=FB,LRECL=80,BLKSIZE=6160)
//*
//CAT7     DD  DSN=&&XMAC,DISP=(,PASS),
//             UNIT=DISK,SPACE=(TRK,(10,10)),
//             DCB=(RECFM=FB,LRECL=80,BLKSIZE=6160)
//*
//CAT8     DD  DSN=&&PROGRAM,DISP=(,PASS),
//             UNIT=DISK,SPACE=(TRK,(40,10)),
//             DCB=(RECFM=FB,LRECL=80,BLKSIZE=6160)
//*
//**********************************************************************
//*          EXPORT THE DEFINITION FROM Endevor                        *
//**********************************************************************
//*
//EXPORTIT EXEC PGM=CONWRITE,PARM='EXPINCL(N)'
//ELMOUT   DD DSN=&&XMAC,DISP=(OLD,PASS)
//*
//*      IEBUPDTE USING SCREEN DEFINITION MEMBER AS INPUT              *
//**********************************************************************
//*
//IEBUP1   EXEC PGM=IEBUPDTE,PARM=NEW
//SYSIN    DD  DSN=&&XMAC,DISP=(OLD,DELETE),
//             DCB=BUFNO=40
//SYSPRINT DD  SYSOUT=*
//SYSUT1   DD  DUMMY
//SYSUT2   DD  DSN=&&MODLIB,DISP=(OLD,PASS)
//*
//**********************************************************************
//*     COPY SCREEN DEFINITION OPTIONALLY ADDING OR REPLACING CONTROL  *
//*     STATEMENTS IN THE SCREEN DEFINITION.                           *
//*          1. SYSIN INPUT IS PROVIDED                                *
//*             SYSIN REPLACES THE CONTROL STATEMENTS IN THE SCREEN    *
//*             DEFINITION                                             *
//*          2. SYSIN INPUT DUMMIED                                    *
//*             SCREEN DEFINITION USED AS IS                           *
//**********************************************************************
//*
//CONTROL  EXEC PGM=ADPCCARD,PARM=''
//STEPLIB  DD  DSN=&TDFLVL..CAWLLOAD,DISP=SHR
//         DD  DSN=&TDFLVL..CAWLLOAD,DISP=SHR
//SYSIN    DD  DUMMY
//SYSOUT   DD  SYSOUT=*
//SYSPRINT DD  SYSOUT=*
//SYSUT1   DD  DSN=&&MODLIB(SCRNDEF),DISP=(OLD,PASS),DCB=BUFNO=40
//SYSUT2   DD  DSN=&&SCRNDEF,DISP=(OLD,PASS)
//TEMPOPT  DD  DSN=&&TEMP,DISP=(OLD,PASS)
//*
//**********************************************************************
//*          ASSEMBLE THE TELON SOURCE CODE                            *
//**********************************************************************
//*
//GEN      EXEC PGM=ASMA90,PARM='NOOBJECT,DECK,SYSPARM(IGYCRCTL)',
//         REGION=2048K
//SYSIN    DD   DSN=&&SCRNDEF,DISP=(OLD,PASS)
//SYSLIB   DD  DSN=W#E0.TECHSUPP.TELON.R51.MACLIB,DISP=SHR
//         DD  DSN=&TDFLVL..CAWLMAC,DISP=SHR
//SYSLIN   DD  DUMMY
//SYSPRINT DD  SYSOUT=*
//SYSPUNCH DD  DSN=&&TEMP,DISP=(OLD,PASS)
//SYSUT1   DD  UNIT=DISK,SPACE=(1700,(600,100)),DSN=&&SYSUT1
//SYSUT2   DD  UNIT=DISK,SPACE=(1700,(600,100)),DSN=&&SYSUT2
//SYSUT3   DD  UNIT=DISK,SPACE=(1700,(600,100)),DSN=&&SYSUT3
//*
//**********************************************************************
//*          PRINT IF GEN FAILED                                       *
//**********************************************************************
//*
//GENPRINT EXEC PGM=IEBGENER,REGION=100K,
//         COND=((5,GT,GEN))
//SYSIN    DD  DUMMY
//SYSPRINT DD  SYSOUT=B
//SYSUT1   DD  DSN=&&GENPR,DISP=(OLD,DELETE)
//SYSUT2   DD  SYSOUT=*
//*                                                     START B2SELC1
//**********************************************************************
//*  RUN SELCOPY TO CHANGE AA1C200I TO AA2C200I FOR AA DB2
//*  PREVIOUSLY  TO CHANGE AA@C200I TO AA#C200I FOR AA DB2
//**********************************************************************
//*
//SELCOPY  EXEC PGM=SELCOPY
//SYSIN    DD  DSN=W#E0.COMPILE.CTLCARDS(DB2CONV),DISP=SHR
//SELIN    DD  DSN=&&TEMP,DISP=(OLD,PASS),DCB=BUFNO=40
//SELOUT   DD  DSN=&&TEMP2,DISP=(,PASS),
//             UNIT=DISK,SPACE=(TRK,(40,10)),
//             DCB=(RECFM=FB,LRECL=80,BLKSIZE=6160)
//SYSPRINT DD  SYSOUT=*
//SYSUDUMP DD  DUMMY
//SYSOUT   DD  SYSOUT=B
//*
//**********************************************************************
//*  COPY THE UPDATED SOURCE BACK TO THE ORIGINAL DATASET              *
//**********************************************************************
//*
//CPYBACK  EXEC PGM=IEBGENER
//SYSIN    DD  DUMMY
//SYSPRINT DD  SYSOUT=*
//SYSUT1   DD  DSN=&&TEMP2,DISP=(OLD,DELETE),DCB=BUFNO=40
//SYSUT2   DD  DSN=&&TEMP,DISP=(OLD,PASS)
//*                                                     END B2SELC1
//******************************************************************060*
//*      IEBUPDTE TO PUT GENERATED PRODUCTS IN A LIBRARY               *
//**********************************************************************
//*
//IEBUPSRC EXEC PGM=IEBUPDTE,PARM=NEW
//SYSIN    DD  DSN=&&TEMP,DISP=(OLD,DELETE),DCB=BUFNO=40
//SYSPRINT DD  SYSOUT=*
//SYSUT1   DD  DUMMY
//SYSUT2   DD  DSN=&&UPDLIB,DISP=(OLD,PASS)
//*
//**********************************************************************
//*          RESOLVE COPY STATEMENTS IN THE GENERATED PROGRAM          *
//*          ALL COPY other Copy STATEMENT MEMBER NAMES WILL BE        *
//*          RESOLVED FROM THE SYSLIB DD STATEMENT LIBRARIES           *
//*          during the Generate action on the COBOL.                  *
//**********************************************************************
//*
//RESOLVE  EXEC PGM=ADPACOPY,
//         PARM=('C- AYY5',',,,,')
//STEPLIB  DD  DSN=W#E0.TECHSUPP.TELON.R51.LOADESA,DISP=SHR
//         DD  DSN=SDPROD.TELON.R51.CAWLLOAD,DISP=SHR
//PRINT    DD  SYSOUT=*
//SYSIN    DD  DSN=&&UPDLIB(PROGRAM),DISP=(OLD,DELETE)
//SYSLIB   DD  DSN=&&MODLIB,DISP=(OLD,DELETE)
//SYSOUT   DD  DSN=&&PROGRAM,DISP=(OLD,PASS)
//SYSPRINT DD  SYSOUT=*
//*
//SHOWME   EXEC PGM=IEBGENER,REGION=100K
//SYSIN    DD  DUMMY
//SYSPRINT DD  SYSOUT=*
//SYSUT1   DD  DSN=&&PROGRAM,DISP=(OLD,PASS)
//SYSUT2   DD  SYSOUT=*
//*                                                     START B2SELC1
//***************************************************************
//*    Copy program SOURCE to Endevor as type TCOB              *
//***************************************************************
//CRE#TCOB EXEC PGM=C1BM3000,COND=(4,LT),MAXRC=4,
//             PARM='SCLIN,TCOBOUT1,,TCOBOUT2'
//PROGRAM  DD  DSN=&&PROGRAM,DISP=(OLD,DELETE)
//SCLIN    DD  *
ADD  ELEMENT &C1ELEMENT
  TO ENVIRONMENT '&C1ENVMNT'
       SYSTEM &C1SYSTEM  SUBSYSTEM &C1SUBSYS TYPE TCOB
FROM FILE 'PROGRAM' MEMBER 'PROGRAM'
  OPTIONS UPDATE  OVERRIDE SIGNOUT
     CCID  '&C1CCID'
  COMMENT  '&C1COMMENT'
  PROCESSOR GROUP = 'COMPILE'
  .
//TCOBOUT1 DD  SYSOUT=*
//TCOBOUT2 DD  SYSOUT=*
//SYSPRINT DD  SYSOUT=*
//SYSOUT   DD  SYSOUT=*
